sa vai srucaḥ saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 1.1]
tadyatsrucaḥ saṃmārṣṭi yathā vai devānāṃ caraṇaṃ tadvā anu manuṣyāṇāṃ tasmād yadā manuṣyāṇām pariveṣaṇam upakﾱptam bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 1.2]
atha pātrāṇi nirṇenijati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 2.1]
tair nirṇijya pariveviṣaty evaṃ vā eṣa devānāṃ yajño bhavati yacchṛtāni havīṃṣi kﾱptā vedis teṣāmetānyeva pātrāṇi yatsrucaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 2.2]
sa yat saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 3.1]
nirṇenektyevainā etannirṇiktābhiḥ pracarāṇīti tadvai dvayenaiva devebhyo nirṇenijaty ekena manuṣyebhyo 'dbhiśca brahmaṇā ca devebhya āpo hi kuśā brahma yajur ekenaiva manuṣyebhyo 'dbhir evaivam v etan nānā bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 3.2]
atha sruvamādatte | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 4.1]
tam pratapati pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātayo niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātaya iti vā | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 4.2]
devā ha vai yajñaṃ tanvānāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 5.1]
te 'surarakṣasebhya āsaṃgād bibhayāṃcakrus tad yajñamukhād evaitan nāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsyato 'pahanti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 5.2]
sa vā ityagrairantarataḥ saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 6.1]
aniśito 'si sapatnakṣiditi yathānuparato yajamānasya sapatnānkṣiṇuyādevam etad āha vājinaṃ tvā vājedhyāyai saṃmārjmīti yajñiyaṃ tvā yajñāya saṃmārjmīty evaitad āhaitenaiva sarvāḥ srucaḥ saṃmārṣṭi vājinīṃ tveti srucaṃ tūṣṇīm prāśitraharaṇaṃ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 6.2]
sa vā ityagrairantarataḥ saṃmārṣṭīti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 7.1]
mūlairbāhyata itīva vā ayam prāṇa itīvodānaḥ prāṇodānāvevaitad dadhāti tasmāditīvemāni lomānītīvemāni | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 7.2]
sa vai saṃmṛjya saṃmṛjya pratapya pratapya prayacchati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 8.1]
yathāvamarśaṃ nirṇijyānavamarśam uttamam parikṣālayed evaṃ tat tasmāt pratapya pratapya prayacchati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 8.2]
sa vai sruvamevāgre saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 9.1]
athetarāḥ sruco yoṣā vai srug vṛṣā sruvas tasmādyadyapi bahvya iva striyaḥ sārdhaṃ yanti ya eva tāsvapi kumāraka iva pumānbhavati sa eva tatra prathama ety anūcya itarās tasmātsruvamevāgre saṃmārṣṭy athetarāḥ srucaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 9.2]
sa vai tathaiva saṃmṛjyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 10.1]
yathāgniṃ nābhivyukṣed yathā yasmā aśanam āhariṣyant syāt tam pātranirṇejanenābhivyukṣed evaṃ tat tasmād u tathaiva saṃmṛjyād yathāgniṃ nābhivyukṣet prāṅ ivaivotkramya | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 10.2]
taddhaike | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 11.1]
sruksammārjanānyagnāvabhyādadhati vedasyāhābhūvant sruca ebhiḥ samamārjiṣur idaṃ vai kiṃcidyajñasya ned idam bahirdhā yajñād bhavad iti tad u tathā na kuryād yathā yasmā aśanamāharettam pātranirṇejanam pāyayedevaṃ tat tasmād u parāsyedevaitāni | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 11.2]
atha patnīṃ saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 12.1]
jaghanārdho vā eṣa yajñasya yatpatnī prāṅme yajñastāyamāno yāditi yunaktyevainām etad yuktā me yajñam anvāsātā iti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 12.2]
yoktreṇa saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 13.1]
yoktreṇa hi yogyaṃ yuñjanty asti vai patnyā amedhyaṃ yadavācīnaṃ nābher athaitadājyam avekṣiṣyamāṇā bhavati tadevāsyā etadyoktreṇāntardadhātyatha medhyenaivottarārdhenājyam avekṣate tasmātpatnīṃ saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 13.2]
sa vā abhivāsaḥ saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 14.1]
oṣadhayo vai vāso varuṇyā rajjus tad oṣadhīr evaitad antardadhāti tatho hainām eṣā varuṇyā rajjurna hinasti tasmādabhivāsaḥ saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 14.2]
sa saṃnahyati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 15.1]
adityai rāsnāsītīyaṃ vai pṛthivyaditiḥ seyaṃ devānām patny eṣā vā etasya patnī bhavati tad asyā etadrāsnāmeva karoti na rajjuṃ hiro vai rāsnā tāmevāsyā etatkaroti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 15.2]
sa vai na granthim kuryāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 16.1]
varuṇyo vai granthir varuṇo ha patnīṃ gṛhṇīyād yad granthiṃ kuryāt tasmānna granthiṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 16.2]
ūrdhvam evodgūhati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 17.1]
viṣṇor veṣyo 'sīti sā vai na paścātprācī devānāṃ yajñamanvāsīteyaṃ vai pṛthivyaditiḥ seyaṃ devānām patnī sā paścāt prācī devānāṃ yajñam anvāste taddhemām abhyārohet sā patnī kṣipre 'muṃ lokam iyāt tatho ha patnī jyogjīvati tadasyā evaitannihnute tatho haināmiyaṃ na hinasti tasmād u dakṣiṇata ivaivānvāsīta | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 17.2]
athājyamavekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 18.1]
yoṣā vai patnī reta ājyam mithunam evaitat prajananaṃ kriyate tasmād ājyam avekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 18.2]
sāvekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 19.1]
adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvapaśyāmīty anārtena tvā cakṣuṣāvapaśyāmīty evaitad āhāgner jihvāsīti yadā vā etadagnau juhvatyathāgnerjihvā ivottiṣṭhanti tasmād āhāgner jihvāsīti suhūr devebhya iti sādhu devebhya ity evaitad āha dhāmne dhāmne me bhava yajuṣe yajuṣa iti sarvasmai me yajñāyaidhītyevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 19.2]
athājyamādāya prāṅ udāharati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 20.1]
tadāhavanīye 'dhiśrayati yasyāhavanīye havīṃṣi śrapayanti sarvo me yajña āhavanīye śṛto 'sad ity atha yadamutrāgre 'dhiśrayati patnīṃ hyavakāśayiṣyan bhavati na hi tadavakalpate yat sāmi pratyaggharet patnīm avakāśayiṣyāmīty atha yat patnīṃ nāvakāśayed antariyāddha yajñāt patnīṃ tatho ha yajñāt patnīṃ nāntareti tasmād u sārdham eva vilāpya prāg udāharaty avakāśya patnīṃ yasyo patnī na bhavaty agra eva tasyāhavanīye 'dhiśrayati tat tata ādatte tad antarvedyāsādayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 20.2]
tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 21.1]
nāntarvedy āsādayed ato vai devānām patnīḥ saṃyājayanty avasabhā aha devānām patnīḥ karoti paraḥpuṃso hāsya patnī bhavatīti tad u hovāca yājñavalkyo yathādiṣṭam patnyā astu kas tad ādriyeta yat paraḥpuṃsā vā patnī syād yathā vā yajño vedir yajña ājyaṃ yajñād yajñaṃ nirmimā iti tasmād antarvedy evāsādayet | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 21.2]
prokṣaṇīṣu pavitre bhavataḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 22.1]
te tata ādatte tābhyāmājyamutpunātyeko vā utpavanasya bandhur medhyamevaitat karoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 22.2]
sa utpunāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 23.1]
savitustvā prasava utpunāmy achidreṇa pavitreṇa sūryasya raśmibhiriti so 'sāveva bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 23.2]
athājyaliptābhyām pavitrābhyām | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 24.1]
prokṣaṇīrutpunāti saviturvaḥ prasava utpunāmyachidreṇa pavitreṇa sūryasya raśmibhiriti so 'sāveva bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 24.2]
tadyadājyaliptābhyām pavitrābhyām | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 25.1]
prokṣaṇīr utpunāti tad apsu payo dadhāti tad idam apsu payo hitam idaṃ hi yadā varṣaty athauṣadhayo jāyanta oṣadhīr jagdhvāpaḥ pītvā tata eṣa rasaḥ sambhavati tasmād u rasasyo caiva sarvatvāya | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 25.2]
athājyamavekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 26.1]
taddhaike yajamānamavakhyāpayanti tad u hovāca yājñavalkyaḥ kathaṃ nu na svayamadhvaryavo bhavanti kathaṃ svayaṃ nānvāhuryatra bhūyasya ivāśiṣaḥ kriyante kathaṃ nveṣāmatraiva śraddhā bhavatīti yāṃ vai kāṃ ca yajña ṛtvija āśiṣam āśāsate yajamānasyaiva sā tasmād adhvaryur evāvekṣeta | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 26.2]
so 'vekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 27.1]
satyaṃ vai cakṣuḥ satyaṃ hi vai cakṣus tasmād yad idānīṃ dvau vivadamānāveyātām aham adarśam aham aśrauṣam iti ya eva brūyād aham adarśam iti tasmā eva śraddadhyāma tat satyenaivaitat samardhayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 27.2]
so 'vekṣate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 28.1]
tejo 'si śukram asy amṛtam asīti sa eṣa satya eva mantras tejo hyetacchukraṃ hyetadamṛtaṃ hyetat tat satyenaivaitat samardhayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 1 28.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 3, 2}
puruṣo vai yajñaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 1.1]
puruṣas tena yajño yad enam puruṣas tanuta eṣa vai tāyamāno yāvāneva puruṣas tāvān vidhīyate tasmāt puruṣo yajñaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 1.2]
tasyeyameva juhūḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 2.1]
iyam upabhṛd ātmaiva dhruvā tadvā ātmana evemāni sarvāṇyaṅgāni prabhavanti tasmād u dhruvāyā eva sarvo yajñaḥ prabhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 2.2]
prāṇa eva sruvaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 3.1]
so 'yam prāṇaḥ sarvāṇyaṅgāny anusaṃcarati tasmād u sruvaḥ sarvā anu srucaḥ saṃcarati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 3.2]
tasyāsāveva dyaurjuhūḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 4.1]
athedam antarikṣam upabhṛd iyam eva dhruvā tad vā asyā eveme sarve lokāḥ prabhavanti tasmād u dhruvāyā eva sarvo yajñaḥ prabhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 4.2]
ayameva sruvo yo 'yam pavate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 5.1]
so 'yam imāṃt sarvāṃllokān anupavate tasmād u sruvaḥ sarvā anu srucaḥ saṃcarati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 5.2]
sa eṣa yajñastāyamānaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 6.1]
devebhyas tāyata ṛtubhyaś chandobhyo yaddhavis tad devānāṃ yat somo rājā yatpuroḍāśas tat tad ādiśya gṛhṇāty amuṣmai tvā juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīty evam u haiteṣām | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 6.2]
atha yānyājyāni gṛhyante | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 7.1]
ṛtubhyaścaiva tāni chandobhyaśca gṛhyante tat tad anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāti sa vai caturjuhvām gṛhṇātyaṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 7.2]
sa yaccaturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 8.1]
ṛtubhyastadgṛhṇāti prayājebhyo hi tad gṛhṇāty ṛtavo hi prayājās tat tad anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāty ajāmitāyai jāmi ha kuryādyadvasantāya tvā grīṣmāya tveti gṛhṇīyāt tasmād anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 8.2]
atha yadaṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 9.1]
chandobhyas tad gṛhṇāty anuyājebhyo hi tadgṛhṇāti chandāṃsi hyanuyājās tat tad anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāty ajāmitāyai jāmi ha kuryād yad gāyatryai tvā triṣṭubhe tveti gṛhṇīyāt tasmād anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 9.2]
atha yaccaturdhruvāyāṃ gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 10.1]
sarvasmai tadyajñāya gṛhṇāti tat tad anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāti kasmā u hyādiśed yataḥ sarvābhya eva devatābhyo 'vadyati tasmād anādiśyājyasyaiva rūpeṇa gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 10.2]
yajamāna eva juhūmanu | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 11.1]
yo 'smā arātīyati sa upabhṛtam anv attaiva juhūm anv ādya upabhṛtam anv attaiva juhūr ādya upabhṛt sa vai catur juhvāṃ gṛhṇāty aṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 11.2]
sa yaccaturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 12.1]
attāram evaitat parimitataraṃ kanīyāṃsaṃ karoty atha yad aṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti gṛhṇāty ādyam evaitad aparimitataram bhūyāṃsaṃ karoti taddhi samṛddhaṃ yatrāttā kanīyānādyo bhūyān | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 12.2]
sa vai caturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇan | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 13.1]
bhūya ājyaṃ gṛhṇātyaṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti gṛhṇankanīya ājyaṃ gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 13.2]
sa yaccaturjuhvāṃ gṛhṇan | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 14.1]
bhūya ājyaṃ gṛhṇāty attāram evaitat parimitataraṃ kanīyāṃsaṃ kurvaṃs tasmin vīryam balaṃ dadhāty atha yad aṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti gṛhṇankanīya ājyaṃ gṛhṇāty ādyam evaitad aparimitataram bhūyāṃsaṃ kurvaṃs tam avīryam abalīyāṃsaṃ karoti tasmāduta rājāpārāṃ viśam prāvasāyāpy ekaveśmanaiva jināti tvad yathā tvat kāmayate tathā sacata eteno ha tad vīryeṇa yaj juhvāṃ bhūya ājyaṃ gṛhṇāti sa yaj juhvāṃ gṛhṇāti juhvaiva taj juhoti yad upabhṛti gṛhṇāti juhvaiva taj juhoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 14.2]
tad āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 15.1]
kasmā u tarhyupabhṛti gṛhṇīyād yad upabhṛtā na juhotīti sa yaddhopabhṛtā juhuyāt pṛthagghaivemāḥ prajāḥ syur naivāttā syān nādyaḥ syād atha yat tajjuhveva samānīya juhoti tasmād imā viśaḥ kṣatriyasyaiva vaśe sati vaiśyam paśava upatiṣṭhante 'tha yattajjuhveva samānīya juhoti tasmād yadota kṣatriyaḥ kāmayate 'thāha vaiśya mayi yat te paro nihitaṃ tad āhareti taṃ jināti tvad yathā tvat kāmayate tathā sacata eteno ha tad vīryeṇa | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 15.2]
tāni vā etāni | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 16.1]
chandobhya ājyāni gṛhyante sa yac catur juhvāṃ gṛhṇāti gāyatryai tad gṛhṇāty atha yad aṣṭau kṛtva upabhṛti gṛhṇāti triṣṭubjagatībhyāṃ tad gṛhṇāty atha yaccatur dhruvāyāṃ gṛhṇāty anuṣṭubhe tad gṛhṇāti vāgvā anuṣṭub vāco vā idaṃ sarvam prabhavati tasmād u dhruvāyā eva sarvo yajñaḥ prabhavatīyam vā anuṣṭub asyai vā idaṃ sarvaṃ prabhavati tasmād u dhruvāyā eva sarvo yajñaḥ prabhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 16.2]
sa gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 17.1]
dhāma nāmāsi priyaṃ devānām ity etad vai devānām priyatamaṃ dhāma yadājyaṃ tasmādāha dhāma nāmāsi priyaṃ devānām ity anādhṛṣṭaṃ devayajanamasīti vajro hyājyaṃ tasmādāhānādhṛṣṭaṃ devayajanamasīti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 17.2]
sa etena yajuṣā | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 18.1]
sakṛjjuhvāṃ gṛhṇāti tris tūṣṇīm etenaiva yajuṣā sakṛdupabhṛti gṛhṇāti saptakṛtvas tūṣṇīm etenaiva yajuṣā sakṛddhruvāyāṃ gṛhṇāti tristūṣṇīṃ tad āhus tristrireva yajuṣā gṛhṇīyāt trivṛddhi yajña iti tad u nu sakṛt sakṛd evātro hyeva trir gṛhītaṃ sampadyate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 2 18.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 3, 3}
prokṣaṇīradhvaryurādatte | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 1.1]
sa idhmamevāgre prokṣati kṛṣṇo 'syākhareṣṭho 'gnaye tvā juṣṭam prokṣāmīti tan medhyam evaitad agnaye karoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 1.2]
atha vedim prokṣati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 2.1]
vedirasi barhiṣe tvā juṣṭām prokṣāmi tan medhyāmevaitadbarhiṣe karoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 2.2]
athāsmai barhiḥ prayacchati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 3.1]
tat purastād granthyāsādayati tatprokṣati barhirasi srugbhyastvā juṣṭam prokṣāmi tan medhyam evaitat srugbhyaḥ karoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 3.2]
atha yāḥ prokṣaṇyaḥ pariśiṣyante | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 4.1]
tābhiroṣadhīnām mūlāny upaninayaty adityai vyundanamasītīyaṃ vai pṛthivy aditis tad asyā evaitadoṣadhīnām mūlāny uponatti tā imā ārdramūlā oṣadhayas tasmād yadyapi śuṣkāṇyagrāṇi bhavantyārdrāṇyeva mūlāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 4.2]
atha visraṃsya granthim | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 5.1]
purastāt prastaraṃ gṛhṇāti viṣṇo stupo 'sīti yajño vai viṣṇus tasyeyam eva śikhā stupa etām evāsminnetad dadhāti purastād gṛhṇāti purastāddhyayaṃ stupas tasmāt purastādgṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 5.2]
atha saṃnahanaṃ visraṃsayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 6.1]
prakﾱptaṃ haivāsya strī vijāyata iti tasmāt saṃnahanaṃ visraṃsayati taddakṣiṇāyāṃ śroṇau nidadhāti nīvirhaivāsyaiṣā dakṣiṇata iva hīyaṃ nīvis tasmād dakṣiṇāyāṃ śroṇau nidadhāti tat punar abhicchādayaty abhicchanneva hīyaṃ nīvis tasmāt punar abhicchādayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 6.2]
atha barhi stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 7.1]
ayaṃ vai stupaḥ prastaro 'tha yānyavāñci lomāni tānyevāsya yaditaram barhis tānyevāsminn etad dadhāti tasmād barhi stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 7.2]
yoṣā vai vediḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 8.1]
tāmetaddevāśca paryāsate ye ceme brāhmaṇāḥ śuśruvāṃso 'nūcānās teṣvevainām etat paryāsīneṣv anagnāṃ karoty anagnatāyā eva tasmād barhi stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 8.2]
yāvatī vai vediḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 9.1]
tāvatī pṛthivy oṣadhayo barhis tad asyām evaitat pṛthivyām oṣadhīrdadhāti tā imā asyām pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ pratiṣṭhitās tasmād barhi stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 9.2]
tad vai bahulaṃ stṛṇīyād ity āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 10.1]
yatra vā asyai bahulatamā oṣadhayas tad asyā upajīvanīyatamaṃ tasmād bahulaṃ stṛṇīyād iti tad vai tadāhartaryevādhi trivṛt stṛṇāti trivṛddhi yajño 'tho api pravarhaṃ stṛṇīyāt stṛṇanti barhir ānuṣagiti tvṛṣiṇābhyanūktam adharamūlaṃ stṛṇāty adharamūlā iva hīmā asyām pṛthivyām oṣadhayaḥ pratiṣṭhitās tasmād adharamūlaṃ stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 10.2]
sa stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 11.1]
ūrṇamradasaṃ tvā stṛṇāmi svāsasthāṃ devebhya iti sādhvīṃ devebhya ityevaitadāha yadāhorṇamradasaṃ tveti svāsasthāṃ devebhya iti svāsadāṃ devebhya ityevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 11.2]
athāgniṃ kalpayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 12.1]
śiro vai yajñasyāhavanīyaḥ pūrvo 'rdho vai śiraḥ pūrvārdhamevaitadyajñasya kalpayaty uparyupari prastaraṃ dhārayan kalpayaty ayaṃ vai stupaḥ prastara etam evāsminn etat pratidadhāti tasmād uparyupari prastaraṃ dhārayan kalpayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 12.2]
atha paridhīn paridadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 13.1]
tad yat paridhīn paridadhāti yatra vai devā agre 'gniṃ hotrāya prāvṛṇata taddhovāca na vā ahamidamutsahe yad vo hotā syāṃ yadvo havyaṃ vaheyaṃ trīn pūrvān prāvṛḍhvaṃ te prādhanviṣus tān nu me 'vakalpayatātha vā aham etad utsākṣye yadvo hotā syāṃ yadvo havyaṃ vaheyamiti tatheti tān asmā etān avākalpayaṃs ta ete paridhayaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 13.2]
sa hovāca | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 14.1]
vajro vai tānvaṣaṭkāraḥ prāvṛṇag vajrād vai vaṣaṭkārādbibhemi yanmā vajro vaṣaṭkāro na pravṛñjyād etaireva mā paridhatta tathā mā vajro vaṣaṭkāro na pravarkṣyatīti tatheti tametaiḥ paryadadhus taṃ na vajro vaṣaṭkāraḥ prāvṛṇak tad varmaivaitad agnaye nahyati yadetaiḥ paridadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 14.2]
ta u haita ūcuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 15.1]
idam u cedasmānyajñe yuṅkthāstv evāsmākam api yajñe bhāga iti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 15.2]
tatheti devā abruvan | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 16.1]
yad bahiṣparidhi skantsyati tad yuṣmāsu hutam atha yadva uparyupari hoṣyanti tad vo 'viṣyatīti sa yadagnau juhvati tad enān avaty atha yad enān uparyupari juhvati tad enān avaty atha yad bahiṣparidhi skandati tad eteṣu hutaṃ tasmād u ha nāga iva skannaṃ syād imāṃ vai te prāviśan yad vā idaṃ kiṃca skandaty asyām eva tat sarvaṃ pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 16.2]
sa skannamabhimṛśati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 17.1]
bhuvapataye svāhā bhuvanapataye svāhā bhūtānām pataye svāhety etāni vai teṣāmagnīnāṃ nāmāni yad bhuvapatir bhuvanapatir bhūtānām patis tad yathā vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ hutam evam asyaiteṣvagniṣu bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 17.2]
taddhaike | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 18.1]
idhmasyaivaitān paridhīn paridadhati tad u tathā na kuryād anavakﾱptā ha tasyaite bhavanti yān idhmasya paridadhāty abhyādhānāya hyevedhmaḥ kriyate tasyo haivaite 'vakﾱptā bhavanti yasyaitān anyān āharanti paridhaya iti tasmād anyān evāhareyuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 18.2]
te vai pālāśāḥ syuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 19.1]
brahma vai palāśo brahmāgnir agnayo hi tasmāt pālāśāḥ syuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 19.2]
yadi pālāśānna vindet | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 20.1]
atho api vaikaṅkatā syur yadi vaikaṅkatān na vinded atho api kārṣmaryamayāḥ syur yadi kārṣmaryamayān na vinded atho api bailvāḥ syur atho khādirā atho audumbarā ete hi vṛkṣā yajñiyās tasmād eteṣāṃ vṛkṣāṇām bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 3 20.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 3, 4}
te vā ārdrāḥ syuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 1.1]
etaddhyeṣāṃ jīvam etena satejasa etena vīryavantas tasmād ārdrāḥ syuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 1.2]
sa madhyamamevāgre | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 2.1]
paridhiṃ paridadhāti gandharvastvā viśvāvasuḥ paridadhātu viśvasyāriṣṭyai yajamānasya paridhir asyagniriḍa īḍita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 2.2]
atha dakṣiṇam paridadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 3.1]
indrasya bāhurasi dakṣiṇo viśvasya ariṣṭyai yajamānasya paridhir asy agniriḍa īḍita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 3.2]
athottaram paridadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 4.1]
mitrāvaruṇau tvottarataḥ paridhattāṃ dhruveṇa dharmaṇā viśvasyāriṣṭyai yajamānasya paridhir asy agniriḍa īḍita ity agnayo hi tasmād āhāgniriḍa īḍita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 4.2]
atha samidhamabhyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 5.1]
sa madhyamamevāgre paridhim upaspṛśati tenaitānagre samindhe 'thāgnāv abhyādadhāti teno agnim pratyakṣaṃ samindhe | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 5.2]
so 'bhyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 6.1]
vītihotraṃ tvā kave dyumantaṃ samidhīmahi agne bṛhantam adhvara ity etayā gāyatryā gāyatrīm evaitat saminddhe sā gāyatrī samiddhānyāni chandāṃsi samindhe chandāṃsi samiddhāni devebhyo yajñaṃ vahanti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 6.2]
atha yāṃ dvitīyāṃ samidham abhyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 7.1]
vasantameva tayā samindhe sa vasantaḥ samiddho 'nyān ṛtūṃt samindha ṛtavaḥ samiddhāḥ prajāśca prajanayanty oṣadhīśca pacanti so 'bhyādadhāti samidasīti samiddhi vasantaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 7.2]
athābhyādhāya japati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 8.1]
sūryastvā purastāt pātu kasyāścid abhiśastyā iti guptyai vā abhitaḥ paridhayo bhavanty athaitat sūryameva purastādgoptāraṃ karoti net purastānnāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsy abhyavacarāniti sūryo hi nāṣṭrāṇāṃ rakṣasām apahantā | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 8.2]
atha yāmevāmūṃ tṛtīyāṃ samidhamabhyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 9.1]
anuyājeṣu brāhmaṇameva tayā samindhe sa brāhmaṇaḥ samiddho devebhyo yajñaṃ vahati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 9.2]
atha stīrṇāṃ vedim upāvartate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 10.1]
sa dve tṛṇe ādāya tiraścī nidadhāti savitur bāhū stha ity ayaṃ vai stupaḥ prastaro 'thāsyaite bhruvāveva tiraścī nidadhāti tasmād ime tiraścyau bhruvau kṣatraṃ vai prastaro viśa itaram barhiḥ kṣatrasya caiva viśaśca vidhṛtyai tasmāt tiraścī nidadhāti tasmād v eva vidhṛtī nāma | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 10.2]
tat prastaraṃ stṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 11.1]
ūrṇamradasaṃ tvā stṛṇāmi svāsasthaṃ devebhya iti sādhuṃ devebhya ityevaitadāha yadāhorṇamradasaṃ tveti svāsasthaṃ devebhya iti svāsadaṃ devebhya ityevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 11.2]
tamabhinidadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 12.1]
ā tvā vasavo rudrā ādityāḥ sadantvity ete vai trayā devā yadvasavo rudrā ādityā ete tvāsīdantv ity evaitad āhābhinihita eva savyena pāṇinā bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 12.2]
atha dakṣiṇena juhūm pratigṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 13.1]
nediha purā nāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsy āviśān iti brāhmaṇo hi rakṣasāmapahantā tasmād abhinihita eva savyena pāṇinā bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 13.2]
atha juhūm pratigṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 14.1]
ghṛtācyasi juhūrnāmneti ghṛtācī hi juhūrhi nāmnā sedam priyeṇa dhāmnā priyaṃ sada āsīdeti ghṛtācy asy upabhṛn nāmnety upabhṛtaṃ ghṛtācī hyupabhṛddhi nāmnā sedam priyeṇa dhāmnā priyaṃ sada āsīdeti ghṛtācyasi dhruvā nāmneti dhruvāṃ ghṛtācī hi dhruvā hi nāmnā sedam priyeṇa dhāmnā priyaṃ sada āsīdeti priyeṇa dhāmnā priyaṃ sada āsīdeti yad anyaddhaviḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 14.2]
sa vā upari juhūṃ sādayati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 15.1]
adha itarāḥ srucaḥ kṣatraṃ vai juhūr viśa itarāḥ srucaḥ kṣatram evaitad viśa uttaraṃ karoti tasmāduparyāsīnaṃ kṣatriyamadhastādimāḥ prajā upāsate tasmād upari juhūṃ sādayatyadha itarāḥ srucaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 15.2]
so 'bhimṛśati | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 16.1]
dhruvā asadanniti dhruvā hyasadann ṛtasya yonāviti yajño vā ṛtasya yonir yajñe hyasadaṃs tā viṣṇo pāhi pāhi yajñam pāhi yajñapatimiti tadyajamānamāha pāhi māṃ yajñanyamiti tadapyātmānaṃ yajñānnāntareti yajño vai viṣṇus tad yajñāyaivaitat sarvam paridadāti guptyai tasmādāha tā viṣṇo pāhīti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 4 16.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 3, 5}
inddhe ha vā etad adhvaryuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 1.1]
idhmenāgniṃ tasmād idhmo nāma samindhe sāmidhenībhirhotā tasmātsāmidhenyo nāma | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 1.2]
sa āha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 2.1]
agnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhītyagnaye hyetatsamidhyamānāyānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 2.2]
tad u haika āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 3.1]
agnaye samidhyamānāya hotaranubrūhīti tad u tathā na brūyād ahotā vā eṣa purā bhavati yadaivainam pravṛṇīte 'tha hotā tasmād u brūyād agnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhītyeva | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 3.2]
āgneyīranvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 4.1]
svayaivainam etad devatayā samindhe gāyatrīr anvāha gāyatraṃ vā agneśchandaḥ svenaivainam etacchandasāsamindhe vīryaṃ gāyatrī brahma gāyatrī vīryeṇaivainametatsamindhe | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 4.2]
ekādaśānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 5.1]
ekādaśākṣarā vai triṣṭub brahma gāyatrī kṣatraṃ triṣṭub etābhyām evainam etad ubhābhyāṃ vīryābhyāṃ samindhe tasmād ekādaśānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 5.2]
sa vai triḥ prathamāmanvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 6.1]
triruttamāṃ trivṛtprāyaṇā hi yajñās trivṛdudayanās tasmāttriḥ prathamām anvāha triruttamāṃ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 6.2]
tāḥ pañcadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ sampadyante pañcadaśo vai vajro vīryaṃ vajro vīryamevaitatsāmidhenīr abhisaṃpādayati tasmād etāsvanūcyamānāsu yaṃ dviṣyāt tam aṅguṣṭhābhyām avabādhetedam aham amum avabādha iti tadenametena vajreṇāvabādhate | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 7.1]
pañcadaśa vā ardhamāsasya rātrayaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 8.1]
ardhamāsaśo vai saṃvatsaro bhavanneti tadrātrīrāpnoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 8.2]
pañcadaśānām u vai gāyatrīṇām | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 9.1]
trīṇi ca śatāni ṣaṣṭiścākṣarāṇi trīṇi ca vai śatāni ṣaṣṭiśca saṃvatsarasyāhāni tadahānyāpnoti tad v eva saṃvatsaramāpnoti | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 9.2]
saptadaśa sāmidhenīḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 10.1]
iṣṭyā anubrūyād upāṃśu tasyai devatāyai yajati yasyā iṣṭaṃ nirvapati dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya pañcartava eṣa eva prajāpatiḥ saptadaśaḥ sarvaṃ vai prajāpatis tat sarveṇaiva taṃ kāmam anaparādhaṃ rādhnoti yasmai kāmāyeṣṭiṃ nirvapaty upāṃśu devatām yajaty aniruktaṃ vā upāṃśu sarvaṃ vā aniruktaṃ tat sarveṇaiva taṃ kāmam anaparādhaṃ rādhnoti yasmai kāmāyeṣṭiṃ nirvapaty eṣa iṣṭer upacāraḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 10.2]
ekaviṃśatiṃ sāmidhenīḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 11.1]
api darśapūrṇamāsayor anubrūyād ity āhur dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya pañcartavas trayo lokās tad viṃśatir eṣa evaikaviṃśo ya eṣa tapati saiṣā gatireṣā pratiṣṭhā tadetāṃ gatim etām pratiṣṭhāṃ gacchati tasmādekaviṃśatimanubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 11.2]
tā haitā gataśrer evānubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 12.1]
ya icchen na śreyāṃt syāṃ na pāpīyāniti yādṛśāya haiva sate 'nvāhus tādṛṅ vā haiva bhavati pāpīyān vā yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etā anvāhuḥ so eṣā mīmāṃsaiva na tvevaitā anūcyante | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 12.2]
trireva prathamāṃ trir uttamām anavānann anubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 13.1]
trayo vā ime lokās tad imān evaitallokāṃt saṃtanotīmāṃl lokāṃt spṛṇute traya ime puruṣe prāṇā etam evāsminnetat saṃtatam avyavacchinnaṃ dadhāty etadanuvacanam | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 13.2]
sa yāvadasya vacaḥ syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 14.1]
evam evānuvivakṣet tasyaitasya paricakṣīta sāmyavānyād anavānann anuvivakṣaṃs tat karma vivṛhyeta sā paricakṣā | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 14.2]
sa yady etan nodāśaṃseta | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 15.1]
apy ekaikām evānavānann anubrūyāt tad ekaikayaivemāṃl lokāṃt saṃtanotyekaikayemāṃl lokāṃt spṛṇute 'tha yatprāṇaṃ dadhāti gāyatrī vai prāṇaḥ sa yatkṛtsnāṃ gāyatrīmanvāha tatkṛtsnaṃ prāṇaṃ dadhāti tasmād ekaikām evānavānann anubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 15.2]
tā vai saṃtatā avyavacchinnā anvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 16.1]
saṃvatsarasyaivaitad ahorātrāṇi saṃtanoti tānīmāni saṃvatsarasyāhorātrāṇi saṃtatāny avyavacchinnāni pariplavante dviṣata u caivaitadbhrātṛvyāya nopasthānaṃ karoty upasthānaṃ ha kuryād yad asaṃtatā anubrūyāt tasmādvai saṃtatā avyavacchinnā anvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 3, 5 16.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 4, 1}
hiṃkṛtyānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 1.1]
nāsāmā yajño 'stīti vā āhur na vā ahiṃkṛtya sāma gīyate sāma yaddhiṃkaroti taddhiṃkārasya rūpaṃ kriyate praṇavenaiva sāmno rūpam upagacchaty o3ṃ o3m ity eteno hāsyaiṣa sarva eva sasāmā yajño bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 1.2]
yad v eva hiṃkaroti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 2.1]
prāṇo vai hiṃkāraḥ prāṇo hi vai hiṃkāras tasmādapigṛhya nāsike na hiṃkartuṃ śaknoti vācā vā ṛcamanvāha vākca vai prāṇaśca mithunaṃ tadetatpurastānmithunam prajananaṃ kriyate sāmidhenīnāṃ tasmādvai hiṃkṛtyānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 2.2]
sa vā upāṃśu hiṃkaroti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 3.1]
atha yad uccair hiṃkuryād anyatarad eva kuryād vācameva tasmād upāṃśu hiṃkaroti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 3.2]
sa vā eti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 4.1]
gāyatrīmevaitadarvācīṃ ca parācīṃ ca yunakti parācyaha devebhyo yajñaṃ vahaty arvācī manuṣyānavati tasmādvā eti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 4.2]
yad v eveti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 5.1]
preti vai prāṇa ety udānaḥ prāṇodānāvevaitaddadhāti tasmād vā eti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 5.2]
yad v eveti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 6.1]
preti vai retaḥ sicyata eti prajāyate preti paśavo vitiṣṭhanta eti samāvartante sarvaṃ vā idam eti ca preti ca tasmādvā eti ca preti cānvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 6.2]
so 'nvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 7.1]
pra vo vājā abhidyava iti tannu preti bhavaty agna āyāhi vītaya iti tad v eti bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 7.2]
tad u haika āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 8.1]
ubhayaṃ vā etat preti sampadyata iti tad u tadātivijñānyamiva pra vo vājā abhidyava iti tan nu prety agna āyāhi vītaya iti tad v eti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 8.2]
so 'nvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 9.1]
pra vo vājā abhidyava iti tannu preti bhavati vājā ity annaṃ vai vājā annam evaitad abhyanūktam abhidyava ity ardhamāsā vā abhidyavo 'rdhamāsānevaitadabhyanūktaṃ haviṣmanta iti paśavo vai haviṣmantaḥ paśūnevaitad abhyanūktam | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 9.2]
ghṛtācyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 10.1]
videgho ha māthavo 'gniṃ vaiśvānaram mukhe babhāra tasya gotamo rāhūgaṇa ṛṣiḥ purohita āsa tasmai ha smāmantryamāṇo na pratiśṛṇoti nenme 'gnirvaiśvānaro mukhān niṣpadyātā iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 10.2]
tamṛgbhirhvayituṃ dadhre | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 11.1]
vītihotraṃ tvā kave dyumantaṃ samidhīmahi agne bṛhantamadhvare videgheti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 11.2]
sa na pratiśuśrāva | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 12.1]
ud agne śucayastava śukrā bhrājanta īrate tava jyotīṃṣyarcayo videghā3 iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 12.2]
sa ha naiva pratiśuśrāva | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 13.1]
taṃ tvā ghṛtasnav īmaha ityevābhivyāharad athāsya ghṛtakīrtāvevāgnirvaiśvānaro mukhādujjajvāla tam na śaśāka dhārayituṃ so 'sya mukhānniṣpede sa imām pṛthivīm prāpādaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 13.2]
tarhi videgho māthava āsa | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 14.1]
sarasvatyāṃ sa tata eva prāṅ dahannabhīyāyemām pṛthivīṃ taṃ gotamaśca rāhūgaṇo videghaśca māthavaḥ paścād dahantam anvīyatuḥ sa imāḥ sarvā nadīratidadāha sadānīrety uttarād girer nirdhāvati tāṃ haiva nātidadāha tāṃ ha sma tām purā brāhmaṇā na taranty anatidagdhāgninā vaiśvānareṇeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 14.2]
tata etarhi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 15.1]
prācīnam bahavo brāhmaṇās taddhākṣetrataram ivāsa srāvitaram ivāsvaditam agninā vaiśvānareṇeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 15.2]
tad u haitarhi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 16.1]
kṣetrataramiva brāhmaṇā u hi nūnamenad yajñair asiṣvadaṃt sāpi jaghanye naidāghe samivaiva kopayati tāvacchītānatidagdhā hyagninā vaiśvānareṇa | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 16.2]
sa hovāca | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 17.1]
videgho māthavaḥ kvāham bhavānīty ata eva te prācīnam bhuvanamiti hovāca saiṣāpyetarhi kosalavidehānām maryādā te hi māthavāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 17.2]
atha hovāca | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 18.1]
gotamo rāhūgaṇaḥ kathaṃ nu na āmantryamāṇo na pratyaśrauṣīriti sa hovācāgnirme vaiśvānaro mukhe 'bhūt sa nenme mukhānniṣpadyātai tasmāt te na pratiśrauṣamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 18.2]
tad u kathamabhūditi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 19.1]
yatraiva tvaṃ ghṛtasnav īmaha ity abhivyāhārṣīs tadeva me ghṛtakīrtāvagnirvaiśvānaro mukhād udajvālīt taṃ nāśakaṃ dhārayituṃ sa me mukhānnirapādīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 19.2]
sa yatsāmidhenīṣu ghṛtavat | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 20.1]
sāmidhenameva tat samevainaṃ tenenddhe vīryam evāsmindadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 20.2]
tad u ghṛtācyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 21.1]
devāñjigāti sumnayuriti yajamāno vai sumnayuḥ sa hi devāñjigīṣati sa hi devāñjighāṃsati tasmādāha devāñjigāti sumnayuriti saiṣāgneyī satyaniruktā sarvaṃ vā aniruktaṃ sarveṇaivaitatpratipadyate | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 21.2]
agna āyāhi vītaya iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 22.1]
tad veti bhavati vītaya iti samantikamiva ha vā ime 'gre lokā āsur ity unmṛśyā haiva dyaurāsa | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 22.2]
te devā akāmayanta | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 23.1]
kathaṃ nu na ime lokā vitarāṃ syuḥ kathaṃ na idaṃ varīya iva syāditi tānetaireva tribhir akṣarairvyanayan vītaya iti ta ime vidūraṃ lokās tato devebhyo varīyo 'bhavad varīyo ha vā asya bhavati yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etāmanvāhurvītaya iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 23.2]
gṛṇāno havyadātaya iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 24.1]
yajamāno vai havyadātir gṛṇāno yajamānāyety evaitadāha ni hotā satsi barhiṣīty agnirvai hotāyaṃ loko barhir asminnevaitalloke 'gniṃ dadhāti so 'yamasmiṃlloke 'gnirhitaḥ saiṣemameva lokamabhyanūktemam evaitayā lokaṃ jayati yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etāmanvāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 24.2]
taṃ tvā samidbhiraṅgira iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 25.1]
samidbhirhyetam aṅgirasa aindhatāṅgira ity aṅgirā u hyagnir ghṛtena vardhayāmasīti tatsāmidhenam padaṃ samevainaṃ tenenddhe vīryamevāsmindadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 25.2]
bṛhacchocā yaviṣṭhyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 26.1]
bṛhad u hyeṣa śocati samiddho yaviṣṭhyeti yaviṣṭho hyagnis tasmādāha yaviṣṭhyeti saiṣaitam eva lokamabhyanūktāntarikṣalokameva tasmādāgneyī satyaniruktānirukto hyeṣa loka etamevaitayā lokaṃ jayati yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etāmanvāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 26.2]
sa naḥ pṛthu śravāyyamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 27.1]
ado vai pṛthu yasmindevā etacchravāyyaṃ yasmindevā acchā deva vivāsasīty accha deva vivāsasy etan no gamayety evaitad āha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 27.2]
bṛhad agne suvīryamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 28.1]
ado vai bṛhadyasmindevā etatsuvīryaṃ yasmin devāḥ saiṣaitam eva lokamabhyanūktā divamevaitamevaitayā lokaṃ jayati yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etāmanvāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 28.2]
so nvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 29.1]
īḍenyo namasya itīḍenyo hyeṣa namasyo hyeṣa tiras tamāṃsi darśata iti tira iva hyeṣa tamāṃsi samiddho dadṛśe samagniridhyate vṛṣeti saṃ hīdhyate vṛṣā vṛṣo agniḥ samidhyata iti saṃ hīdhyate | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 29.2]
aśvo na devavāhana iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 30.1]
aśvo ha vā eṣa bhūtvā devebhyo yajñaṃ vahati yadvai netyṛcy omiti tat tasmād āhāśvo na devavāhana iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 30.2]
taṃ haviṣmanta īḍata iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 31.1]
haviṣmanto hyetaṃ manuṣyā īḍate tasmādāha taṃ haviṣmanta īḍata iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 31.2]
vṛṣaṇaṃ tvā vayaṃ vṛṣan vṛṣaṇaḥ samidhīmahīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 32.1]
saṃ hyenamindhate 'gne dīdyataṃ bṛhaditi dīdayeva hyeṣa bṛhatsamiddhaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 32.2]
taṃ vā etam | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 33.1]
vṛṣaṇvantaṃ tricam anvāhāgneyyo vā etāḥ sarvāḥ sāmidhenyo bhavantīndro vai yajñasya devatendro vṛṣaiteno hāsyaitāḥ sendrāḥ sāmidhenyo bhavanti tasmādvṛṣaṇvantaṃ tricam anvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 33.2]
so 'nvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 34.1]
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti devāśca vā asurāścobhaye prājāpatyāḥ paspṛdhire tāṃt spardhamānān gāyatryantarā tasthau yā vai sā gāyatryāsīd iyaṃ vai sā pṛthivīyaṃ haiva tadantarā tasthau ta ubhaya eva vidāṃcakrur yatarān vai na iyam upāvartsyati te bhaviṣyanti paretare bhaviṣyantīti tām ubhaya evopamantrayāṃcakrire 'gnir eva devānāṃ dūta āsa saharakṣā ity asurarakṣasam asurāṇāṃ sāgnim evānupreyāya tasmād anvāhāgniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti sa hi devānāṃ dūta āsīddhotāraṃ viśvavedasam iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 34.2]
tad u haike 'nvāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 35.1]
hotā yo viśvavedasa iti ned aram ity ātmānaṃ bravāṇīti tad u tathā na brūyān mānuṣaṃ ha te yajñe kurvanti vyṛddhaṃ vai tadyajñasya yanmānuṣaṃ nedvyṛddham yajñe karavāṇīti tasmād yathaivarcānūktameva anubrūyāddhotāraṃ viśvavedasam ity evāsya yajñasya sukratum ity eṣa hi yajñasya sukratur yad agnis tasmād āhāsya yajñasya sukratum iti seyaṃ devān upāvavarta tato devā abhavan parāsurā bhavati ha vā ātmanā parāsya sapatnā bhavanti yasyaivaṃ viduṣa etām anvāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 35.2]
tāṃ vā aṣṭamīmanubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 36.1]
gāyatrī vā eṣā nidānenāṣṭākṣarā vai gāyatrī tasmād aṣṭamīmanubrūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 36.2]
taddhaike | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 37.1]
purastāddhāyye dadhaty annaṃ dhāyye mukhata idam annādyaṃ dadhma iti vadantas tad u tathā na kuryād anavakﾱptā tasyaiṣā bhavati yaḥ purastāddhāyye dadhāti daśamī vā hi tarhy ekādaśī vā sampadyate tasyo haivaiṣāvakﾱptā bhavati yasyaitāmaṣṭamīm anvāhus tasmādupariṣṭādeva dhāyye dadhyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 37.2]
samidhyamāno adhvara iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 38.1]
adhvaro vai yajñaḥ samidhyamāno yajña ityevaitadāhāgniḥ pāvaka īḍya iti pāvako hyeṣa īḍyo hyeṣa śociṣkeśastamīmaha iti śocantīva hyetasya keśāḥ samiddhasya samiddho agna āhutety ataḥ prācīnaṃ sarvam idhmam abhyādadhyād yad anyat samidho 'pavṛṅkta iva hy etaddhotā yad vā anyat samidha idhmasyātiricyate tasmād ataḥ prācīnaṃ sarvam idhmam abhyādadhyād yad anyat samidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 38.2]
devān yakṣi svadhvareti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 39.1]
adhvaro vai yajño devānyakṣi suyajñiyetyevaitadāha tvāṃ hi havyavāḍ asīty eṣa hi havyavāḍ yad agnis tasmādāha tvaṃ hi havyavāḍ asīty ā juhotā duvasyatāgnim prayatyadhvare vṛṇīdhvaṃ havyavāhanamiti sampreṣyaty evaitayājuhuta ca yajata ca yasmai kāmāya samaindhiḍhvaṃ tat kurutety evaitad āhāgnim prayatyadhvara ity adhvaro vai yajño 'gniṃ prayati yajña ityevaitad āha vṛṇīdhvaṃ havyavāhanam ity eṣa hi havyavāhano yad agnis tasmād āha vṛṇīdhvaṃ havyavāhanam iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 39.2]
taṃ vā etam | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 40.1]
adhvaravantaṃ tricamanvāha devānha vai yajñena yajamānāṃtsapatnā asurā dudhūrṣāṃcakrus te dudhūrṣanta eva na śekur dhūrvituṃ te parābabhūvus tasmād yajño 'dhvaro nāma dudhūrṣan ha vā enaṃ sapatnaḥ parābhavati yasyaivaṃ viduṣo 'dhvaravantaṃ tricam anvāhur yāvad v eva saumyenādhvareṇeṣṭvā jayati tāvajjayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 1 40.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 4, 2}
etaddha vai devā agniṃ gariṣṭhe 'yuñjan | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 1.1]
yaddhotṛtva idaṃ no havyaṃ vaheti tametadgariṣṭhe yuktvopāmadan vīryavānvai tvamasyalaṃ vai tvametasmā asīti vīrye samādadhato yathedam apyetarhi jñātīnāṃ yaṃ gariṣṭhe yuñjanti tam upamadanti vīryavān vai tvam asy alaṃ vai tvam etasmā asīti vīrye samādadhataḥ sa yadata ūrdhvam anvāhopastautyevainam etad vīryam evāsmin dadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 1.2]
agne mahāṃ asi brāhmaṇa bhārateti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 2.1]
brahma hyagnis tasmādāha brāhmaṇeti bhāratetyeṣa hi devebhyo havyaṃ bharati tasmādbharato 'gnir ityāhur eṣa u vā imāḥ prajāḥ prāṇo bhūtvā bibharti tasmād v evāha bhārateti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 2.2]
athārṣeyam pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 3.1]
ṛṣibhyaścaivainam etad devebhyaśca nivedayaty ayam mahāvīryo yo yajñam prāpaditi tasmād ārṣeyam pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 3.2]
parastād arvāk pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 4.1]
parastāddhyarvācyaḥ prajāḥ prajāyante jyāyasaspataya u caivaitaṃ nihnuta idaṃ hi pitaivāgre 'tha putro 'tha pautras tasmāt parastād arvāk pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 4.2]
sa ārṣeyamuktvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 5.1]
deveddho manviddha iti devā hyetam agra aindhata tasmādāha deveddha iti manviddha iti manur hyetam agra ainddha tasmādāha manviddha iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 5.2]
ṛṣiṣṭuta iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 6.1]
ṛṣayo hyetamagre 'stuvaṃs tasmādāharṣiṣṭuta iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 6.2]
viprānumadita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 7.1]
ete vai viprā yadṛṣaya ete hyetam anvamadaṃs tasmādāha viprānumadita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 7.2]
kaviśasta iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 8.1]
ete vai kavayo yadṛṣaya ete hyetamaśaṃsaṃs tasmādāha kaviśasta iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 8.2]
brahmasaṃśita iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 9.1]
brahmasaṃśito hyeṣa ghṛtāhavana iti ghṛtāhavano hyeṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 9.2]
praṇīryajñānāṃ rathīradhvarāṇāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 10.1]
etena vai sarvānyajñānpraṇayanti ye ca pākayajñā ye cetare tasmād āha praṇīryajñānāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 10.2]
rathīradhvarāṇāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 11.1]
ratho ha vā eṣa bhūtvā devebhyo yajñaṃ vahati tasmādāha rathīradhvarāṇāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 11.2]
atūrto hotā tūrṇir havyavāḍ iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 12.1]
na hyetaṃ rakṣāṃsi taranti tasmād āhātūrto hoteti tūrṇir havyavāḍ iti sarvaṃ hyeṣa pāpmānaṃ tarati tasmādāha tūrṇir havyavāḍ iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 12.2]
āspātraṃ juhūrdevānāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 13.1]
devapātraṃ vā eṣa yadagnis tasmādagnau sarvebhyo devebhyo juhvati devapātraṃ hyeṣa prāpnoti ha vai tasya pātraṃ yasya pātram prepsyati ya evametadveda | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 13.2]
camaso devapāna iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 14.1]
camasena ha vā etena bhūtena devā bhakṣayanti tasmādāha camaso devapāna iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 14.2]
arāṁ ivāgne nemirdevāṃstvaṃ paribhūrasīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 15.1]
yathārānnemiḥ sarvataḥ paribhūrevaṃ tvaṃ devāṃtsarvataḥ paribhūrasīty evaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 15.2]
āvaha devānyajamānāyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 16.1]
tadasmai yajñāya devān āvoḍhavā āhāgnimagna āvaheti tadāgneyāyājyabhāgāyāgnim āvoḍhavā āha somamāvaheti tatsaumyāyājyabhāgāya somam āvoḍhavā āhāgnimāvaheti tadya eṣa ubhayatrācyuta āgneyaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati tasmā agnimāvoḍhavā āha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 16.2]
atha yathādevatam | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 17.1]
devāṁ ājyapāṁ āvaheti tat prayājānuyājān āvoḍhavā āha prayājānuyājā vai devā ājyapā agniṃ hotrāyāvaheti tadagniṃ hotrāyāvoḍhavā āha svaṃ mahimānamāvaheti tatsvam mahimānamāvoḍhavā āha vāg vā asya svo mahimā tad vācam āvoḍhavā āhā ca vaha jātavedaḥ suyajā ca yajeti tadyā evaitaddevatā āvoḍhavā āha tā evaitad āhā cainā vahānuṣṭhyā ca yajeti yad āha suyajā ca yajeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 17.2]
sa vai tiṣṭhannanvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 18.1]
anvāha hyetadasau hyanuvākyā tadasāvevaitadbhūtvānvāha tasmāttiṣṭhannanvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 18.2]
āsīno yājyāṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 19.1]
iyaṃ hi yājyā tasmānna kaścana tiṣṭhanyājyāṃ yajatīyaṃ hi yājyā tadiyamevaitad bhūtvā yajati tasmādāsīno yājyāṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 2 19.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 4, 3}
yo ha vā agniḥ sāmidhenībhiḥ samiddhaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 1.1]
atitarāṃ ha vai sa itarasmād agnes tapaty anavadhṛṣyo hi bhavatyanavamṛśyaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 1.2]
sa yathā haivāgniḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 2.1]
sāmidhenībhiḥ samiddhastapatyevaṃ haiva brāhmaṇaḥ sāmidhenīrvidvānanubruvaṃstapaty anavadhṛṣyo hi bhavatyanavamṛśyaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 2.2]
so 'nvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 3.1]
pra va iti prāṇo vai pravān prāṇamevaitayā saminddhe 'gna āyāhi vītaya ity apāno vā etavān apānamevaitayā saminddhe bṛhacchocā yaviṣṭhyety udāno vai bṛhacchocā udānamevaitayā saminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 3.2]
sa naḥ pṛthu śravāyyamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 4.1]
śrotraṃ vai pṛthu śravāyyaṃ śrotreṇa hīdamuru pṛthu śṛṇoti śrotramevaitayā saminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 4.2]
īḍenyo namasya iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 5.1]
vāgvā īḍenyā vāgghīdaṃ sarvamīṭṭe vācedaṃ sarvamīḍitaṃ vācamevaitayā saminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 5.2]
aśvo na devavāhana iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 6.1]
mano vai devavāhanam mano hīdam manasvinaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vanīvāhyate mana evaitayā saminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 6.2]
agne dīdyatam bṛhaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 7.1]
cakṣurvai dīdayeva cakṣurevaitayā saminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 7.2]
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 8.1]
ya evāyam madhyamaḥ prāṇa etamevaitayā saminddhe sā haiṣāntasthā prāṇānām ato hyanya ūrdhvāḥ prāṇā ato 'nye 'vāñco 'ntasthā ha bhavanty antasthām enam manyante ya evam etām antasthām prāṇānāṃ veda | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 8.2]
śociṣkeśas tam īmaha iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 9.1]
śiśnaṃ vai śociṣkeśaṃ śiśnaṃ hīdaṃ śiśninam bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śocayati śiśnam evaitayāsaminddhe | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 9.2]
samiddho agna āhuteti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 10.1]
ya evāyamavāṅprāṇa etamevaitayā saminddha ā juhotā duvasyateti sarvamātmānaṃ saminddha ā nakhebhyo 'tho lomabhyaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 10.2]
sa yadyenam prathamāyāṃ sāmidhenyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 11.1]
tam prati brūyāt prāṇaṃ vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhāḥ prāṇenātmana ārttimāriṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 11.2]
yadi dvitīyasyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 12.1]
tam prati brūyād apānaṃ vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhā apānenātmana ārttimāriṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 12.2]
yadi tṛtīyasyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 13.1]
tam prati brūyādudānaṃ vai ... udānenātmanaḥ ... syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 13.2]
yadi caturthyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 14.1]
tam pratibrūyācchrotraṃ vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhāḥ śrotreṇātmana ārttimāriṣyasi badhiro bhaviṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 14.2]
yadi pañcamyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 15.1]
tam prati brūyād vācaṃ vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhā vācātmana ārttimāriṣyasi mūko bhaviṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 15.2]
yadi ṣaṣṭhyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 16.1]
tam prati brūyān mano vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhā manasātmana ārttimāriṣyasi manomuṣigṛhīto momughaścariṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 16.2]
yadi saptamyāṃ anuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 17.1]
taṃ prati brūyāc cakṣurvā etadātmano 'gnāvādhāścakṣuṣātmana ārttimāriṣyasyandho bhaviṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 17.2]
yadyaṣṭamyām anuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 18.1]
taṃ prati brūyān madhyaṃ vā etatprāṇamātmano 'gnāvādhā madhyena prāṇenātmana ārtim āriṣyasyuddhmāya mariṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 18.2]
yadi navamyām anuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 19.1]
taṃ prati brūyācchiśnaṃ vā etadātmano 'gnāvādhāḥ śiśnenātmana ārttimāriṣyasi klībo bhaviṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 19.2]
yadi daśamyāmanuvyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 20.1]
taṃ prati brūyād avāñcaṃ vā etatprāṇamātmano 'gnāvādhā avācā prāṇenātmana ārttimāriṣyasy apinaddho mariṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 20.2]
yadyekādaśyāmanuvyāharet taṃ prati brūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 21.1]
sarvaṃ vā etadātmānamagnāvādhāḥ sarveṇātmanārtim āriṣyasi kṣipre 'muṃ lokam eṣyasīti tathā haiva syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 21.2]
sa yathā haivāgnim | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 22.1]
sāmidhenībhiḥ samiddhamāpadyārttiṃ nyetyevaṃ haiva brāhmaṇaṃ sāmidhenīrvidvāṃsaṃ samanubruvantam anuvyāhṛtyārttiṃ nyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 3 22.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 4, 4}
taṃ vā etamagniṃ samaindhiṣata | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 1.1]
samiddhe devebhyo juhavāmeti tasminnete eva prathame āhutī juhoti manase caiva vāce ca manaśca haiva vāk ca yujau devebhyo yajñaṃ vahataḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 1.2]
sa yadupāṃśu kriyate | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 2.1]
tanmano devebhyo yajñaṃ vahaty atha yadvācā niruktaṃ kriyate tadvāgdevebhyo yajñaṃ vahaty etad vā idaṃ dvayaṃ kriyate tadete evaitat saṃtarpayati tṛpte prīte devebhyo yajñaṃ vahāta iti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 2.2]
sruveṇa tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 3.1]
yaṃ manasa āghārayati vṛṣā hi mano vṛṣā hi sruvaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 3.2]
srucā tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 4.1]
yaṃ vāca āghārayati yoṣā hi vāg yoṣā hi sruk | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 4.2]
tūṣṇīṃ tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 5.1]
yaṃ manasa āghārayati na svāheti canāniruktaṃ hi mano 'niruktaṃ hyetadyattūṣṇīm | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 5.2]
mantreṇa tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 6.1]
yaṃ vāca āghārayati niruktā hi vāṅ nirukto hi mantraḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 6.2]
āsīnastamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 7.1]
yam manasa āghārayati tiṣṭhaṃstaṃ yaṃ vāce manaśca ha vai vākca yujau devebhyo yajñaṃ vahato yataro vai yujorhrasīyānbhavatyupavahaṃ vai tasmai kurvanti vāgvai manaso hrasīyasy aparimitataramiva hi manaḥ parimitatareva hi vāk tad vāca evaitadupavahaṃ karoti te sayujau devebhyo yajñaṃ vahatas tasmāttiṣṭhan vāca āghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 7.2]
devā ha vai yajñaṃ tanvānāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 8.1]
te 'surarakṣasebhya āsaṅgādbibhayāṃcakrus ta etaddakṣiṇataḥ pratyudaśrayann ucchritamiva hi vīryaṃ tasmāddakṣiṇatastiṣṭhann āghārayati sa yadubhayata āghārayati tasmādidam manaśca vākca samānameva sannāneva śiro ha vai yajñasyaitayoranyatara āghārayor mūlam anyataraḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 8.2]
sruveṇa tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 9.1]
yo mūlaṃ yajñasya srucā tamāghārayati yaḥ śiro yajñasya | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 9.2]
tūṣṇīṃ tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 10.1]
yo mūlam yajñasya tūṣṇīmiva hīdaṃ mūlaṃ no hyatra vāgvadati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 10.2]
mantreṇa tamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 11.1]
yaḥ śiro yajñasya vāgghi mantraḥ śīrṣṇo hīyamadhi vāgvadati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 11.2]
āsīnastamāghārayati | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 12.1]
yo mūlaṃ yajñasya niṣaṇṇamiva hīdam mūlaṃ tiṣṭhaṃstamāghārayati yaḥ śiro yajñasya tiṣṭhatīva hīdaṃ śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 12.2]
sa sruveṇa pūrvam āghāram āghāryāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 13.1]
agnim agnīt saṃmṛḍḍhīti yathā dhuramadhyūhedevaṃ tadyatpūrvamāghāram āghārayaty adhyuhya hi dhuraṃ yuñjanti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 13.2]
atha saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 14.1]
yunaktyevainam etadyukto devebhyo yajñaṃ vahāditi tasmāt saṃmārṣṭi parikrāmaṃ saṃmārṣṭi parikrāmaṃ hi yogyaṃ yuñjanti tristriḥ saṃmārṣṭi trivṛddhi yajñaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 14.2]
sa saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 15.1]
agne vājajidvājaṃ tvā sariṣyantaṃ tvā vājajitaṃ saṃmārjmīti yajñaṃ tvā vakṣyantaṃ yajñiyaṃ saṃmārjmīty evaitad āhāthopariṣṭāt tūṣṇīṃ tris tad yathā yuktvā prājet prehi vahety evam evaitat kaśayopakṣipati prehi devebhyo yajñaṃ vaheti tasmād upariṣṭāttūṣṇīṃ tris tad yad etadantareṇa karma kriyate tasmād idam manaśca vākca samānam eva sannāneva | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 4 15.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 4, 5}
sa srucottaramāghāramāghārayiṣyan | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 1.1]
pūrveṇa srucāvañjaliṃ nidadhāti namo devebhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhya iti tad devebhyaścaivaitatpitṛbhyaścārtvijyaṃ kariṣyannihnute suyame me bhūyāstamiti srucāvādatte subhare me bhūyāstam bhartuṃ vāṃ śakeyam ity evaitad āhāskannam adya devebhya ājyaṃ saṃbhriyāsam ity avikṣubdham adya devebhyo yajñaṃ tanavā ityevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 1.2]
aṅghriṇā viṣṇo mā tvāvakramiṣamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 2.1]
yajño vai viṣṇustasmā evaitannihnute mā tvāvakramiṣam iti vasumatīm agne te chāyāmupastheṣamiti sādhvīmagne te chāyām upastheṣam ity evaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 2.2]
viṣṇo sthānamasīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 3.1]
yajño vai viṣṇustasyeva hyetadantikaṃ tiṣṭhati tasmādāha viṣṇo sthānam asītīta indro vīryamakṛṇodityato hīndrastiṣṭhandakṣiṇato nāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsyapāhaṃs tasmādāheta indro vīryamakṛṇodity ūrdhvo 'dhvara āsthād ity adhvaro vai yajña ūrdhvo yajña āsthādityevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 3.2]
agne verhotraṃ verdūtyamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 4.1]
ubhayaṃ vā etadagnirdevānāṃ hotā ca dūtaśca tadubhayaṃ viddhi yaddevānām asīty evaitadāhāvatāṃ tvāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ava tvaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī iti nātra tirohitamivāsti sviṣṭakṛddevebhya indra ājyena haviṣābhūtsvāhetīndro vai yajñasya devatā tasmādāhendra ājyeneti vāce vā etamāghāram āghārayatīndro vāg ity u vā āhus tasmād v evāhendra ājyeneti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 4.2]
athāsaṃsparśayant srucau paryetya | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 5.1]
dhruvayā samanakti śiro vai yajñasyottara āghāra ātmā vai dhruvā tadātmany evaitacchiraḥ pratidadhāti śiro vai yajñasyottara āghāraḥ śrīrvai śiraḥ śrīrhi vai śiras tasmādyo 'rdhasya śreṣṭho bhavatyasāvamuṣyārdhasya śira ityāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 5.2]
yajamāna eva dhruvāmanu | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 6.1]
yo 'smā arātīyati sa upabhṛtamanu sa yaddhopabhṛtā samañjyād yo yajamānāyārātīyati tasmiṃchriyaṃ dadhyāt tad yajamāna evaitacchriyaṃ dadhāti tasmāddhruvayā samanakti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 6.2]
sa samanakti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 7.1]
saṃ jyotiṣā jyotiriti jyotir vā itarasyāmājyam bhavati jyotiritarasyāṃ te hyetadubhe jyotiṣī saṃgacchete tasmādevaṃ samanakti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 7.2]
athāto manasaścaiva vācaśca | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 8.1]
ahambhadra uditam manaśca ha vai vākcāhambhadra ūdāte | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 8.2]
taddha mana uvāca | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 9.1]
ahameva tvacchreyo 'smi na vai mayā tvaṃ kiṃ canānabhigataṃ vadasi sā yanmama tvaṃ kṛtānukarānuvartmāsy ahameva tvacchreyo 'smīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 9.2]
atha ha vāguvāca | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 10.1]
ahameva tvacchreyasyasmi yadvai tvaṃ vetthāhaṃ tadvijñapayāmyahaṃ saṃjñapayāmīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 10.2]
te prajāpatiṃ pratipraśnameyatuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 11.1]
sa prajāpatirmanasa evānūvāca mana eva tvacchreyo manaso vai tvaṃ kṛtānukarānuvartmāsi śreyaso vai pāpīyān kṛtānukaro 'nuvartmā bhavatīti | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 11.2]
sā ha vāk paroktā visiṣmiye | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 12.1]
tasyai garbhaḥ papāta sā ha vāk prajāpatim uvācāhavyavāḍ evāhaṃ tubhyam bhūyāsaṃ yāṃ mā parāvoca iti tasmādyatkiṃ ca prājāpatyaṃ yajñe kriyata upāṃśveva tatkriyate havyavāḍḍhi vākprajāpataya āsīt | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 12.2]
taddhaitaddevāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 13.1]
retaś carman vā yasminvā babhrus taddha sma pṛcchanty atreva tyād iti tato 'triḥ saṃbabhūva tasmād apyātreyyā yoṣitainasvy etasyai hi yoṣāyai vāco devatāyā ete sambhūtāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 4, 5 13.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 5, 1}
sa vai pravarāyāśrāvayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 1.1]
tad yat pravarāyāśrāvayati yajño vā āśrāvaṇaṃ yajñam abhivyāhṛtyātha hotāram pravṛṇā iti tasmāt pravarāyāśrāvayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 1.2]
sa idhmasaṃnahanānyevābhipadyāśrāvayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 2.1]
sa yad vānārabhya yajñamadhvaryurāśrāvayedvepano vā ha syādanyāṃ vārttimārchet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 2.2]
taddhaike | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 3.1]
vede stīrṇāyai barhirabhipadyāśrāvayantīdhmasya vā śakalam apacchidyābhipadyāśrāvayantīdaṃ vai kiṃcidyajñasyedaṃ yajñamabhipadyāśrāvayāma iti vadantas tad u tathā na kuryād etadvai kiṃcidyajñasya yairidhmaḥ saṃnaddho bhavaty agniṃ saṃmṛjanti tad v eva khalu yajñamabhipadyāśrāvayati tasmād idhmasaṃnahanāny evābhipadyāśrāvayet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 3.2]
sa āśrāvya | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 4.1]
ya eva devānāṃ hotā tamevāgre pravṛṇīte 'gnimeva tadagnaye caivaitaddevebhyaśca nihnute yadahāgre 'gnim pravṛṇīte tadagnaye nihnute 'tha yo devānāṃ hotā tamagre pravṛṇīte tad u devebhyo nihnute | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 4.2]
sa āha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 5.1]
agnirdevo daivyo hotety agnirhi devānāṃ hotā tasmādāhāgnirdevo daivyo hoteti tadagnaye caiva devebhyaśca nihnute yadahāgre 'gnimāha tadagnaye nihnute 'tha yo devānāṃ hotā tamagra āha tad u devebhyo nihnute | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 5.2]
devānyakṣadvidvāṃścikitvāniti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 6.1]
eṣa vai devānanuvidvānyadagniḥ sa enānanuvidvān anuṣṭhyā yakṣad ity evaitad āha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 6.2]
manuṣvadbharatavaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 7.1]
manurha vā agre yajñeneje tadanukṛtyemāḥ prajā yajante tasmādāha manuṣvaditi manoryajña ity u vā āhus tasmād v evāha manuṣvaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 7.2]
bharatavaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 8.1]
eṣa hi devebhyo havyam bharati tasmādbharato 'gnirityāhureṣa u vā imāḥ prajāḥ prāṇo bhūtvā bibharti tasmād v evāha bharatavaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 8.2]
athārṣeyam pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 9.1]
ṛṣibhyaścaivainametaddevebhyaśca nivedayatyayam mahāvīryo yo yajñam prāpaditi tasmādārṣeyam pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 9.2]
parastādarvākpravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 10.1]
parastāddhyarvācyaḥ prajāḥ prajāyante jyāyasaspataya u caivaitannihnuta idaṃ hi pitaivāgre 'tha putro 'tha pautras tasmāt parastād arvāk pravṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 10.2]
sa ārṣeyamuktvāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 11.1]
brahmaṇvaditi brahma hyagnis tasmādāha brahmaṇvad ity ā ca vakṣaditi tadyā evaitaddevatā āvoḍhavā āha tā evaitad āhā ca vakṣaditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 11.2]
brāhmaṇā asya yajñasya prāvitāra iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 12.1]
ete vai brāhmaṇā yajñasya prāvitāro ye 'nūcānā ete hyenaṃ tanvata eta enaṃ janayanti tad u tebhyo nihnute tasmādāha brāhmaṇā asya yajñasya prāvitāra iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 12.2]
asau mānuṣa iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 13.1]
tadimam mānuṣaṃ hotāraṃ pravṛṇīte hotā haiṣa purāthaitarhi hotā | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 13.2]
sa pravṛto hotā | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 14.1]
japati devatā upadhāvati yathānuṣṭhyā devebhyo vaṣaṭkuryādyathānuṣṭhyā devebhyo havyaṃ vahedyathā na hvaledevaṃ devatā upadhāvati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 14.2]
tatra japati etat tvā deva savitarvṛṇata iti tatsavitāram prasavāyopadhāvati sa hi devānām prasavitāgniṃ hotrāyeti tadagnaye caivaitaddevebhyaśca nihnute yadahāgre 'gnimāha tadagnaye nihnute 'tha yo devānāṃ hotā tamagra āha tad u devebhyo nihnute | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 15.1]
saha pitrā vaiśvānareṇeti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 16.1]
saṃvatsaro vai pitā vaiśvānaraḥ prajāpatis tat saṃvatsarāyaivaitat prajāpataye nihnute 'gne pūṣanbṛhaspate pra ca vada pra ca yajety anuvakṣyanvā etadyakṣyanbhavati tadaitābhya evaitaddevatābhyo nihnute yūyamanubrūta yūyaṃ yajateti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 16.2]
vasūnāṃ rātau syāma | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 17.1]
rudrāṇāmurvyāyāṃ svādityā aditaye syāmānehasa ityete vai trayā devā yadvasavo rudrā ādityā eteṣāmabhiguptau syāmetyevaitadāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 17.2]
juṣṭāmadya devebhyo vācam udyāsam iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 18.1]
juṣṭamadya devebhyo 'nūcyāsam ity evaitadāha taddhi samṛddhaṃ yo juṣṭaṃ devebhyo 'nubravat | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 18.2]
juṣṭām brahmabhya iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 19.1]
juṣṭamadya brāhmaṇebhyo 'nūcyāsam ity evaitadāha taddhi samṛddham yo juṣṭam brāhmaṇebhyo 'nubravat | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 19.2]
juṣṭāṃ narāśaṃsāyeti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 20.1]
prajā vai naras tat sarvābhyaḥ prajābhya āha taddhi samṛddhaṃ yaśca veda yaśca na sādhvanvavocatsādhvanvavocadityeva visṛjyante yadadya hotṛvarye jihmaṃ cakṣuḥ parāpatat agniṣ ṭat punar ābhriyājjātavedā vicarṣaṇiriti yathā yānagre 'gnīnhotrāya prāvṛṇata te prādhanvannevaṃ yanme 'tra pravareṇāmāyi tanme punar āpyāyayetyevaitad āha tatho hāsyaitat punar āpyāyate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 20.2]
athādhvaryuṃ cāgnīdhaṃ ca saṃmṛśati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 21.1]
mano vā adhvaryur vāgghotā tanmanaścaivaitadvācaṃ ca saṃdadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 21.2]
tatra japati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 22.1]
ṣaṇmorvīr aṃhasas pāntvagniśca pṛthivī cāpaśca vājaścāhaśca rātriścetyetā mā devatā ārtter gopāyantv ity evaitadāha tasyo hi na hvalāsti yametā devatā ārttergopāyeyuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 22.2]
atha hotṛṣadanamupāvartate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 23.1]
sa hotṛṣadanādekaṃ tṛṇaṃ nirasyati nirastaḥ parāvasuriti parāvasurha vai nāmāsurāṇāṃ hotā sa tamevaitaddhotṛṣadanānnirasyati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 23.2]
atha hotṛṣadana upaviśati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 24.1]
idamahamarvāvasoḥ sadane sīdāmīty arvāvasurvai nāma devānāṃ hotā tasyaivaitat sadane sīdati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 24.2]
tatra japati viśvakarmaṃs tanūpā asi mā modoṣiṣṭam mā mā hiṃsiṣṭam eṣa vāṃ loka ityudaṅṅejaty antarā vā etad āhavanīyaṃ ca gārhapatyaṃ cāste tad u tābhyāṃ nihnute mā modoṣiṣṭam mā mā hiṃsiṣṭamiti tathā hainametau na hiṃstaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 25.1]
athāgnimīkṣamāṇo japati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 26.1]
viśve devāḥ śāstana mā yatheha hotā vṛto manavai yanniṣadya pra me brūta bhāgadheyaṃ yathā vo yena pathā havyam ā vo vahānīti yathā yebhyaḥ pakvaṃ syāt tān brūyād v anu mā śāsta yathā va āhariṣyāmi yathā vaḥ parivekṣyāmīty evamevaitad deveṣu praśāsanamicchate 'nu mā śāsta yathā vo 'nuṣṭhyā vaṣaṭkuryām anuṣṭhyā havyaṃ vaheyam iti tasmād evaṃ japati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 1 26.2]
{ŚBM, 1, 5, 2}
agnirhotā vettvagnerhotramiti agniridaṃ hotā vettvityevaitadāhāgnerhotramiti tasyo hi hotraṃ vettu prāvitramiti yajño vai prāvitraṃ vettu yajñam ityevaitadāha sādhu te yajamāna devateti sādhu te yajamāna devatā yasya te 'gnirhotety evaitadāha ghṛtavatīmadhvaryo srucam āsyasveti tad adhvaryuṃ prasauti sa yadekāmivāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 1.1]
yajamāna eva juhūmanu | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 2.1]
yo 'smā arātīyati sa upabhṛtamanu sa yaddve iva brūyādyajamānāya dviṣantam bhrātṛvyam pratyudyāminaṃ kuryād attaiva juhūmanvādya upabhṛtamanu sa yaddve iva brūyādattra ādyam pratyudyāminaṃ kuryāt tasmādekāmivaivāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 2.2]
devayuvaṃ viśvavārāmiti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 3.1]
upastautyevaināmetanmahayatyeva yadāha devayuvaṃ viśvavārām itīḍāmahai devāṁ īḍenyān namasyāma namasyānyajāma yajñiyān itīḍāmahai tāndevānya īḍenyā namasyāma tānye namasyā yajāma yajñiyān iti manuṣyā vā īḍenyāḥ pitaro namasyā devā yajñiyāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 3.2]
yā vai prajā yajñe 'nanvābhaktāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 4.1]
parābhūtā vai tā evamevaitadyā imāḥ prajā aparābhūtās tā yajña ābhajati manuṣyānanu paśavo devānanu vayāṃsyoṣadhayo vanaspatayo yadidaṃ kiṃcaivam u tatsarvaṃ yajña ābhaktam | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 4.2]
tā vā etāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 5.1]
nava vyāhṛtayo bhavanti naveme puruṣe prāṇā etānevāsminnetaddadhāti tasmānnava vyāhṛtayo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 5.2]
yajño ha devebhyo 'pacakrāma | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 6.1]
taṃ devā anvamantrayantā naḥ śṛṇūpa na āvartasveti so 'stu tathetyeva devānupāvavarta tenopāvṛttena devā ayajanta teneṣṭvaitadabhavanyadidaṃ devāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 6.2]
sa yadāśrāvayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 7.1]
yajñamevaitadanumantrayata ā naḥ śṛṇūpa na āvartasvety atha yatpratyāśrāvayati yajña evaitad upāvartate 'stu tatheti tenopāvṛttena retasā bhūtenartvijaḥ sampradāyaṃ caranti yajamānena parokṣaṃ yathā pūrṇapātreṇa sampradāyaṃ careyurevamanenartvijaḥ sampradāyaṃ caranti tad vācaivaitat sampradāyaṃ caranti vāgghi yajño vāg u hi retas tad etenaivaitat saṃpradāyaṃ caranti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 7.2]
so 'nubrūhītyevoktvādhvaryuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 8.1]
nāpavyāharen no eva hotāpavyāhared āśrāvayatyadhvaryus tad agnīdhaṃ yajña upāvartate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 8.2]
so 'gnīn nāpavyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 9.1]
ā pratyāśrāvaṇāt pratyāśrāvayatyagnīt tat punaradhvaryuṃ yajña upāvartate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 9.2]
so 'dhvaryurnāpavyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 10.1]
ā yajeti vaktor yajetyevādhvaryurhotre yajñaṃ samprayacchati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 10.2]
sa hotā nāpavyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 11.1]
ā vaṣaṭkārāt taṃ vaṣaṭkāreṇāgnāveva yonau reto bhūtaṃ siñcaty agnirvai yonir yajñasya sa tataḥ prajāyata iti nu haviryajñe 'tha saumye 'dhvare | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 11.2]
sa vai grahaṃ gṛhītvādhvaryuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 12.1]
nāpavyāhared opākaraṇād upāvartadhvamityevādhvaryurudgātṛbhyo yajñaṃ samprayacchati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 12.2]
ta udgātāro nāpavyāhareyuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 13.1]
ottamāyā eṣottametyevodgātāro hotre yajñaṃ samprayacchanti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 13.2]
sa hotā nāpavyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 14.1]
ā vaṣaṭkārāt taṃ vaṣaṭkāreṇāgnāveva yonau reto bhūtaṃ siñcaty agnirvai yonir yajñasya sa tataḥ prajāyate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 14.2]
sa yaddha so 'pavyāharet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 15.1]
yaṃ yajña upāvartate yathā pūrṇapātram parāsiñcedevaṃ ha sa yajamānam parāsiñcet sa yatra haivamṛtvijaḥ saṃvidānā yajñena caranti sarvameva tatra kalpate na muhyati tasmādevameva yajño bhartavyaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 15.2]
tā vā etāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 16.1]
pañca vyāhṛtayo bhavanty o śrāvayāstu śrauṣaḍyaja ye yajāmahe vauṣaḍiti pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktaḥ paśuḥ pañcartavaḥ saṃvatsarasyaiṣaikā yajñasya mātraiṣā sampat | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 16.2]
tāsāṃ saptadaśākṣarāṇi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 17.1]
saptadaśo vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiryajña eṣaikā yajñasya mātraiṣā sampat | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 17.2]
o śrāvayeti vai devāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 18.1]
purovātaṃ sasṛjire 'stu śrauṣaḍityabhrāṇi samaplāvayan yajeti vidyutaṃ ye yajāmaha iti stanayitnuṃ vaṣaṭkāreṇaiva prāvarṣayan | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 18.2]
sa yadi vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syāt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 19.1]
yadīṣṭyā vā yajeta darśapūrṇamāsayor vaiva brūyād vṛṣṭikāmo vā asmīti tatro adhvaryuṃ brūyāt purovātaṃ ca vidyutaṃ ca manasā dhyāyetyabhrāṇi manasā dhyāyetyagnīdhaṃ stanayitnuṃ ca varṣaṃ ca manasā dhyāyeti hotāraṃ sarvāṇyetāni manasā dhyāyeti brahmāṇaṃ varṣati haiva tatra yatraivamṛtvijaḥ saṃvidānā yajñena caranti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 19.2]
o śrāvayeti vai devāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 20.1]
virājam abhyājuhuvur astu śrauṣaḍiti vatsam upāvāsṛjan yajetyudajayan ye yajāmaha ity upāsīdan vaṣaṭkāreṇaiva virājam aduhateyaṃ vai virāḍ asyai vā eṣa doha evaṃ ha vā asmā iyaṃ virāṭ sarvān kāmānduhe ya evametaṃ virājo dohaṃ veda | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 2 20.2]

devāśca vā asurāśca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 2.1]
ubhaye prājāpatyāḥ paspṛdhira etasminyajñe prajāpatau pitari saṃvatsare 'smākamayam bhaviṣyatyasmākamayam bhaviṣyatīti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 2.2]
tato devāḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 3.1]
arcantaḥ śrāmyantaścerus ta etānprayājāndadṛśus tairayajanta tair ṛtūnt saṃvatsaram prājayann ṛtubhyaḥ saṃvatsarāt sapatnān antarāyaṃs tasmātprajayāḥ prajayā ha vai nāmaitadyatprayājā iti tatho evaiṣa etair ṛtūnt saṃvatsaram prayajaty ṛtubhyaḥ saṃvatsarātsapatnānantareti tasmātprayājairyajate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 3.2]
te vā ājyahaviṣo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 4.1]
vajro vā ājyametena vai devā vajreṇājyenartūnt saṃvatsaram prājayannṛtubhyaḥ saṃvatsarāt sapatnānantarāyaṃs tatho evaiṣa etena vajreṇājyenartūnt saṃvatsaram prajayaty ṛtubhyaḥ saṃvatsarātsapatnān antareti tasmādājyahaviṣo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 4.2]
etadvai saṃvatsarasya svam payaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 5.1]
yadājyaṃ tatsvenaivainametatpayasā devāḥ svyakurvata tatho evainameṣa etat svenaiva payasā svīkurute tasmādājyahaviṣo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 5.2]
sa yatraiva tiṣṭhanprayājebhya āśrāvayet | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 6.1]
tata eva nāpakrāmet saṃgrāmo vā eṣa saṃnidhīyate yaḥ prayājair yajate yataro vai saṃyattayoḥ parājayate 'pa vai saṃkrāmaty abhitarām u vai jayan krāmati tasmādabhitarāmabhitarāmeva krāmed abhitarām abhitarām āhutīrjuhuyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 6.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 7.1]
yatraiva tiṣṭhanprayājebhya āśrāvayettata eva nāpakrāmed yatro eva samiddhatamam manyeta tadāhutīr juhuyāt samiddhahomena hyeva samṛddhā āhutayaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 7.2]
sa āśrāvyāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 8.1]
samidho yajeti tadvasantaṃ saminddhe sa vasantaḥ samiddho 'nyān ṛtūnt saminddha ṛtavaḥ samiddhāḥ prajāśca prajanayantyoṣadhīśca pacanti tad v eva khalu sarvānṛtūnnirāhātha yaja yajety evottarān āhājāmitāyai jāmi ha kuryād yat tanūnapātaṃ yajeḍo yajeti brūyāt tasmād yaja yajetyevottarānāha | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 8.2]
sa vai samidho yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 9.1]
vasanto vai samidvasantameva taddevā avṛñjata vasantāt sapatnān antarāyan vasantam evaiṣa etadvṛṅkte vasantāt sapatnān antareti tasmātsamidho yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 9.2]
atha tanūnapātaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 10.1]
grīṣmo vai tanūnapād grīṣmo hyāsām prajānāṃ tanūstapati grīṣmameva taddevā avṛñjata grīṣmātsapatnānantarāyan grīṣmamevaiṣa etadvṛṅkte grīṣmātsapatnānantareti tasmāttanūnapātaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 10.2]
atheḍo yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 11.1]
varṣā vā iḍa iti hi varṣā iḍo yadidaṃ kṣudraṃ sarīsṛpaṃ grīṣmahemantābhyāṃ nityaktam bhavati tadvarṣā īḍitam ivānnam icchamānaṃ carati tasmādvarṣā iḍo varṣā eva taddevā avṛñjata varṣābhyaḥ sapatnān antarāyan varṣā u evaiṣa etadvṛṅkte varṣābhyaḥ sapatnānantareti tasmādiḍo yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 11.2]
atha barhiryajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 12.1]
śaradvai barhiriti hi śarad barhir yā imā oṣadhayo grīṣmahemantābhyāṃ nityaktā bhavanti tā varṣā vardhante tāḥ śaradi barhiṣo rūpaṃ prastīrṇāḥ śere tasmāccharad barhiḥ śaradameva taddevā avṛñjata śaradaḥ sapatnāntarāyañcharadam evaiṣa etadvṛṅkte śaradaḥ sapatnānantareti tasmād barhiryajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 12.2]
atha svāhā svāheti yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 13.1]
anto vai yajñasya svāhākāro 'nta ṛtūnāṃ hemanto vasantāddhi parārdhyo 'ntenaiva tadantaṃ devā avṛñjatāntenāntāt sapatnān antarāyann anteno evaiṣa etadantaṃ vṛṅkte 'ntenāntātsapatnānantareti tasmātsvāheti yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 13.2]
tadvā etat | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 14.1]
vasanta eva hemantāt punarasur etasmāddhyeṣa punarbhavati punarha vā asmiṃlloke bhavati ya evametad veda | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 14.2]
sa vai vyantu vetviti yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 15.1]
ajāmitāyai jāmi ha kuryād yad vyantu vyantviti vaiva yajed vetu vetviti vā vyantviti vai yoṣā vetviti vṛṣā mithunamevaitatprajananaṃ kriyate tasmādvyantu vetviti yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 15.2]
atha caturthe prayāje samānayati barhiṣi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 16.1]
prajā vai barhī reta ājyaṃ tatprajāsvevaitadretaḥ sicyate tena retasā siktenemāḥ prajāḥ punarabhyāvartam prajāyante tasmāccaturthe prayāje samānayati barhiṣi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 16.2]
saṃgrāmo vā eṣa saṃnidhīyate | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 17.1]
yaḥ prayājairyajate yataraṃ vai saṃyattayor mitram āgacchati sa jayati tadetadupabhṛto 'dhi juhūm mitram āgacchati tena prajayati tasmāccaturthe prayāje samānayati barhiṣi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 17.2]
yajamāna eva juhūmanu | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 18.1]
yo 'smā arātīyati sa upabhṛtam anu yajamānāyaivaitaddviṣantam bhrātṛvyam baliṃ hārayaty attaiva juhūmanvādya upabhṛtamanv attra evaitadādyam baliṃ hārayati tasmāccaturthe prayāje samānayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 18.2]
sa vā anavamṛśant samānayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 19.1]
sa yaddhāvamṛśed yajamānaṃ dviṣatā bhrātṛvyenāvamṛśed attāram ādyenāvamṛśet tasmād anavamṛśant samānayati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 19.2]
athottarāṃ juhūmadhyūhati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 20.1]
yajamānam evaitad dviṣati bhrātṛvye 'dhyūhaty attāramādye 'dhyūhati tasmāduttarāṃ juhūmadhyūhati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 20.2]
devā ha vā ūcuḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 21.1]
hanta vijitamevānu sarvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayāma yadi no 'surarakṣasānyāsajeyuḥ saṃsthita eva no yajñaḥ syāditi | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 21.2]
ta uttame prayāje | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 22.1]
svāhākāreṇaiva sarvaṃ yajñaṃ samasthāpayant svāhāgnimiti tad āgneyam ājyabhāgaṃ samasthāpayant svāhā somamiti tat saumyamājyabhāgaṃ samasthāpayant svāhāgnimiti tadya eṣa ubhayatrācyuta āgneyaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati taṃ samasthāpayan | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 22.2]
atha yathādevataṃ | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 23.1]
svāhā devā ājyapā iti tat prayājānuyājānt samasthāpayan prayājānuyājā vai devā ājyapā juṣāṇo agnirājyasya vetviti tadagniṃ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ samasthāpayannagnirhi sviṣṭakṛt sa eṣo 'pyetarhi tathaiva yajñaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate yathaivainaṃ devāḥ samasthāpayaṃstasmāduttame prayāje svāhāsvāheti yajati yāvanti havīṃṣi bhavanti vijitam evaitad anu sarvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayati tasmād yad ata ūrdhvaṃ viloma yajñe kriyeta na tad ādriyeta saṃsthito me yajña iti ha vidyāt sa haiṣa yajño yātayāmevāsa yathā vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ hutaṃ svāhākṛtam | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 23.2]
te devā akāmayanta | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 24.1]
kathaṃ nvimaṃ yajñam punar āpyāyayemāyātayāmānaṃ kuryāma tenāyātayāmnā pracaremeti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 24.2]
sa yajjuhvāmājyam pariśiṣṭamāsīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 25.1]
yena yajñaṃ samasthāpayaṃstenaiva yathāpūrvaṃ havīṃṣyabhyaghārayan punarevaināni tad āpyāyayann ayātayāmānyakurvann ayātayāma hyājyaṃ tasmāduttamam prayājamiṣṭvā yathāpūrvaṃ havīṃṣy abhighārayati punarevaināni tadāpyāyayatyayātayāmāni karotyayātayāma hyājyaṃ tasmādyasya kasya ca haviṣo 'vadyati punar eva tad abhighārayati sviṣṭakṛta eva tat punar āpyāyaty ayātayāma karoty atha yadā sviṣṭakṛte 'vadyati na tataḥ punar abhighārayati no hi tataḥ kāṃcana haviṣo 'gnāvāhutiṃ hoṣyan bhavati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 3 25.2]

sa vai samidho yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 1.1]
prāṇā vai samidhaḥ prāṇānevaitat saminddhe prāṇairhyayam puruṣaḥ samiddhas tasmād abhimṛśeti brūyād yadyupatāpī syāt sa yadyuṣṇaḥ syād aiva tāvacchaṃseta samiddho hi sa tāvadbhavati yady u śītaḥ syānnāśaṃseta tat prāṇān evāsminnetad dadhāti tasmātsamidho yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 1.2]
atha tanūnapātaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 2.1]
reto vai tanūnapād reta evaitatsiñcati tasmāttanūnapātaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 2.2]
atheḍo yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 3.1]
prajā vā iḍo yadā vai retaḥ siktaṃ prajāyate 'tha tad īḍitam ivānnam icchamānaṃ carati tat praivaitajjanayati tasmādiḍo yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 3.2]
atha barhiryajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 4.1]

atha svāhāsvāheti yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 5.1]
hemanto vā ṛtūnāṃ svāhākāro hemanto hīmāḥ prajāḥ svaṃ vaśamupanayate tasmāddhemanmlāyanty oṣadhayaḥ pra vanaspatīnām palāśāni mucyante pratitarām iva vayāṃsi bhavanty adhastarāmiva vayāṃsi patanti vipatitalomeva pāpaḥ puruṣo bhavati hemanto hīmāḥ prajāḥ svaṃ vaśamupanayate svī ha vai tamardhaṃ kurute śriye 'nnādyāya yasminnardhe bhavati ya evam etad veda | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 5.2]
devāśca vā asurāśca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 6.1]
ubhaye prājāpatyāḥ paspṛdhire te daṇḍair dhanurbhirna vyajayanta te hāvijayamānā ūcur hanta vācyeva brahman vijigīṣāmahai sa yo no vācaṃ vyāhṛtām mithunena nānunikrāmāt sa sarvam parājayātā atha sarvam itare jayāniti tatheti devā abruvaṃste devā indramabruvan vyāhareti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 6.2]
sa indro 'bravīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 7.1]
eko mamety athāsmākam eketītare 'bruvaṃs tad u tan mithunam evāvindan mithunaṃ hyekaścaikā ca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 7.2]
dvau mametīndro 'bravīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 8.1]
athāsmākaṃ dve itītare 'bruvaṃs tad u tan mithunam evāvindan mithunaṃ hi dvau ca dve ca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 8.2]
trayo mametīndro 'bravīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 9.1]
athāsmākaṃ tisra itītare 'bruvaṃs tad u tan mithunamevāvindan mithunaṃ hi trayaśca tisraśca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 9.2]
catvāro mametīndro 'bravīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 10.1]
athāsmākaṃ catasra itītare 'bruvaṃs tad u tan mithunamevāvindan mithunaṃ hi catvāraśca catasraśca | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 10.2]
pañca mametīndro 'bravīt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 11.1]
tata itare mithunaṃ nāvindan no hyata ūrdhvaṃ mithunamasti pañca pañceti hyevaitad ubhayam bhavati tato 'surāḥ sarvam parājayanta sarvasmāddevā asurān ajayant sarvasmātsapatnān asurān nirabhajan | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 11.2]
tasmātprathame prayāja iṣṭe brūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 12.1]
eko mametyekā tasya yamahaṃ dveṣmīti yady u na dviṣyād yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti brūyāt | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 12.2]
dvau mameti dvitīye prayāje | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 13.1]
dve tasya yo 'smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 13.2]
trayo mameti tṛtīye prayāje | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 14.1]

catvāro mameti caturthe prayāje | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 15.1]
catasrastasya yo 'smāndveṣṭi yaṃca vayaṃ dviṣma iti | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 15.2]
pañca mameti pañcame prayāje | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 16.1]
na tasya kiṃcana yo 'smāndveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti sa pañca pañcetyeva bhavanparābhavati tathāsya sarvaṃ saṃvṛṅkte sarvasmātsapatnānnirbhajati ya evametadveda | [ŚBM, 1, 5, 4 16.2]

te vā ete ulmuke udūhanti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 1.1]
anuyājebhyo yātayāmeva vā etadagnirbhavati devebhyo hi yajñamūhivān bhavaty ayātayāmnyanuyājāṃs tanavāmahā iti tasmādvā ete ulmuke udūhanti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 1.2]

atha samidhamabhyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 3.1]

tāṃ hotānumantrayate | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 4.1]
eṣā te agne samit tayā vardhasva cā ca pyāyasva vardhiṣīmahi ca vayam ā ca pyāsiṣīmahīti tadyathaivādaḥ samidhyamānāyānvāhaivam evaitad anvāha tadetaddhotuḥ karma sa yadi manyeta na hotā vedetyapi svayam eva yajamāno 'numantrayeta | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 4.2]
atha saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 5.1]
yunaktyevainam etadyukto yadata ūrdhvamasaṃsthitaṃ yajñasya tadvahāditi tasmāt saṃmārṣṭi sakṛt sakṛt saṃmārṣṭi tristrirvā agre devebhyaḥ saṃmṛjanti nettathā karavāma yathā devebhya iti tasmāt sakṛtsakṛt saṃmārṣṭy ajāmitāyai jāmi ha kuryādyattriḥ pūrvaṃ triraparaṃ tasmātsakṛtsakṛt saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 5.2]
sa saṃmārṣṭi | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 6.1]
agne vājajidvājaṃ tvā sasṛvāṃsaṃ vājajitaṃ saṃmārjmīti sariṣyantamiti vā agra āha sariṣyanniva hi tarhi bhavaty athātra sasṛvāṃsamiti sasṛveva hyatra bhavati tasmādāha sasṛvāṃsamiti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 6.2]
athānuyājānyajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 7.1]
yā vā etena yajñena devatā hvayati yābhya eṣa yajñastāyate sarvā vai tattā iṣṭā bhavanti tadyattāsu sarvāsviṣṭāsvathaitat paścevānuyajati tasmādanuyājā nāma | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 7.2]
atha yadanuyājānyajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 8.1]
chandāṃsi vā anuyājāḥ paśavo vai devānāṃ chandāṃsi tadyathedaṃ paśavo yuktā manuṣyebhyo vahanty evaṃ chandāṃsi yuktāni devebhyo yajñaṃ vahanti tadyatra chandāṃsi devānt samatarpayann atha chandāṃsi devāḥ samatarpayaṃs tadatas tat prāg abhūd yacchandāṃsi yuktāni devebhyo yajñam avākṣur yad enānt samatītṛpan | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 8.2]
atha yadanuyājānyajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 9.1]
chandāṃsi vā anuyājāś chandāṃsyevaitatsaṃtarpayati tasmādanuyājānyajati tasmād yena vāhanena dhāvayet tadvimucya brūyāt pāyayatainat suhitaṃ kurutety eṣa u vāhanasyāpahnavaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 9.2]
sa vai khalu barhiḥ prathamaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 10.1]
tadvai kaniṣṭhaṃ chandaḥ sadgāyatrī prathamā chandasāṃ yujyate tad u tadvīryeṇaiva yacchyeno bhūtvā divaḥ somamāharat tad ayathāyatham manyante yatkaniṣṭhaṃ chandaḥ sadgāyatrī prathamā chandasāṃ yujyate 'thātra yathāyathaṃ devāśchandāṃsyakalpayannanuyājeṣu net pāpavasyasam asad iti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 10.2]
sa vai khalu barhiḥ prathamaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 11.1]
ayaṃ vai loko barhir oṣadhayo barhir asminnevaitalloka oṣadhīr dadhāti tā imā asmiṃlloka oṣadhayaḥ pratiṣṭhitās tadidaṃ sarvaṃ jagadasyāṃ teneyaṃ jagatī tajjagatīm prathamāmakurvan | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 11.2]
atha narāśaṃsaṃ dvitīyaṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 12.1]
antarikṣaṃ vai narāśaṃsaḥ prajā vai naras tā imā antarikṣamanu vāvadyamānāḥ prajāścaranti yadvai vadati śaṃsatīti vai tadāhus tasmādantarikṣaṃ narāśaṃso 'ntarikṣam u vai triṣṭup tat triṣṭubhaṃ dvitīyāmakurvan | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 12.2]
athāgniruttamaḥ | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 13.1]

devānyajety evādhvaryurāha | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 14.1]

athottamam anuyājam iṣṭvā samānīya juhoti | [ŚBM, 1, 8, 2 17.1]

tām u hāgnir abhidadhyau mithuny anayā syām iti | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 15.1]

te hocur hantedaṃ juhavāmahā iti | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 16.1]
kasmai na idam prathamāya hoṣyantīti | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 16.2]
mahyam iti haivāgnir uvāca mahyam iti yo 'yam pavate mahyam iti sūryaḥ | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 16.3]
te na saṃpādayāṃcakruḥ | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 16.4]
te hāsampādyocuḥ prajāpatim eva pitaram pratyayāma | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 16.5]

sa hovācāgnaye | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.1]
agnir anuṣṭhyā svaṃ retaḥ prajanayiṣyate | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.2]
tathā prajaniṣyadhva iti | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.3]
atha tubhyam iti sūryam | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.4]
atha yad eva hūyamānasya vyaśnute tad evaitasya yo 'yam pavata iti | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.5]
tad ebhya idam apy etarhi tathaiva juhvaty agnaya eva sāyaṃ sūryāya prātaḥ | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.6]
atha yad eva hūyamānasya vyaśnute tad evaitasya yo 'yam pavate | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 17.7]
te hutvā devā imām prajātim prājāyanta yaiṣām iyam prajātir imāṃ vijitiṃ vyajayanta yeyam eṣāṃ vijitiḥ | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 18.1]
imam eva lokam agnir ajayad antarikṣaṃ vāyur divam eva sūryaḥ | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 18.2]
sa yo haivaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoty etāṃ haiva prajātim prajāyate yām eta etat prājāyantaitāṃ vijitiṃ vijayate yām eta etad vyajayanta | [ŚBM, 2, 2, 4 18.3]
