varuṇasavo vā eṣa yadrājasūyam | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 21.1]
pṛthivy u haitasmādbibheti mahadvā ayamabhūdyo 'bhyaṣeci yadvai māyaṃ nāvadṛṇīyādity eṣa u hāsyai bibheti yadvai meyaṃ nāvadhūnvīteti tadanayaivaitanmitradheyaṃ kurute na hi mātā putraṃ hinasti na putro mātaraṃ tasmādevaṃ japati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 21.2]
so 'vatiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 22.1]
haṃsaḥ śuciṣadvasurantarikṣasaddhotā vediṣadatithirduroṇasat | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 22.2]
nṛṣad varasad ṛtasad vyomasad abjā gojā ṛtajā adrijā ṛtam bṛhad ity etāmatichandasaṃ japann eṣā vai sarvāṇi chandāṃsi yadatichandās tathainam pāpmā nānvavatiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 22.3]
taṃ na saṃgrahītānvavatiṣṭhet | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 23.1]
nettaṃ lokam anvavatiṣṭhād yaṃ suṣuvāṇo 'nvavāsthāditi taṃ sarathameva rathavāhana ādadhati tato 'vāṅ apapravate tathā taṃ lokaṃ nānvavatiṣṭhati yaṃ suṣuvāṇo 'nvavāsthāt | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 23.2]
uttareṇāhavanīyam pūrvāgnirudvṛto bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 24.1]
sa rathavāhanasya dakṣiṇamanvanuṣyandaṃ śatamānau pravṛttāvābadhnāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 24.2]
audumbarīṃ śākhāmupagūhati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 25.1]
tayoranyataramupaspṛśatīyadasyāyurasyāyurmayi dhehi yuṅṅ asi varco mayi dhehīti tadāyurvarca ātmandhatte | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 25.2]
athaudumbarīṃ śākhāmupaspṛśati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 26.1]
ūrg asy ūrjam mayi dhehīti tad ūrjam ātman dhatte tasyaitasya karmaṇa etāv eva śatamānau pravṛttau dakṣiṇā tau brahmaṇe dadāti brahmā hi yajñaṃ dakṣiṇato 'bhigopāyati tasmāttau brahmaṇe dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 26.2]
agreṇa maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyam | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 27.1]
maitrāvaruṇī payasyā nihitā bhavati tāmasya bāhū abhyupāvaharatīndrasya vāṃ vīryakṛto bāhū abhyupāvaharāmīti paśūnāṃ vā eṣa raso yatpayasyā tat paśūnām evāsyaitad rasam bāhū abhyupāvaharati tadyanmaitrāvaruṇī bhavati mitrāvaruṇā u hi bāhū tasmānmaitrāvaruṇī bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 3 27.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 4, 4}
maitrāvaruṇyā payasyayā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 1.1]
tasyā aniṣṭa eva sviṣṭakṛdbhavatyathāsmā āsandīm āharanty uparisadyaṃ vā eṣa jayati yo jayatyantarikṣasadyaṃ tad enam uparyāsīnam adhastādimāḥ prajā upāsate tasmādasmā āsandīmāharanti saiṣā khādirī vitṛṇṇā bhavati yeyaṃ vardhravyutā bharatānām | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 1.2]
tāmagreṇa | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 2.1]
maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyaṃ nidadhāti syonāsi suṣadāsīti śivāmevaitacchagmāṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 2.2]
athādhīvāsamāstṛṇāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 3.1]
kṣatrasya yonirasīti tadyaiva kṣatrasya yonistāmevaitatkaroti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 3.2]
athainamāsādayati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 4.1]
syonāmāsīda suṣadāmāsīdeti śivāṃ śagmāmāsīdety evaitad āha kṣatrasya yonimāsīdeti tadyaiva kṣatrasya yonistasyāmevainametaddadhāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 4.2]
athāntarāṃse 'bhimṛśya japati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 5.1]
niṣasāda dhṛtavrata iti dhṛtavrato vai rājā na vā eṣa sarvasmā iva vadanāya na sarvasmā iva karmaṇe yadeva sādhu vadedyatsādhu kuryāttasmai vā eṣa ca śrotriyaś caitau ha vai dvau manuṣyeṣu dhṛtavratau tasmādāha niṣasāda dhṛtavrata iti varuṇaḥ pastyāsv eti viśo vai pastyā vikṣv ety evaitadāha sāmrājyāya sukraturiti rājyāyetyevaitadāha yadāha sāmrājyāya sukraturiti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 5.2]
athāsmai pañcākṣānpāṇāvāvapati abhibhūrasyetāste pañca diśaḥ kalpantām ity eṣa vā ayān abhibhūr yat kalir eṣa hi sarvān ayān abhibhavati tasmādāhābhibhūrasīty etās te pañca diśaḥ kalpantāmiti pañca vai diśastadasmai sarvā eva diśaḥ kalpayati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 6.1]
athainam pṛṣṭhatastūṣṇīmeva daṇḍairghnanti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 7.1]
taṃ daṇḍairghnanto daṇḍavadhamatinayanti tasmād rājādaṇḍyo yadenaṃ daṇḍavadhamatinayanti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 7.2]
atha varaṃ vṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 8.1]
yaṃ ha vai kaṃ ca suṣuvāṇo varaṃ vṛṇīte so 'smai sarvaḥ samṛdhyate tasmādvaraṃ vṛṇīte | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 8.2]
sa brahmannityeva prathamamāmantrayate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 9.1]
brahma prathamamabhivyāharāṇi brahmaprasūtāṃ vācaṃ vadānīti tasmād brahmannityeva prathamamāmantrayate tvam brahmāsītītaraḥ pratyāha savitāsi satyaprasava iti vīryamevāsminnetaddadhāti savitārameva satyaprasavaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 9.2]
brahmannityeva dvitīyamāmantrayate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 10.1]
tvam brahmāsītītaraḥ pratyāha varuṇo 'si satyaujā iti vīryamevāsminn etaddadhāti varuṇameva satyaujasaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 10.2]
brahmannityeva tṛtīyamāmantrayate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 11.1]
tvam brahmāsītītaraḥ pratyāhendro 'si viśaujā iti vīryamevāsminn etad dadhātīndrameva viśaujasaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 11.2]
brahmannityeva caturthamāmantrayate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 12.1]
tvam brahmāsītītaraḥ pratyāha rudro 'si suśeva iti tadvīryāṇyevāsminn etat pūrvāṇi dadhāty athainam etacchamayatyeva tasmādeṣa sarvasyeśāno mṛḍayati yadenaṃ śamayati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 12.2]
brahmannityeva pañcamamāmantrayate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 13.1]
tvam brahmāsītītaro 'niruktam pratyāha parimitaṃ vai niruktaṃ tatparimitam evāsminnetatpūrvaṃ vīryaṃ dadhāty athātrāniruktam pratyāhāparimitaṃ vā aniruktaṃ tadaparimitamevāsminnetatsarvaṃ vīryaṃ dadhāti tasmādatrāniruktam pratyāha | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 13.2]
atha sumaṅgalanāmānaṃ hvayati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 14.1]
bahukāra śreyaskara bhūyaskareti ya evaṃnāmā bhavati kalyāṇam evaitan mānuṣyai vāco vadati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 14.2]
athāsmai brāhmaṇa sphyam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 15.1]
adhvaryurvā yo vāsya purohito bhavatīndrasya vajro 'si tena me radhyeti vajro vai sphyaḥ sa etena vajreṇa brāhmaṇo rājānamātmano 'balīyāṃsaṃ kurute yo vai rājā brāhmaṇād abalīyān amitrebhyo vai sa balīyānbhavati tadamitrebhya evainametadbalīyāṃsaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 15.2]
taṃ rājā rājabhrātre prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 16.1]
indrasya vajro 'si tena me radhyeti tena rājā rājabhrātaramātmano 'balīyāṃsaṃ kurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 16.2]
taṃ rājabhrātā sūtāya vā sthapataye vā prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 17.1]
indrasya vajro 'si tena me radhyeti tena rājabhrātā sūtaṃ vā sthapatiṃ vātmano 'balīyāṃsaṃ kurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 17.2]
taṃ sūto vā sthapatirvā grāmaṇye prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 18.1]
indrasya vajro 'si tena me radhyeti tena sūto vā sthapatirvā grāmaṇyamātmano 'balīyāṃsaṃ kurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 18.2]
taṃ grāmaṇīḥ sajātāya prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 19.1]
indrasya vajro 'si tena me radhyeti tena grāmaṇīḥ sajātamātmano 'balīyāṃsaṃ kurute tadyadevaṃ samprayacchante net pāpavasyasam asad yathāpūrvamasaditi tasmādevaṃ samprayacchante | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 19.2]
atha sajātaśca pratiprasthātā ca | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 20.1]
etena sphyena pūrvāgnau śukrasya purorucādhidevanaṃ kuruto 'ttā vai śukro 'ttāramevaitatkurutaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 20.2]
atha manthinaḥ purorucā vimitaṃ viminutaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 21.1]
ādyo vai manthī tadattāramevaitatkṛtvāthāsmā etadādyaṃ janayatastasmānmanthinaḥ purorucā vimitaṃ viminutaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 21.2]
athādhvaryuḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 22.1]
caturgṛhītamājyaṃ gṛhītvādhidevane hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya juhoty agniḥ pṛthur dharmaṇaspatir juṣāṇo agniḥ pṛthurdharmaṇaspatirājyasya vetu svāheti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 22.2]
athākṣānnivapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 23.1]
svāhākṛtāḥ sūryasya raśmibhiryatadhvaṃ sajātānām madhyameṣṭhyāyety eṣa vā agniḥ pṛthur yad adhidevanaṃ tasyaite 'ṅgārā yad akṣās tamevaitena prīṇāti tasya ha vā eṣānumatā gṛheṣu hanyate yo vā rājasūyena yajate yo vaitadevaṃ vedaiteṣvakṣeṣvāha gāṃ dīvyadhvamiti pūrvāgnivāhau dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 23.2]
athāhāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte 'nubrūhīti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 24.1]
tadyadantareṇāhutī etatkarma kriyata eṣa vai prajāpatirya eṣa yajñastāyate yasmādimāḥ prajāḥ prajātā etam v evāpyetarhyanu prajāyante tadenam madhyata evaitasya prajāpaterdadhāti madhyataḥ suvati tasmādantareṇāhutī etatkarma kriyata āśrāvyāhāgniṃ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajeti vaṣaṭkṛte juhoti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 24.2]
atheḍāmādadhāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 25.1]
upahūtāyām iḍāyām apa upaspṛśya māhendraṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇāti māhendraṃ grahaṃ gṛhītvā stotramupākaroti taṃ stotrāya pramīvati sa upāvarohati so 'nte stotrasya bhavatyante śastrasya | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 4 25.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 4, 5}
varuṇāddha vā abhiṣiṣicānādbhargo 'pacakrāma | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 1.1]
vīryaṃ vai bharga eṣa viṣṇuryajñaḥ so 'smādapacakrāma śaśvad ya eṣo 'pāṃ rasaḥ saṃbhṛto bhavati yenainametadabhiṣiñcati so 'sya bhargaṃ nirjaghāna | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 1.2]
tametābhirdevatābhir anusamasarpat | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 2.1]
savitrā prasavitrā sarasvatyā vācā tvaṣṭrā rūpaiḥ pūṣṇā paśubhirindreṇāsme bṛhaspatinā brahmaṇā varuṇenaujasāgninā tejasā somena rājñā viṣṇunaiva daśamyā devatayānvavindat | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 2.2]
tadyadenametābhirdevatābhiranusamasarpat | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 3.1]
tasmātsaṃsṛpo nāmātha yaddaśame 'hanprasuto bhavati tasmād daśapeyo 'tho yaddaśa daśaikaikaṃ camasamanuprasṛptā bhavanti tasmād v eva daśapeyaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 3.2]
tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 4.1]
daśa pitāmahāntsomapāntsakhyāya prasarpet tatho hāsya somapīthamaśnute daśapeyo hīti tadvai jyā dvau trīnityeva pitāmahāntsomapān vindanti tasmādetā eva devatāḥ saṃkhyāya prasarpet | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 4.2]
etābhirvai devatābhirvaruṇa etasya somapīthamāśnuta | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 5.1]
tatho evaiṣa etābhireva devatābhiretasya somapītham aśnute tasmādetā eva devatāḥ saṃkhyāya prasarpedatha yadaivaiṣodavasānīyeṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhata etasyābhiṣecanīyasya | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 5.2]
athaitāni havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 6.1]
sāvitraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vāṣṭākapālaṃ vā puroḍāśaṃ savitā vai devānām prasavitā savitṛprasūta eva tadvaruṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etatsavitṛprasūta evānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 6.2]
atha sārasvataṃ caruṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 7.1]
vāgvai sarasvatī vācaiva tadvaruṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etad vācaivānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 7.2]
atha tvāṣṭraṃ daśakapālam puroḍāśaṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 8.1]
tvaṣṭā vai rūpāṇāmīṣṭe tvaṣṭraiva tadrūpairvaruṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etattvaṣṭraiva rūpairanusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 8.2]
atha pauṣṇaṃ caruṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 9.1]
paśavo vai pūṣā paśubhireva tadvaruṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etatpaśubhir evānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 9.2]
athaindramekādaśakapālam puroḍāśaṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 10.1]
indriyaṃ vai vīryamindra indriyeṇaiva tadvīryeṇa varuṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etadindriyeṇaiva vīryeṇānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 10.2]
atha bārhaspatyaṃ caruṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 11.1]
brahma vai bṛhaspatirbrahmaṇaiva tadvaruṇo 'nusamasarpat tatho evaiṣa etad brahmaṇaivānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 11.2]
atha vāruṇaṃ yavamayaṃ caruṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 12.1]
sa yenaivaujasemāḥ prajā varuṇo 'gṛhṇāttenaiva tadojasā varuṇo 'nusamasarpat teno evaiṣa tadojasānusaṃsarpati tatraikam puṇḍarīkam prayacchati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 12.2]
upasado daśamyo devatāḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 13.1]
tatra pañca puṇḍarīkāṇyupaprayacchati tāṃ dvādaśapuṇḍarīkāṃ srajaṃ pratimuñcate sā dīkṣā tayā dīkṣayā dīkṣate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 13.2]
atha yaddvādaśa bhavanti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 14.1]
dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya sarvaṃ vai saṃvatsaraḥ sarveṇaivainam etad dīkṣayati yāni puṇḍarīkāṇi tāni divo rūpaṃ tāni nakṣatrāṇāṃ rūpaṃ ye vadhakāste 'ntarikṣasya rūpaṃ yāni bisāni tānyasyai tadenameṣu lokeṣvadhi dīkṣayati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 14.2]
atha rājānaṃ krītvā | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 15.1]
dvedhopanahya parivahanti tato 'rdhamāsandyāmāsādya pracaratyatha ya eṣo 'rdho brahmaṇo gṛhe nihito bhavati tamāsandyāmāsādyātithyena pracarati yadātithyena pracaratyathopasadbhiḥ pracarati yadopasadbhiḥ pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 15.2]
athaitāni havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 16.1]
āgneyamaṣṭākapālam puroḍāśaṃ saumyaṃ caruṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ trikapālaṃ vā puroḍāśaṃ caruṃ vā tena yatheṣṭyaivaṃ yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 16.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 17.1]
hvalati vā eṣa yo yajñapathādety eti vā eṣa yajñapathādya upasatpathādeti tasmādupasatpathādeva neyāt | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 17.2]
sa yadagniṃ yajati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 18.1]
agninaivaitattejasānusaṃsarpaty atha yatsomaṃ yajati somenaivaitadrājñānusaṃsarpaty atha yadviṣṇuṃ yajati yajño vai viṣṇustadyajñam pratyakṣamāpnoti tam pratyakṣamāptvātmankurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 18.2]
sa eṣa saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 19.1]
saptadaśo vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiryajñastadyajñam pratyakṣamāpnoti tam pratyakṣam āptvātman kurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 19.2]
tasya dvādaśa prathamagarbhāḥ paṣṭhauhyo dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 20.1]
dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiryajñastadyajñam pratyakṣamāpnoti tam pratyakṣamāptvātmankurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 20.2]
tāsāṃ dvādaśa garbhāḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 21.1]
tāścaturviṃśatiścaturviṃśatirvai saṃvatsarasyārdhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiryajñas tad yajñam pratyakṣamāpnoti tam pratyakṣamāptvātmankurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 21.2]
tā brahmaṇe dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 22.1]
brahmā hi yajñaṃ dakṣiṇato 'bhigopāyati tasmāttā brahmaṇe dadāti hiraṇmayīṃ srajam udgātre rukmaṃ hotre hiraṇmayau prākāśāvadhvaryubhyāmaśvam prastotre vaśām maitrāvaruṇāyarṣabham brāhmaṇācchaṃsine vāsasī neṣṭāpotṛbhyām anyataratoyuktaṃ yavācitamachāvākāya gāmagnīdhe | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 22.2]
tā vā etāḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 23.1]
dvādaśa vā trayodaśa vā dakṣiṇā bhavanti dvādaśa vā vai trayodaśa vā saṃvatsarasya māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiryajñastadyajñam pratyakṣamāpnoti tam pratyakṣamāptvātmankurute | [ŚBM, 5, 4, 5 23.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 5, 1}
āgneyo 'ṣṭākapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 1.1]
tam pūrvārdha āsādayaty aindra ekādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati saumyo vā carustaṃ dakṣiṇārdha āsādayati vaiśvadevaścarurbhavati tam paścārdha āsādayati maitrāvaruṇī payasyā bhavati tāmuttarārdha āsādayati bārhaspatyaścarurbhavati tam madhya āsādayatyeṣa caruḥ pañcabilas tad yat pañca havīṃṣi bhavanti teṣām pañca bilāni tasmāccaruḥ pañcabilo nāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 1.2]
tad yad etena rājasūyayājī yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 2.1]
yad evainaṃ diśaḥ samārohayati yad ṛtūn yat stomān yacchandāṃsi tasmādevainam etena niṣkrīṇāti sa yaddhaitena rājasūyayājī na yajetodvā ha mādyet pra vā patet tasmād vā etena rājasūyayājī yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 2.2]
sa yadāgneyenāṣṭākapālena puroḍāśena pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 3.1]
yad evainam prācīṃ diśaṃ samārohayati yad ṛtūn yat stomān yacchandāṃsi tasmādevainametena niṣkrīṇāti saṃsravam bārhaspatye carāvavanayati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 3.2]
atha yadaindreṇaikādaśakapālena puroḍāśena pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 4.1]
saumyena vā caruṇā yad evainaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśaṃ samārohayati yad ṛtūn yat stomān yacchandāṃsi tasmād evainametena niṣkrīṇāti saṃsravam bārhaspatye carāvavanayati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 4.2]
atha yad vaiśvadevena caruṇā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 5.1]
yad evainam pratīcīṃ diśaṃ samārohayati yadṛtūnyatstomānyacchandāṃsi tasmādevainametena niṣkrīṇāti saṃsravam bārhaspatye carāvavanayati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 5.2]
atha yanmaitrāvaruṇyā payasyayā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 6.1]
yad evainam udīcīṃ diśaṃ samārohayati yadṛtūnyatstomānyacchandāṃsi tasmādevainametena niṣkrīṇāti saṃsravam bārhaspatye carāvavanayati tadyatsaṃsravānbārhaspatye carāvavanayati sarvata evāsminnetadannādyaṃ dadhāti tasmād u diśo diśa eva rājñe 'nnādyamabhihriyate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 6.2]
atha yadbārhaspatyena caruṇā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 7.1]
yadevainamūrdhvāṃ diśaṃ samārohayati yadṛtūnyatstomānyacchandāṃsi tasmādevainametena niṣkrīṇāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 7.2]
sa ya eṣa āgneyo 'ṣṭākapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 8.1]
tasya hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇāgneyo vā eṣa yajño bhavaty agne reto hiraṇyaṃ tasmāddhiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇā tadagnīdhe dadāty agnir vā eṣa nidānena yad āgnīdhras tasmāt tad agnīdhe dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 8.2]
atha ya eṣa aindra ekādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 9.1]
tasyarṣabho dakṣiṇā sa haindro yadṛṣabho yady u saumyaś carur bhavati tasya babhrurgaurdakṣiṇā sa hi saumyo yad babhrus tam brahmaṇe dadāti brahmā hi yajñaṃ dakṣiṇato 'bhigopāyati tasmāttam brahmaṇe dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 9.2]
atha ya eṣa vaiśvadevaścarurbhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 10.1]
tasya pṛṣangaurdakṣiṇā bhūmā vā etad rūpāṇāṃ yat pṛṣato gor viśo vai viśve devā bhūmā vai viṭ tasmāt pṛṣan gaur dakṣiṇā taṃ hotre dadāti hotā hi bhūmā tasmāttaṃ hotre dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 10.2]
atha yaiṣā maitrāvaruṇī payasyā bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 11.1]
tasyai vaśā dakṣiṇā sā hi maitrāvaruṇī yad vaśā yadi vaśāṃ na vindedapi yaiva kā cāpravītā syāt sarvā hyeva vaśāpravītā tāmadhvaryubhyāṃ dadāti prāṇodānau vā adhvaryū prāṇodānau mitrāvaruṇau tasmāt tām adhvaryubhyāṃ dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 11.2]
atha ya eṣa bārhaspatyaścarurbhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 12.1]
tasya śitipṛṣṭho gaurdakṣiṇaiṣā vā ūrdhvā bṛhaspater dik tad eṣa upariṣṭādaryamṇaḥ panthās tasmācchitipṛṣṭho bārhaspatyasya dakṣiṇā tam brahmaṇe dadāti bṛhaspatirvai devānām brahmaiṣa vā etasya brahmā bhavati tasmāttam brahmaṇe dadāti sa haitenāpi viṣṭhāvrājyannādyakāmo yajeta tad asmint sarvato 'nnādyaṃ dadhāti sa hānnāda eva bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 1 12.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 5, 2}
sa vai prayujāṃ havirbhiryajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 1.1]
tadyatprayujāṃ havirbhiryajata ṛtūnvā etat suṣuvāṇo yuṅkte ta enamṛtavo yuktā vahanty ṛtūnvā prayuktānanucarati tasmātprayujāṃ havirbhiryajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 1.2]
tāni vai dvādaśa bhavanti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 2.1]
dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya tasmāddvādaśa bhavanti māsi māsi yajetetyāhuḥ ko veda manuṣyasya tasmānna māsi māsi yajeta śamyāparāvyādhe śamyāparāvyādha eva ṣaḍbhiryajate prāṅ yān atha punarāvṛttaḥ śamyāparāvyādhe śamyāparāvyādha eva ṣaḍbhiryajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 2.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 3.1]
ṣaḍevaitāni pūrvāṇi havīṃṣi nirvapati samānabarhīṃṣi tāsāṃ devatānāṃ rūpaṃ yathā śiśire yuktvā prāñca ā prāvṛṣaṃ yāyus tatṣaḍṛtūn yuṅkte ta enaṃ ṣaḍṛtavo yuktāḥ prāñca ā prāvṛṣaṃ vahanti ṣaḍvartūnprayuktānāprāvṛṣamanucarati pūrvāgnivāhāṃ dvau dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 3.2]
ṣaḍevottarāṇi havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 4.1]
samānabarhīṃṣi tāsāṃ devatānāṃ rūpaṃ yathā punarāvarteranvārṣikamabhi tatṣaḍṛtūnyuṅkte ta enaṃ ṣaḍṛtavo yuktā vārṣikamabhi vahanti ṣaḍvartūnprayuktānvārṣikamanucarati pūrvāgnivāhāṃ dvau dakṣiṇā tad yat pūrvāgnivāho dakṣiṇartūn vā etatsuṣuvāṇo yuṅkte vahanti vā anaḍvāhas tasmāt pūrvāgnivāho dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 4.2]
taddha smaitatpurā kurupañcālā āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 5.1]
ṛtavo vā asmānyuktā vahanty ṛtūnvā prayuktānanucarāma iti yadeṣāṃ rājāno rājasūyayājina āsustaddha sma tadabhyāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 5.2]
āgneyo 'ṣṭākapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 6.1]
saumyaścaruḥ sāvitro dvādaśakapālo vāṣṭākapālo vā puroḍāśo bārhaspatyaś carustvāṣṭro daśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo vaiśvānaro dvādaśakapāla etāni ṣaṭ pūrvāṇi havīṃṣi bhavanti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 6.2]
ṣaḍevottare caravaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 7.1]
sārasvataścaruḥ pauṣṇaścarur maitraścaruḥ kṣaitrapatyaścarur vāruṇaścarur ādityaścarur eta u ṣaḍuttare caravaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 7.2]
atha śyenīṃ vicitragarbhāmadityā ālabhate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 8.1]
tasyā eṣaivāvṛd yāṣṭāpadyai vaśāyā iyaṃ vā aditir asyā evainametadgarbhaṃ karoti tasyā etādṛśyeva śyenī vicitragarbhā dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 8.2]
atha pṛṣatīṃ vicitragarbhām marudbhya ālabhate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 9.1]
tasyā eṣaivāvṛd viśo vai maruto viśāmevainametadgarbhaṃ karoti tasyāṃ etādṛśyeva pṛṣatī vicitragarbhā dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 9.2]
etau paśubandhau | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 10.1]
tadetāveva santāvanyathevālabhante yāmadityā ālabhanta ādityebhyastāmālabhante sarvaṃ vā ādityāḥ sarvasyaivainametadgarbhaṃ karoti yām marudbhya ālabhante viśvebhyastāṃ devebhya ālabhante sarvaṃ vai viśve devāḥ sarvasyaivainametadgarbhaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 2 10.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 5, 3}
abhiṣecanīyeneṣṭvā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 1.1]
keśānna vapate tad yat keśān na vapate vīryaṃ vā etad apāṃ rasaḥ saṃbhṛto bhavati yenainam etad abhiṣiñcati tasyābhiṣiktasya keśān prathamān prāpnoti sa yat keśānvapetaitāṃ śriyam jihmāṃ vināśayed vyuduhyāt tasmāt keśān na vapate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 1.2]
saṃvatsaraṃ na vapate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 2.1]
saṃvatsarasaṃmitā vai vratacaryā tasmāt saṃvatsaraṃ na vapate sa eṣa vratavisarjanīyopayogo nāma stomo bhavati keśavapanīyaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 2.2]
tasyaikaviṃśam prātaḥsavanam | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 3.1]
saptadaśam mādhyandinaṃ savanam pañcadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sahokthaiḥ saha ṣoḍaśinā saha rātryā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 3.2]
trivṛdrāthantaraḥ saṃdhirbhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 4.1]
eṣa evaikaviṃśo ya eṣa tapati sa etasmād ekaviṃśād apayuṅkte sa saptadaśam abhipratyavaiti saptadaśāt pañcadaśam pañcadaśād asyāmeva trivṛti pratiṣṭhāyām pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 4.2]
tasya rathantaram pṛṣṭham bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 5.1]
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām evaitat pratiṣṭhāyām pratitiṣṭhaty atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā atirātras tasmādatirātro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 5.2]
sa vai nyeva vartayate keśānna vapate vīryaṃ vā etad apāṃ rasaḥ saṃbhṛto bhavati yenainametadabhiṣiñcati tasyābhiṣiktasya keśān prathamān prāpnoti sa yatkeśānvapetaitāṃ śriyaṃ jihmāṃ vināśayed vyuhyād atha yan nivartayate tadātmanyevaitāṃ śriyaṃ niyunakti tasmānnyeva vartayate keśānna vapate tasyaiṣaiva vratacaryā bhavati yāvajjīvaṃ nāsyām pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 6.1]
āsandyā upānahā upamuñcate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 7.1]
upānaḍbhyām adhi yad asya yānam bhavati ratho vā kiṃcidvā sarvaṃ vā eṣa idam uparyupari bhavaty arvāg evāsmād idaṃ sarvam bhavati yo rājasūyena yajate tasmādasyaiṣaiva vratacaryā bhavati yāvajjīvaṃ nāsyām pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 3 7.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 5, 4}
śyeta āśvino bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 1.1]
śyetāviva hyaśvināvavirmalhā sārasvatī bhavatyṛṣabhamindrāya sutrāmṇa ālabhate durvedā evaṃsamṛddhāḥ paśavo yadyevaṃsamṛddhānna vindedapyajānevālabheraṃste hi suśrapatarā bhavanti sa yadyajānālabheraṃllohita āśvino bhavati tadyadetayā yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 1.2]
tvaṣṭurha vai putraḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 2.1]
triśīrṣā ṣaḍakṣa āsa tasya trīṇyeva mukhānyāsustadyadevaṃrūpa āsa tasmādviśvarūpo nāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 2.2]
tasya somapānamevaikam mukhamāsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 3.1]
surāpāṇam ekam anyasmā aśanāyaikaṃ tamindro didveṣa tasya tāni śīrṣāṇi pracicheda | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 3.2]
sa yatsomapānamāsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 4.1]
tataḥ kapiñjalaḥ samabhavattasmātsa babhruka iva babhruriva hi somo rājā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 4.2]
atha yat surāpāṇam āsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 5.1]
tataḥ kalaviṅkaḥ samabhavattasmātso 'bhimādyatka iva vadaty abhimādyann iva hi surām pītvā vadati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 5.2]
atha yadatyasmā aśanāyāsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 6.1]
tatastittiriḥ samabhavattasmātsa viśvarūpatama iva santyeva ghṛtastokā iva tvan madhustokā iva tvat parṇeṣvāścutitā evaṃrūpamiva hi sa tenāśanamāvayat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 6.2]
sa tvaṣṭā cukrodha | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 7.1]
kuvinme putramavadhīditi so 'pendrameva somamājahre sa yathāyaṃ somaḥ prasuta evam apendra evāsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 7.2]
indro ha vā īkṣāṃcakre | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 8.1]
idaṃ vai mā somādantaryantīti sa yathā balīyān abalīyasa evam anupahūta eva yo droṇakalaśe śukra āsa tam bhakṣayāṃcakāra sa hainaṃ jihiṃsa so 'sya viṣvaṅṅeva prāṇebhyo dudrāva mukhāddhaivāsya na dudrāva tasmātprāyaścittirāsa sa yaddhāpi mukhād adroṣyan na haiva prāyaścittir abhaviṣyat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 8.2]
catvāro vai varṇāḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 9.1]
brāhmaṇo rājanyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro na haiteṣāmekaścana bhavati yaḥ somaṃ vamati sa yaddhaiteṣām ekaścit syāt syāddhaiva prāyaścittiḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 9.2]
sa yannasto 'dravat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 10.1]
tataḥ siṃhaḥ samabhavad atha yat karṇābhyām adravat tato vṛkaḥ samabhavad atha yadavācaḥ prāṇād adravat tataḥ śārdūlajyeṣṭhāḥ śvāpadāḥ samabhavann atha yaduttarātprāṇādadravatsā parisrud atha trirniraṣṭhīvattataḥ kuvalaṃ karkandhu badaramiti samabhavat sa sarveṇaiva vyārdhyata sarvaṃ hi somaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 10.2]
sa somātipūto maṅkuriva cacāra | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 11.1]
tametayāśvināvabhiṣajyatāṃ taṃ sarveṇaiva samārdhayatāṃ sarvaṃ hi somaḥ sa vasīyān eveṣṭvābhavat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 11.2]
te devā abruvan | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 12.1]
sutrātam batainam atrāsatām iti tasmātsautrāmaṇī nāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 12.2]
sa haitayāpi somātipūtam bhiṣajyet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 13.1]
sarveṇa vā eṣa vyṛdhyate yaṃ somo 'tipavate sarvaṃ hi somastaṃ sarveṇaiva samardhayati sarvaṃ hi somaḥ sa vasīyāneveṣṭvā bhavati tasmād u haitayāpi somātipūtam bhiṣajyet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 13.2]
tadyadetayā rājasūyayājī yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 14.1]
sarvānvā eṣa yajñakratūnavarunddhe sarvā iṣṭīrapi darvihomān yo rājasūyena yajate devasṛṣṭā vā eṣeṣṭir yat sautrāmaṇy anayā me 'pīṣṭamasadanayāpi sūyā iti tasmādvā etayā rājasūyayājī yajate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 14.2]
atha yadāśvino bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 15.1]
aśvinau vā enamabhiṣajyatāṃ tatho evainameṣa etadaśvibhyāmeva bhiṣajyati tasmād āśvino bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 15.2]
atha yatsārasvato bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 16.1]
vāgvai sarasvatī vācā vā enam aśvināvabhiṣajyatāṃ tatho evainameṣa etad vācaiva bhiṣajyati tasmātsārasvato bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 16.2]
atha yadaindro bhavati indro vai yajñasya devatā tayaivainametadbhiṣajyati tasmādaindro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 17.1]
eteṣu paśuṣu | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 18.1]
siṃhalomāni vṛkalomāni śārdūlalomānīty āvapaty etadvai tataḥ samabhavadyadenaṃ somo 'tyapavata tenaivainametatsamardhayati kṛtsnaṃ karoti tasmādetānyāvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 18.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 19.1]
ulkayā ha sa nakhinyā paśūn anuṣuvati ya etāni paśuṣvāvapati tasmād u parisrutyevāvapet tathā holkayā nakhinyā paśūn nānuṣuvati tatho evainaṃ samardhayati kṛtsnaṃ karoti tasmād u parisrutyevāvapet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 19.2]
atha pūrvedyuḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 20.1]
parisrutaṃ saṃdadhāty aśvibhyām pacyasva sarasvatyai pacyasvendrāya sutrāmṇe pacyasveti sā yadā parisrud bhavaty athainayā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 20.2]
dvāvagnī uddharanti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 21.1]
uttaravedāvevottaramuddhate dakṣiṇaṃ net somāhutīśca surāhutīśca saha juhavāmeti tasmād dvāvagnī uddharantyuttaravedāvevottaramuddhate dakṣiṇam atha yadā vapābhiḥ pracaratyathaitayā parisrutā pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 21.2]
tāṃ darbhaiḥ pāvayati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 22.1]
pūtāsaditi vāyuḥ pūtaḥ pavitreṇa pratyaṅ somo atisrutaḥ indrasya yujyaḥ sakheti tat kuvalasaktūn karkandhusaktūn badarasaktūn ity āvapaty etadvai tataḥ samabhavad yat trir niraṣṭhīvat tenaivainam etat samardhayati kṛtsnaṃ karoti tasmādetānāvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 22.2]
atha grahāngṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 23.1]
ekaṃ vā trīnvaikastveva grahītavya ekā hi purorug bhavaty ekānuvākyaikā yājyā tasmād eka eva grahītavyaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 23.2]
sa gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 24.1]
kuvidaṅga yavamanto yavaṃ cidyathā dāntyanupūrvaṃ viyūya ihehaiṣāṃ kṛṇuhi bhojanāni ye barhiṣo namauktiṃ yajanti upayāmagṛhīto 'sy aśvibhyāṃ tvā sarasvatyai tvendrāya tvā sutrāmṇa iti yady u trīn gṛhṇīyād etayaiva gṛhṇīyād upayāmais tu tarhi nānā gṛhṇīyād athāhāśvibhyām sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe 'nubrūhīti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 24.2]
so 'nvāha | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 25.1]
yuvaṃ surāmam aśvinā namucāvāsure sacā vipipānā śubhaspatī indraṃ karmasv āvatam ity āśrāvyāhāśvinau sarasvatīmindraṃ sutrāmāṇaṃ yajeti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 25.2]
sa yajati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 26.1]
putramiva pitarāv aśvinobhendrāvathuḥ kāvyairdaṃsanābhiḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 26.2]
yatsurāmaṃ vyapibaḥ śacībhiḥ sarasvatī tvā maghavannabhiṣṇagiti dvirhotā vaṣaṭkaroti dvir adhvaryurjuhoty āharati bhakṣaṃ yady u trīn gṛhṇīyādetasyaivānu homamitarau hūyete | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 26.3]
atha kumbhaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 27.1]
śatavitṛṇṇo vā bhavati navavitṛṇṇo vā sa yadi śatavitṛṇṇaḥ śatāyurvā ayam puruṣaḥ śatatejāḥ śatavīryas tasmācchatavitṛṇṇo yady u navavitṛṇṇo naveme puruṣe prāṇās tasmānnavavitṛṇṇaḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 27.2]
taṃ śikyodutam | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 28.1]
uparyuparyāhavanīyaṃ dhārayanti sā yā pariśiṣṭā parisrudbhavati tāmāsiñcati tāṃ vikṣarantīmupatiṣṭhate pitṝṇāṃ somavatāṃ tisṛbhirṛgbhiḥ pitṝṇām barhiṣadāṃ tisṛbhirṛgbhiḥ pitṝṇām agniṣvāttānāṃ tisṛbhir ṛgbhis tad yad evam upatiṣṭhate yatra vai soma indramatyapavata sa yat pitṝn agacchat trayā vai pitaras tenaivainam etat samardhayati kṛtsnaṃ karoti tasmād evamupatiṣṭhate | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 28.2]
athaitāni havīṃṣi nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 29.1]
sāvitraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vāṣṭākapālaṃ vā puroḍāśaṃ vāruṇaṃ yavamayaṃ carum aindram ekādaśakapālam puroḍāśam | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 29.2]
sa yatsāvitro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 30.1]
savitā vai devānām prasavitā savitṛprasūta evaitadbhiṣajyati tasmātsāvitro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 30.2]
atha yadvāruṇo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 31.1]
varuṇo vā ārpayitā tadya evārpayitā tenaivaitadbhiṣajyati tasmādvāruṇo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 31.2]
atha yadaindro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 32.1]
indro vai yajñasya devatā sā yaiva yajñasya devatā tayaivaitadbhiṣajyati tasmādaindro bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 32.2]
sa yadi haitayāpi somātipūtam bhiṣajyet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 33.1]
iṣṭā anuyājā bhavanty avyūḍhe srucāv athaitair havirbhiḥ pracarati paścādvai somo 'tipavate paścādevainametena medhenāpidadhāty āśvinam u tarhi dvikapālam puroḍāśaṃ nirvaped atha yadā vapābhiḥ pracaraty athaitenāśvinena dvikapālena puroḍāśena pracarati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 33.2]
tad u tathā na kuryāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 34.1]
hvalati vā eṣa yo yajñapathād ety eti vā eṣa yajñapathādya evaṃ karoti tasmād yatraivaiteṣām paśūnāṃ vapābhiḥ pracaranti tadevaitairhavirbhiḥ pracareyur no tarhyāśvinaṃ dvikapālam puroḍāśaṃ nirvapet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 34.2]
tasya napuṃsako gaurdakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 35.1]
na vā eṣa strī na pumānyannapuṃsako gaur yad aha pumāṃstena na strī yad u strī teno na pumāṃs tasmānnapuṃsako gaur dakṣiṇāśvā vā rathavāhī sā hi na strī na pumān yad aśvā rathavāhī yadaha ratham vahati tena na strī yad u strī teno na pumāṃs tasmād aśvā rathavāhī dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 4 35.2]
{ŚBM, 5, 5, 5}
aindravaiṣṇavaṃ dvādaśakapālam puroḍāśaṃ nirvapati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 1.1]
tadyadetayā yajate vṛtre ha vā idamagre sarvam āsa yad ṛco yad yajūṃṣi yat sāmāni tasmā indro vajram prājihīrṣat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 1.2]
sa ha viṣṇumuvāca | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 2.1]
vṛtrāya vai vajram prahariṣyāmy anu mā tiṣṭhasveti tatheti ha viṣṇur uvācānu tvā sthāsye prahareti tasmā indro vajramudyayāma sa udyatādvajrādvṛtro bibhayāṃcakāra | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 2.2]
sa hovāca | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 3.1]
asti vā idaṃ vīryaṃ tannu te prayacchāni mā tu me prahārṣīriti tasmai yajūṃṣi prāyacchat tasmai dvitīyamudyayāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 3.2]
sa hovāca | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 4.1]
asti vā idaṃ vīryaṃ tan nu te prayacchāni mā tu me prahārṣīr iti tasmā ṛcaḥ prāyacchat tasmai tṛtīyamudyayāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 4.2]
asti vā idaṃ vīryaṃ tannu te prayacchāni mā tu me prahārṣīr iti tasmai sāmāni prāyacchat tasmād apy etarhy evam evaitairvedair yajñaṃ tanvate yajurbhir evāgre 'thargbhir atha sāmabhir evaṃ hyasmā etat prāyacchat | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 5.1]
tasya yo yonir āśaya āsa | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 6.1]
tam anuparāmṛśya saṃlupyāchinat saiṣeṣṭir abhavat tad yad etasminnāśaye tridhāturivaiṣā vidyāśeta tasmāttraidhātavī nāma | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 6.2]
atha yadaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ havirbhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 7.1]
indro hi vajram udayacchad viṣṇuranvatiṣṭhata | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 7.2]
atha yaddvādaśakapālo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 8.1]
dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsarasya saṃvatsarasaṃmitaiṣeṣṭis tasmād dvādaśakapālo bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 8.2]
tamubhayeṣāṃ vrīhiyavāṇāṃ gṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 9.1]
vrīhimayamevāgre piṇḍamadhiśrayati tadyajuṣāṃ rūpam atha yavamayaṃ tad ṛcāṃ rūpamatha vrīhimayaṃ tatsāmnāṃ rūpaṃ tad etat trayyai vidyāyai rūpaṃ kriyate saiṣā rājasūyayājina udavasānīyeṣṭirbhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 9.2]
sarvānvā eṣa yajñakratūnavarunddhe | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 10.1]
sarvā iṣṭīrapi darvihomānyo rājasūyena yajate tasya yātayāmeva yajño bhavati so 'smāt parāṅiva bhavaty etāvānvai sarvo yajño yāvāneṣa trayo vedas tasyaitadrūpaṃ kriyata eṣa yonirāśayas tad etena trayeṇa vedena punaryajñamārabhate tathāsyāyātayāmā yajño bhavati tatho asmānna parāṅ bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 10.2]
sarvānvā eṣa yajñakratūnavarunddhe | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 11.1]
sarvā iṣṭīrapi darvihomānyo rājasūyena yajate devasṛṣṭo vā eṣeṣṭir yat traidhātavy anayā me 'pīṣṭamasadanayāpi sūyā iti tasmādvā eṣā rājasūyayājina udavasānīyeṣṭir bhavati | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 11.2]
atho yaḥ sahasraṃ vā bhūyo vā dadyāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 12.1]
tasya hāpyudavasānīyā syād riricāna iva vā eṣa bhavati yaḥ sahasraṃ vā bhūyo vā dadāty etad vai sahasraṃ vācaḥ prajātaṃ yadeṣa trayo vedas tat sahasreṇa riricānam punarāpyāyayati tasmād u ha tasyāpyudavasānīyā syāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 12.2]
atho ye dīrghasattramāsīran | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 13.1]
saṃvatsaraṃ vā bhūyo vā teṣāṃ hāpyudavasānīyā syāt sarvaṃ vai teṣām āptaṃ bhavati sarvaṃ jitaṃ ye dīrghasattramāsate saṃvatsaraṃ vā bhūyo vā sarvameṣā tasmād u ha teṣāmapyudavasānīyā syāt | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 13.2]
atho hainayāpyabhicaret | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 14.1]
etayā vai bhadrasenam ājātaśatravam āruṇirabhicacāra kṣipraṃ kilāstṛṇuteti ha smāha yājñavalkyo 'pi ha vā enayendro vṛtrasyāsthānamachinad api ha vā enayāsthānaṃ chinatti ya enayābhicarati tasmād u hainayāpyabhicaret | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 14.2]
atho hainayāpi bhiṣajyet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 15.1]
yaṃ nvevaikayarcā bhiṣajyed ekena yajuṣaikena sāmnā taṃ nvevāgadaṃ kuryāt kim u yaṃ trayeṇa vedena tasmād u hainayāpi bhiṣajyet | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 15.2]
tasyai trīṇi śatamānāni hiraṇyāni dakṣiṇā | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 16.1]
tāni brahmaṇe dadāti na vai brahmā pracarati na stute na śaṃsaty atha sa yaśo na vai hiraṇyena kiṃcana kurvanty atha tad yaśas tasmāttrīṇi śatamānāni brahmaṇe dadāti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 16.2]
tisro dhenūrhotre | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 17.1]
bhūmā vai tisro dhenavo bhūmā hotā tasmāttisro dhenūrhotre | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 17.2]
trīṇi vāsāṃsyadhvaryave | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 18.1]
tanute vā adhvaryuryajñaṃ tanvate vāsāṃsi tasmāttrīṇi vāsāṃsyadhvaryave gām agnīdhe | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 18.2]
tā vā etāḥ | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 19.1]
dvādaśa vā trayodaśa vā dakṣiṇā bhavanti dvādaśa vā vai trayodaśa vā saṃvatsarasya māsāḥ saṃvatsarasaṃmitaiṣeṣṭis tasmād dvādaśa vā trayodaśa vā dakṣiṇā bhavanti | [ŚBM, 5, 5, 5 19.2]

sa | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494124_1]

te etān sapta puruṣān ekam puruṣam akurvan | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494127_1]

atha yā eteṣām saptānām puruṣāṇām śrīḥ yaḥ rasaḥ āsīt tam ūrdhvam samudauhan tat asya śiraḥ abhavat | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494129_1]
yat śriyam samudauhan tasmāt śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494129_2]
tasmin etasmin prāṇāḥ aśrayanta | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494129_3]
tasmāt vā iva etat śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494129_4]

saḥ eva puruṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ abhavat | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494130_1]

sa vai sapta puruṣaḥ bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494132_1]

parokṣa kāmāḥ hi devāḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 1, 1 494142_7]
