atha vaikaṅkatīm ādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 1.1]
prajāpatir yām prathamām āhutimajuhot sa hutvā yatra nyamṛṣṭa tato vikaṅkataḥ samabhavat saiṣā prathamāhutir yad vikaṅkatas tām asminnetajjuhoti tayainam etat prīṇāti parasyā adhi saṃvato 'varāṃ abhyātara yatrāhamasmi tāṃ aveti yathaiva yajustathā bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 1.2]
athaudumbarīmādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 2.1]
devāścāsurāścobhaye prājāpatyā aspardhanta te ha sarva eva vanaspatayo 'surānabhyupeyur udumbaro haiva devānna jahau te devā asurānjitvā teṣāṃ vanaspatīnavṛñjata | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 2.2]
te hocuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 3.1]
hanta yaiṣu vanaspatiṣūrg yo rasa udumbare taṃ dadhāma te yady apakrāmeyur yātayāmā apakrāmeyur yathā dhenur dugdhā yathānaḍvān ūhivāniti tad yaiṣu vanaspatiṣūrg yo rasa āsīd udumbare tam adadhus tayaitad ūrjā sarvān vanaspatīn prati pacyate tasmāt sa sarvadārdraḥ sarvadā kṣīrī tad etat sarvam annaṃ yad udumbaraḥ sarve vanaspatayaḥ sarveṇaivainam etad annena prīṇāti sarvairvanaspatibhiḥ saminddhe | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 3.2]
paramasyāḥ parāvata iti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 4.1]
yā paramā parāvad ity etad rohidaśva ihāgahīti rohito hāgneraśvaḥ purīṣyaḥ purupriya iti paśavyo bahupriya ity etad agne tvaṃ tarā mṛdha ity agne tvaṃ tara sarvānpāpmana ityetat | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 4.2]
athāparaśuvṛkṇam ādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 5.1]
jāyata eṣa etadyaccīyate sa eṣa sarvasmā annāya jāyata etad v ekamannaṃ yad aparaśuvṛkṇaṃ tenainam etat prīṇāti yadagne kāni kāni cid ā te dārūṇi dadhmasi sarvaṃ tadastu te ghṛtaṃ tajjuṣasva yaviṣṭhyeti yathaiva yajus tathā bandhus tad yat kiṃ cāparaśuvṛkṇaṃ tad asmā etat svadayati tad asmā annaṃ kṛtvāpidadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 5.2]
athādhaḥśayam ādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 6.1]
jāyata eṣa etad yaccīyate sa eṣa sarvasmā annāya jāyata etad v ekam annaṃ yad adhaḥśayaṃ tenainam etat prīṇāti yad atty upajihvikā yad vamro atisarpatīty upajihvikā vā hi tad atti vamro vātisarpati sarvaṃ tad astu te ghṛtaṃ tajjuṣasva yaviṣṭhyeti yathaiva yajus tathā bandhus tad yat kiṃ cādhaḥśayaṃ tad asmā etat svadayati tad asmā annaṃ kṛtvāpidadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 6.2]
athaitā uttarāḥ pālāśyo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 7.1]
brahma vai palāśo brahmaṇaivainam etat saminddhe yad v eva pālāśyaḥ somo vai palāśa eṣo ha paramāhutir yat somāhutis tām asminn etajjuhoti tayainam etat prīṇāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 7.2]
ahar ahar aprayāvam bharanta iti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 8.1]
ahar ahar amattā āharanta ity etad aśvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsamasmā iti yathāśvāya tiṣṭhate ghāsam ity etad rāyaspoṣeṇa sam iṣā madanta iti rayyā ca poṣeṇa ca samiṣā madanta ity etad agne mā te prativeśā riṣāmeti yathaivāsya prativeśo na riṣyed evam etad āha | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 8.2]
nābhā pṛthivyāḥ samidhāne agnāviti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 9.1]
eṣā ha nābhiḥ pṛthivyai yatraiṣa etat samidhyate rāyaspoṣāya bṛhate havāmaha iti rayyai ca poṣāya ca bṛhate havāmaha ity etad irammadam itīrayā hyeṣa matto bṛhad uktham iti bṛhaduktho hyeṣa yajatram iti yajñiyam ity etaj jetāram agnim pṛtanāsu sāsahimiti jetā hyagniḥ pṛtanā u sāsahiḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 9.2]
yāḥ senā abhītvarīḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 10.1]
daṃṣṭrābhyām malimlūnye janeṣu malimlavo yo asmabhyam arātīyād yaśca no dveṣate janaḥ nindād yo asmān dhipsācca sarvaṃ tam masmasā kurviti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 10.2]
etad vai devāḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 11.1]
yaś cainānadveḍyaṃ cādviṣus tam asmā annaṃ kṛtvāpyadadhus tenainam aprīṇann annam ahaitasyābhavad adahad u devānām pāpmānaṃ tathaivaitad yajamāno yaś cainaṃ dveṣṭi yaṃ ca dveṣṭi tam asmā annaṃ kṛtvāpidadhāti tenainam prīṇāty annam ahaitasya bhavati dahaty u yajamānasya pāpmānam | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 11.2]
tā etā ekādaśādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 12.1]
akṣatriyasya vāpurohitasya vāsarvaṃ vai tad yad ekādaśāsarvaṃ tad yad akṣatriyo vāpurohito vā | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 12.2]
dvādaśa kṣatriyasya vā purohitasya vā | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 13.1]
sarvaṃ vai tadyaddvādaśa sarvaṃ tad yat kṣatriyo vā purohito vā | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 13.2]
sa purohitasyādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 14.1]
saṃśitam me brahma saṃśitaṃ vīryam balam saṃśitaṃ kṣatraṃ jiṣṇu yasyāhamasmi purohita iti tadasya brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca saṃśyati | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 14.2]
atha kṣatriyasya | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 15.1]
ud eṣām bāhū atiram ud varco atho balam kṣiṇomi brahmaṇāmitrānunnayāmi svāṁ ahamiti yathaiva kṣiṇuyād amitrān unnayet svān evametad āhobhe tv evaite ādadhyād ayaṃ vā agnirbrahma ca kṣatraṃ cemamevaitadagnimetābhyāmubhābhyāṃ saminddhe brahmaṇā ca kṣatreṇa ca | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 15.2]
tāstrayodaśa sampadyante | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 16.1]
trayodaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaro 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvataivainametadannena prīṇāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 16.2]
prādeśamātryo bhavanti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 17.1]
prādeśamātro vai garbho viṣṇur annam etad ātmasaṃmitenaivainam etad annena prīṇāti yad u vā ātmasaṃmitam annaṃ tadavati tanna hinasti yadbhūyo hinasti tad yat kanīyo na tadavati tiṣṭhannādadhāti tasyopari bandhuḥ svāhākāreṇa reto vā idaṃ siktamayam agnis tasmin yat kāṣṭhāny asvāhākṛtāny abhyādadhyāddhiṃsyāddhainaṃ tā yat samidhastena nāhutayo yad u svāhākāreṇa tenānnam annaṃ hi svāhākāras tatho hainaṃ na hinasti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 3 17.2]
{ŚBM, 6, 6, 4}
atha viṣṇukramān krāntvā | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 1.1]
vātsapreṇopasthāyāstamita āditye bhasmaiva prathamam udvapaty etad vā enam etenānnena prīṇāty etābhiḥ samidbhis tasyānnasya jagdhasyaiṣa pāpmā sīdati bhasma tenainam etad vyāvartayati tasminn apahatapāpman vācaṃ visṛjate vācaṃ visṛjya samidham ādadhāti rātryā evainam etad annena prīṇāti rātrīṃ rātrīm aprayāvam bharanta iti tasyokto bandhū rātryā evaitām ariṣṭiṃ svastim āśāste tad yat kiṃ cāto rātryopasamādadhāty āhutikṛtaṃ haivāsmai tad upasamādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 1.2]
atha prātarudita āditye | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 2.1]
bhasmaiva prathamam udvapaty etad vā enam etenānnena prīṇāty etayā samidhā yacca rātryopasamādadhāti tasyānnasya jagdhasyaiṣa pāpmā sīdati bhasma tenainam etad vyāvartayati tasminn apahatapāpman vācaṃ visṛjate vācaṃ visṛjya samidham ādadhāty ahna evainam etad annena prīṇāty aharahar aprayāvam bharanta iti tasyokto bandhur ahna evaitām ariṣṭiṃ svastim āśāste tad yat kiṃ cāto 'hnopasamādadhāty āhutikṛtaṃ haivāsmai tadupasamādadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 2.2]
ahorātre vā abhivartamāne saṃvatsaram āpnutaḥ saṃvatsara idaṃ sarvam āhnāyaivaitām ariṣṭiṃ svastimāśāste | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 3.1]
atha yadāsmai vratam prayacchanti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 4.1]
atha vrate nyajya samidhamādadhāti na vrate nyañjyād ity u haika āhur āhutiṃ tajjuhuyād anavakﾱptaṃ vai tadyaddīkṣita āhutiṃ juhuyāditi | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 4.2]
sa vai nyañjyādeva | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 5.1]
daivo vā asyaiṣa ātmā mānuṣo 'yaṃ sa yanna nyañjyān na haitaṃ daivam ātmānam prīṇīyād atha yan nyanakti tatho haitaṃ daivam ātmānam prīṇāti sā yat samittena nāhutir yad u vrate nyaktā tenānnam annaṃ hi vratam | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 5.2]
sa vai samidham ādhāyātha vratayati | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 6.1]
daivo vā asyaiṣa ātmā mānuṣo 'yaṃ devā u vā agre 'tha manuṣyās tasmāt samidhamādhāyātha vratayati | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 6.2]
annapate 'nnasya no dehīti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 7.1]
aśanapate 'śanasya no dehīty etad anamīvasya śuṣmiṇa ity anaśanāyasya śuṣmiṇa ity etat pra pra dātāraṃ tāriṣa iti yajamāno vai dātā pra yajamānaṃ tāriṣa ity etad ūrjaṃ dhehi dvipade catuṣpada ity āśiṣam āśāste yad u bhinnāyai prāyaścittim āhottarasmiṃstad anvākhyāna iti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 7.2]
yady eṣokhā bhidyeta | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 8.1]
yābhinnā navā sthāly urubilī syāt tasyām enam paryāvaped ārcchati vā eṣokhā yā bhidyate 'nārto iyaṃ devatānārtāyām imam anārtam bibharāṇīti tatrokhāyai kapālam purastāt prāsyati tatho haiṣa etasyai yonerna cyavate | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 8.2]
atha mṛdam āhṛtya | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 9.1]
ukhāṃ copaśayāṃ ca piṣṭvā saṃsṛjyokhāṃ karoty etayaivāvṛtānupaharan yajus tūṣṇīm eva paktvā paryāvapati karmaṇireva tatra prāyaścittiḥ punas tat kapālam ukhāyām upasamasyokhāṃ copaśayāṃ ca piṣṭvā saṃsṛjya nidadhāti prāyaścittibhyaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 9.2]
atha yadyeṣa ukhyo 'gnir anugacchet | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 10.1]
gārhapatyaṃ vāva sa gacchati gārhapatyāddhi sa āhṛto bhavati gārhapatyād evainam prāñcam uddhṛtyopasamādhāyokhām pravṛñjyād etayaivāvṛtānupaharan yajus tūṣṇīm eva tāṃ yadāgnir ārohati | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 10.2]
atha prāyaścittī karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 11.1]
sarvebhyo vā eṣa etaṃ kāmebhya ādhatte tad yad evāsyātra kāmānāṃ vyavacchidyate 'gnāvanugate tadevaitatsaṃtanoti saṃdadhāty ubhe prāyaścittī karoty adhvaraprāyaścittiṃ cāgniprāyaścittiṃ cādhvarasya pūrvām athāgnes tasyokto bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 11.2]
sa samidhājyasyopahatya | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 12.1]
āsīna āhutiṃ juhoti viśvakarmaṇe svāhety athopotthāya samidham ādadhāti punastvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ samindhatām punarbrahmāṇo vasunītha yajñair ity etāstvā devatāḥ punaḥ samindhatām ity etad ghṛtena tvaṃ tanvaṃ vardhayasva satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmā iti ghṛtenāha tvaṃ vardhayasva yebhya u tvāṃ kāmebhyo yajamāna ādhatta te 'sya sarve satyāḥ santvityetat | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 12.2]
atha yadi gārhapatyo 'nugacchet | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 13.1]
araṇī vāva sa gacchaty araṇibhyāṃ hi sa āhṛto bhavaty araṇibhyām evainam mathitvopasamādhāya prāyaścittī karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 13.2]
atha yadi prasuta āhavanīyo 'nugacchet | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 14.1]
gārhapatyaṃ vāva sa gacchati gārhapatyāddhi sa āhṛto bhavati gārhapatyādevainam prāñcaṃ sāṃkāśinena hṛtvopasamādhāya prāyaścittī karoti yas tasmin kāle 'dhvaraḥ syāt tām adhvaraprāyaścittiṃ kuryāt samānyagniprāyaścittiḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 14.2]
atha yadyāgnīdhrīyo 'nugacchet | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 15.1]
gārhapatyaṃ vāva sa gacchati gārhapatyāddhi sa āhṛto bhavati gārhapatyād evainam prāñcamuttareṇa sado hṛtvopasamādhāya prāyaścittī karoty atha yadi gārhapatyo 'nugacchet tasyokto bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 6, 4 15.2]
{ŚBM, 6, 7, 1}
rukmam pratimucya bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 1.1]
satyaṃ haitad yad rukmaḥ satyaṃ vā etaṃ yantum arhati satyenaitaṃ devā abibharuḥ satyenaivainam etad bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 1.2]
tadyattatsatyam | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 2.1]
asau sa ādityaḥ sa hiraṇmayo bhavati jyotirvai hiraṇyaṃ jyotir eṣo 'mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛtam eṣa parimaṇḍalo bhavati parimaṇḍalo hyeṣa ekaviṃśatinirbādha ekaviṃśo hyeṣa bahiṣṭān nirbādham bibharti raśmayo vā etasya nirbādhā bāhyata u vā etasya raśmayaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 2.2]
yad v eva rukmam pratimucya bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 3.1]
asau vā āditya eṣa rukmo no haitam agnim manuṣyo manuṣyarūpeṇa yantum arhaty etenaiva rūpeṇaitad rūpam bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 3.2]
yad v eva rukmam pratimucya bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 4.1]
reto vā idaṃ siktam ayam agnis tejo vīryaṃ rukmo 'smiṃs tad retasi tejo vīryaṃ dadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 4.2]
yad eva rukmam pratimucya bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 5.1]
etadvai devā abibhayuryadvai na imam iha rakṣāṃsi nāṣṭrā na hanyur iti tasmā etam antikād goptāram akurvann amum evādityam asau vā āditya eṣa rukmas tathaivāsmā ayam etam antikād goptāraṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 5.2]
kṛṣṇājine niṣyūto bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 6.1]
yajño vai kṛṣṇājinaṃ yajño vā etaṃ yantum arhati yajñenaitaṃ devā abibharur yajñenaivaitam etad bibharti lomataś chandāṃsi vai lomāni chandāṃsi vā etaṃ yantum arhanti chandobhir etaṃ devā abibharuś chandobhir evainam etad bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 6.2]
abhi śuklāni ca kṛṣṇāni ca lomāni niṣyūto bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 7.1]
ṛksāmayor haite rūpe ṛksāme vā etaṃ yantum arhata ṛksāmābhyām etaṃ devā abibharur ṛksāmābhyām evainam etad bibharti śāṇo rukmapāśas trivṛt tasyokto bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 7.2]
tam uparinābhi bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 8.1]
asau vā āditya eṣa rukma uparinābhy u vā eṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 8.2]
yad v evoparinābhi | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 9.1]
avāgvai nābhe retaḥ prajātis tejo vīryaṃ rukmo nenme retaḥ prajātiṃ tejo vīryaṃ rukmaḥ pradahād iti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 9.2]
yad v evoparinābhi | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 10.1]
etadvai paśor medhyataraṃ yad uparinābhi purīṣasaṃhitataraṃ yad avāṅnābhes tad yad eva paśor medhyataraṃ tenainam etad bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 10.2]
yad v evoparinābhi | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 11.1]
yad vai prāṇasyāmṛtam ūrdhvaṃ tannābher ūrdhvaiḥ prāṇair uccaraty atha yan martyam parāk tan nābhim atyeti tad yad eva prāṇasyāmṛtaṃ tad enam etad abhisaṃpādayati tenainam etadbibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 11.2]
athainam āsandyā bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 12.1]
iyaṃ vā āsandyasyāṃ hīdaṃ sarvam āsannam iyaṃ vā etaṃ yantum arhaty anayaitaṃ devā abibharur anayaivainam etad bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 12.2]
audumbarī bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 13.1]
ūrg vai rasa udumbara ūrjaivainam etad rasena bibharty atho sarva ete vanaspatayo yad udumbaraḥ sarve vā etaṃ vanaspatayo yantum arhanti sarvair etaṃ vanaspatibhir devā abibharuḥ sarvair evainam etad vanaspatibhir bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 13.2]
prādeśamātry ūrdhvā bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 14.1]
prādeśamātro vai garbho viṣṇur yonir eṣā garbhasaṃmitāṃ tad yoniṃ karoty aratnimātrī tiraścī bāhur vā aratnir bāhuno vai vīryaṃ kriyate vīryasaṃmitaiva tad bhavati vīryaṃ vā etaṃ yantum arhati vīryeṇaitaṃ devā abibharur vīryeṇaivainam etad bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 14.2]
catuḥsraktayaḥ pādā bhavanti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 15.1]
catuḥsraktīnyanūcyāni catasro vai diśo diśo vā etaṃ yantum arhanti digbhir etaṃ devā abibharur digbhir evainam etad bibharti mauñjībhī rajjubhir vyutā bhavati trivṛdbhis tasyokto bandhur mṛdā digdhā tasyo evokto 'tho anatidāhāya | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 15.2]
athainaṃ śikyena bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 16.1]
ime vai lokā eṣo 'gnir diśaḥ śikyaṃ digbhir hīme lokāḥ śaknuvanti sthātuṃ yacchaknuvanti tasmācchikyaṃ digbhir evainam etad bibharti ṣaḍudyāmam bhavati ṣaḍḍhi diśo mauñjaṃ trivṛt tasyokto bandhur mṛdā digdhaṃ tasyo evokto 'tho anatidāhāya | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 16.2]
tasyāpa eva pratiṣṭhā | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 17.1]
apsu hīme lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitā āditya āsañjanam āditye hīme lokā digbhir āsaktāḥ sa yo haitad evaṃ vedaitenaiva rūpeṇaitad rūpam bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 17.2]
yad v evainaṃ śikyena bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 18.1]
saṃvatsara eṣo 'gnirṛtavaḥ śikyam ṛtubhir hi saṃvatsaraḥ śaknoti sthātuṃ yacchaknoti tasmācchikyam ṛtubhir evainam etad bibharti ṣaḍudyāmam bhavati ṣaḍḍhyṛtavaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 18.2]
tasyāhorātre eva pratiṣṭhā | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 19.1]
ahorātrayor hyayaṃ saṃvatsaraḥ pratiṣṭhitaś candramā āsañjanaṃ candramasi hyayaṃ saṃvatsara ṛtubhir āsaktaḥ sa yo haitadevaṃ vedaitenaiva rūpeṇaitad rūpam bibharti tasya ha vā eṣa saṃvatsarabhṛto bhavati ya evaṃ veda saṃvatsaropāsito haiva tasya bhavati ya evaṃ na vedety adhidevatam | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 19.2]
athādhyātmam | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 20.1]
ātmaivāgniḥ prāṇāḥ śikyam prāṇair hyayam ātmā śaknoti sthātuṃ yacchaknoti tasmācchikyaṃ prāṇair evainam etad bibharti ṣaḍudyāmam bhavati ṣaḍḍhi prāṇāḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 20.2]
tasya mana eva pratiṣṭhā | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 21.1]
manasi hyayamātmā pratiṣṭhito 'nnam āsañjanam anne hyayamātmā prāṇair āsaktaḥ sa yo haitad evaṃ vedaitenaiva rūpeṇaitad rūpam bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 21.2]
athainam ukhayā bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 22.1]
ime vai lokā ukheme vā etaṃ lokā yantum arhanty ebhiretaṃ lokair devā abibharur ebhir evainam etallokair bibharti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 22.2]
sā yad ukhā nāma | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 23.1]
etad vai devā etena karmaṇaitayāvṛtemāṃl lokān udakhanan yad udakhanaṃs tasmād utkhotkhā ha vai tām ukhety ācakṣate parokṣam parokṣakāmā hi devāḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 23.2]
tad vā ukheti dve akṣare | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 24.1]
dvipād yajamāno yajamāno 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvataivainam etad bibharti so eva kumbhī sā sthālī tat ṣaṭ ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaro 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvat tad bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 24.2]
athainam iṇḍvābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 25.1]
asau vā āditya eṣo 'gnir ahorātre iṇḍve amuṃ tad ādityam ahorātrābhyām parigṛhṇāti tasmād eṣo 'horātrābhyām parigṛhītaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 25.2]
yad v evainam iṇḍvābhyām parigṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 26.1]
asau vā āditya eṣo 'gnir imā u lokāv iṇḍve amum tad ādityam ābhyāṃ lokābhyām parigṛhṇāti tasmād eṣa ābhyāṃ lokābhyām parigṛhītaḥ parimaṇḍale bhavataḥ parimaṇḍalau hīmau lokau mauñje trivṛtī tasyokto bandhur mṛdā digdhe tasyo evokto 'tho anatidāhāya | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 26.2]
athātaḥ sampad eva | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 27.1]
āsandī cokhā ca śikyaṃ ca rukmapāśaś cāgniś ca rukmaśca tat ṣaṭ ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaro 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvat tad bhavatīṇḍve tad aṣṭāv aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī gāyatro 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvat tad bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 27.2]
atha sarvasampat | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 28.1]
catvāraḥ pādāś catvāry anūcyāni śikyaṃ ca rukmapāśaśca yad u kiṃ ca rajjavyaṃ śikyaṃ tad anūkhāgnī rukmas tat trayodaśa trayodaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaro 'gnir yāvān agnir yāvatyasya mātrā tāvat tad bhavati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 1 28.2]
{ŚBM, 6, 7, 2}
taṃ tiṣṭhan pratimuñcate | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 1.1]
asau vā āditya eṣa rukmaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 1.2]
tiṣṭhatīva vā asāvādityaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 1.3]
atho tiṣṭhan vai vīryavattara udaṅ prāṅ tiṣṭhan | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 1.4]
tasyokto bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 1.5]
dṛśāno rukma urvyā vyadyaud iti dṛśyamāno hy eṣa rukma urvyā vidyotate | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 2.1]
durmarṣam āyuḥ śriye rucāna iti durmaraṃ vā etasyāyuḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 2.2]
śriyo eṣa rocate | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 2.3]
agnir amṛto abhavad vayobhir iti sarvair vā eṣa vayobhir amṛto 'bhavad yad enaṃ dyaur ajanayad iti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 2.4]
dyaur vā etam ajanayat suretā iti suretā hy eṣā yasyā eṣa retaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 2.5]
athainam iṇḍvābhyām parigṛhṇāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.1]
naktoṣāsā samanasā virūpe ity ahorātre vai naktoṣāsā samanasā virūpe | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.2]
dhāpayete śiśum ekaṃ samīcī iti yad vai kiṃ cāhorātrayos tenaitam eva samīcī dhāpayete | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.3]
dyāvākṣāmā rukmo antar vibhātīti harann etad yajur japati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.4]
ime vai dyāvāpṛthivī dyāvākṣāmā | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.5]
te eṣa yann antarā vibhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.6]
tasmād etaddharan yajur japati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.7]
devā agniṃ dhārayan draviṇodā iti parigṛhya nidadhāti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.8]
prāṇā vai devā draviṇodāḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.9]
ta etam agra evam adhārayan | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.10]
tair evainam etaddhārayati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 3.11]
atha śikyapāśam pratimuñcate | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.1]
viśvā rūpāṇi pratimuñcate kavir ity asau vā ādityaḥ kaviḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.2]
viśvā rūpā śikyam | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.3]
prāsāvīd bhadraṃ dvipade catuṣpada ity udyan vā eṣa dvipade catuṣpade ca bhadram prasauti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.4]
vi nākam akhyat savitā vareṇya iti svargo vai loko nākaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.5]
tam eṣa udyann evānuvipaśyan yan u prayāṇam uṣaso virājatīty uṣā vā agre vyucchati | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.6]
tasyā eṣa vyuṣṭiṃ virājann anūdeti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 4.7]
athainam ato vikṛtyā vikaroti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 5.1]
idam evaitad retaḥ siktaṃ vikaroti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 5.2]
tasmād yonau retaḥ siktaṃ vikriyate | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 5.3]
suparṇo 'si garutmān iti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.1]
vīryaṃ vai suparṇo garutmān | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.2]
vīryam evainam etad abhisaṃskaroti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.3]
trivṛt te śira iti trivṛtam asya stomaṃ śiraḥ karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.4]
gāyatraṃ cakṣur iti gāyatraṃ cakṣuḥ karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.5]
bṛhadrathantare pakṣāv iti bṛhadrathantare pakṣau karoti | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 2 6.6]

āpo diva ūdhaḥ | [ŚBM, 6, 7, 4 4.9]

{ŚBM, 10, 2, 2}

prāṇā vai sādhyā devāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 3.2]

prajāpatir vai suparṇo garutmān | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 4.2]
eṣa savitā | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 4.3]

sa vai saptapuruṣo bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 5.1]

taṃ vā udbāhunā puruṣeṇa mimīte | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 6.1]
puruṣo vai yajñaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 6.2]
tenedaṃ sarvam mitam | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 6.3]
tasyaiṣā paramā mātrā yad udbāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 6.4]

tasmād u bāhyenaiva lekhām pariśridbhyaḥ khanet | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 6.7]
atha pakṣayor aratnī upādadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 7.1]
pakṣayos tad vīryaṃ dadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 7.2]
bāhū vai pakṣau | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 7.3]
bāhubhyām u vā annam adyate | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 7.4]
annāyaiva tam avakāśaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 7.5]

atha pucche vitastim upādadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.1]
pratiṣṭhāyāṃ tad vīryaṃ dadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.2]

hastena vā annam adyate | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.4]
annāyaiva tam avakāśaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.5]
tad yat pucche vitastim upādadhāty anna evainaṃ tat pratiṣṭhāpayati | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.6]
tad yat tatra kanīya upādadhāty anne hy evainaṃ tat pratiṣṭhāpayati | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.7]
atho etāvad vā idam mitam bhavaty etāvad idam | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.8]
tad yad evam mimīta etasyaivāptyai | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 2 8.9]
{ŚBM, 10, 2, 3}

tan navatiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 3 4.2]

athaikaḥ puruṣo 'tyeti | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 3 5.5]

evam eṣa saptavidha etayā vedyā sampadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 3 5.8]

na tathā kuryāt | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 3 6.2]
na vai jātaṃ garbhaṃ yonir anuvardhate | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 3 6.3]

{ŚBM, 10, 2, 4}
saṃvatsaro vai prajāpatiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 1.1]
agnir u sarve kāmāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 1.2]

sa ekaśatadhātmānaṃ vyadhatta | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 1.4]

sa eṣa ekaśatavidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 3.2]
tasya raśmayaḥ śataṃ vidhāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 3.3]

tasminn eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 6.5]

prāṇabhṛtsu pañcāśad iṣṭakāḥ pañcāśad yajūṃṣi tacchataṃ sādanaṃ ca sūdadohāś caikaśatatame | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 8.3]
tat samānaṃ sādayitvā hi sūdadohasādhivadati | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 8.4]

evam u saptavidha ekaśatavidham abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 8.7]

iti nu vidhānām | [ŚBM, 10, 2, 4 8.9]

{ŚBM, 10, 4, 2}
saṃvatsaro vai prajāpatir agniḥ somo rājā candramāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 1.1]

sa dvedhātmānaṃ vyauhat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 4.1]

sa na vyāpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 4.3]
trīn ātmano 'kuruta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 5.1]

sa naiva vyāpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 5.3]

sa naiva vyāpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 6.2]

sa naiva vyāpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 14.2]
na saptadaśadhā vyabhavat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 14.3]
aṣṭādaśātmano 'kuruta catvāriṃśadiṣṭakān | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 15.1]
sa naiva vyāśnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 15.2]
naikāṃ na viṃśatidhā vyabhavat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 15.3]
viṃśatim ātmano 'kuruta ṣaṭtriṃśadiṣṭakān | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 16.1]
sa naiva vyāpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 16.2]
naikaviṃśatidhā vyabhavan na dvāviṃśatidhā na trayoviṃśatidhā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 16.3]
caturviṃśatim ātmano 'kuruta triṃśadiṣṭakān | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 17.1]
so 'trātiṣṭhata pañcadaśe vyūhe | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 17.2]
tad yat pañcadaśe vyūhe 'tiṣṭhata tasmāt pañcadaśāpūryamāṇasya rūpāṇi pañcadaśāpakṣīyamāṇasya | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 17.3]
atha yac caturviṃśatim ātmano 'kuruta tasmāc caturviṃśatyardhamāsaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 18.1]
sa etaiś caturviṃśatyā triṃśadiṣṭakair ātmabhir na vyabhavat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 18.2]
sa pañcadaśāhno rūpāṇy apaśyad ātmanas tanvo muhūrtāṃl lokampṛṇāḥ pañcadaśaiva rātreḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 18.3]
tad yan muhu trāyante tasmān muhūrtāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 18.4]
atha yat kṣudrāḥ santa imāṃl lokān āpūrayanti tasmāl lokampṛṇāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 18.5]
eṣa vā idaṃ sarvam pacati ahorātrair ardhamāsair māsair ṛtubhiḥ saṃvatsareṇa | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 19.1]
tad amunā pakvam ayam pacati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 19.2]
pakvasya pakteti ha smāha bhāradvājo 'gnim amunā hi pakvam ayam pacatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 19.3]
tāni saṃvatsare daśa ca sahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca śatāni samapadyanta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 20.1]
so'trātiṣṭhata daśasu ca sahasreṣv aṣṭāsu ca śateṣu | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 20.2]
atha sarvāṇi bhūtāni paryaikṣat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.1]
sa trayyām eva vidyāyāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny apaśyat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.2]
atra hi sarveṣāṃ chandasām ātmā sarveṣāṃ stomānāṃ sarveṣām prāṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ devānām | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.3]
etad vā asti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.4]
etaddhy amṛtam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.5]
yaddhy amṛtaṃ taddhy asti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.6]
etad u tad yan martyam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 21.7]
sa aikṣata prajāpatiḥ trayyāṃ vāva vidyāyāṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāni | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 22.1]
hanta trayīm eva vidyām ātmānam abhisaṃskaravā iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 22.2]
sa ṛco vyauhad dvādaśa bṛhatīsahasrāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.1]
etāvatyo harco yāḥ prajāpatisṛṣṭāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.2]
tās triṃśattame vyūhe paṅktiṣv atiṣṭhanta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.3]
tā yat triṃśattame vyūhe 'tiṣṭhanta tasmāt triṃśan māsasya rātrayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.4]
atha yat paṅktiṣu tasmāt pāṅktaḥ prajāpatiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.5]
tā aṣṭāśataṃ śatāni paṅktayo 'bhavan | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 23.6]
athetarau vedau vyauhad dvādaśaiva bṛhatīsahasrāṇy aṣṭau yajuṣāṃ catvāri sāmnām | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.1]
etāvaddhaitayor vedayor yat prajāpatisṛṣṭam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.2]
tau triṃśattame vyūhe paṅktiṣv atiṣṭhetām | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.3]
tau yat triṃśattame vyūhe 'tiṣṭhetāṃ tasmāt triṃśan māsasya rātrayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.4]
atha yat paṅktiṣu tasmāt pāṅktaḥ prajāpatiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.5]
tā aṣṭāśatam eva śatāni paṅktayo 'bhavan | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 24.6]
te sarve trayo vedāḥ daśa ca sahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca śatāny aśītīnām abhavan | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 25.1]
sa muhūrtena muhūrtenāśītim āpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 25.2]
muhūrtena muhūrtenāśītiḥ samapadyata | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 25.3]
sa eṣu triṣu lokeṣūkhāyām yonau reto bhūtam ātmānam asiñcac chandomayaṃ stomamayam prāṇamayaṃ devatāmayam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 26.1]
tasyārdhamāse prathama ātmā samaskriyata davīyasi paro davīyasi paraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 26.2]
saṃvatsara eva sarvaḥ kṛtsnaḥ samaskriyata | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 26.3]
tad yat pariśritam upādhatta tad rātrim upādhatta tad anu pañcadaśa muhūrtān muhūrtān anu pañcadaśāśītīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.1]
atha yad yajuṣmatīm upādhatta tad ahar upādhatta tad anu pañcadaśa muhūrtān muhūrtān anu pañcadaśāśītīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.2]
evam etāṃ trayīṃ vidyām ātmann āvapatātmann akuruta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.3]
so 'traiva sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām ātmābhavac chandomaya stomamayaḥ prāṇamayo devatāmayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.4]
sa etanmaya eva bhūtvordhva udakrāmat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.5]
sa yaḥ sa udakrāmad eṣa sa candramāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 27.6]
tasyaiṣā pratiṣṭhā ya eṣa tapati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 28.1]
etasmād evādhyacīyataitasminn adhyacīyata | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 28.2]
ātmana evainaṃ tan niramimītātmanaḥ prājanayat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 28.3]
sa yad agniṃ ceṣyamāṇo dīkṣate yathaiva tat prajāpatir eṣu triṣu lokeṣūkhāyāṃ yonau reto bhūtam ātmānam asiñcad evam evaiṣa etad ātmānam ukhāyāṃ yonau reto bhūtaṃ siñcati chandomayaṃ stomamayam prāṇamayaṃ devatāmayam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 29.1]
tasyārdhamāse prathama ātmā saṃskriyate davīyasi paro davīyasi paraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 29.2]
saṃvatsara eva sarvaḥ kṛtsnaḥ saṃskriyate | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 29.3]
tad yat pariśritam upadhatte tad rātrim upadhatte tad anu pañcadaśa muhūrtān muhūrtān anu pañcadaśāśītīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 30.1]
atha yad yajuṣmatīm upadhatte tad ahar upadhatte tad anu pañcadaśa muhūrtān muhūrtān anu pañcadaśāśītīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 30.2]
evam etāṃ trayīṃ vidyām ātmann āvapata ātman kurute | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 30.3]
so 'traiva sarveṣām bhūtānām ātmā bhavati chandomaya stomamayaḥ prāṇamayo devatāmayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 30.4]
sa etanmaya eva bhūtvordhva utkrāmati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 30.5]
tasyaiṣā pratiṣṭhā ya eṣa tapati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 31.1]
etasmād v evādhicīyata etasminn adhicīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 31.2]
ātmana evainaṃ tan nirmimīta ātmanaḥ prajanayati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 31.3]
sa yadaivaṃvid asmāl lokāt praity athaitam evātmānam abhisaṃbhavati chandomayaṃ prāṇamayaṃ devatāmayam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 31.4]
sa etanmaya eva bhūtvordhva utkrāmati ya evaṃ vidvān etat karma kurute yo vaitad evaṃ veda | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 2 31.5]
{ŚBM, 10, 4, 3}
eṣa vai mṛtyur yat saṃvatsaraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.1]
eṣa hi martyānām ahorātrābhyām āyuḥ kṣiṇoti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.2]
atha mriyante | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.3]
tasmād eṣa eva mṛtyuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.4]
sa yo haitam mṛtyuṃ saṃvatsaraṃ veda na hāsyaiṣa purā jaraso 'horātrābhyām āyuḥ kṣiṇoti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.5]
sarvaṃ haivāyur eti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 1.6]
eṣa u evāntakaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.1]
eṣa hi martyānām ahorātrābhyām āyuṣo 'ntaṃ gacchati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.2]
atha mriyante | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.3]
tasmād eṣa evāntakaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.4]
sa yo haitam antakam mṛtyuṃ saṃvatsaraṃ veda na hāsyaiṣa purā jaraso 'horātrābhyām āyuṣo 'ntaṃ gacchati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.5]
sarvaṃ haivāyur eti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 2.6]
te devāḥ etasmād antakān mṛtyoḥ saṃvatsarāt prajāpater bibhayāṃcakrur yad vai no 'yam ahorātrābhyām āyuṣo 'ntaṃ na gacched iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 3.1]
ta etān yajñakratūṃs tenire agnihotraṃ darśapūrṇamāsau cāturmāsyāni paśubandhaṃ saumyam adhvaram | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 4.1]
ta etair yajñakratubhir yajamānā nāmṛtatvam ānaśire | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 4.2]
te hāpy agniṃ cikyire | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 5.1]
te 'parimitā eva pariśrita upadadhur aparimitā yajuṣmatīr aparimitā lokampṛṇā yathedam apy etarhy eka upadadhatīti devā akurvann iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 5.2]
te ha naivāmṛtatvam ānaśire | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 5.3]
te 'rcantaḥ śrāmyantaś ceruḥ amṛtatvam avarurutsamānāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 6.1]
tān ha prajāpatir uvāca na vai me sarvāṇi rūpāṇy upadhattha | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 6.2]
ati vaiva recayatha na vābhyāpayatha | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 6.3]
tasmān nāmṛtā bhavatheti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 6.4]
te hocus tebhyo vai nas tvam eva tad brūhi yathā te sarvāṇi rūpāṇy upadadhāmeti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 7.1]
sa hovāca ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni pariśrita upadhatta ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni yajuṣmatīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.1]
adhi ṣaṭtriṃśatam atha lokampṛṇā daśa ca sahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca śatāny upadhatta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.2]
atha me sarvāṇi rūpāṇy upadhāsyatha | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.3]
athāmṛtā bhaviṣyatheti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.4]
te ha tathā devā upadadhuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.5]
tato devā amṛtā āsuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 8.6]
sa mṛtyur devān abravīd ittham eva sarve manuṣyā amṛtā bhaviṣyanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.1]
atha ko mahyam bhāgo bhaviṣyatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.2]
te hocur nāto 'paraḥ kaścana saha śarīreṇāmṛto 'sat | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.3]
yadaiva tvam etam bhāgaṃ harāsā atha vyāvṛtya śarīreṇāmṛto 'sad yo 'mṛto 'sad vidyayā vā karmaṇā veti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.4]
yad vai tad abruvan vidyayā vā karmaṇā vety eṣā haiva sā vidyā yad agniḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.5]
etad u haiva tat karma yad agniḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 9.6]
te ya evam etad vidur ye vaitat karma kurvate mṛtvā punaḥ sambhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 10.1]
te sambhavanta evāmṛtatvam abhisaṃbhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 10.2]
atha ya evaṃ na vidur ye vaitat karma na kurvate mṛtvā punaḥ sambhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 10.3]
ta etasyaivānnaṃ punaḥ punar bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 10.4]
sa yad agniṃ cinute etam eva tad antakam mṛtyuṃ saṃvatsaram prajāpatim agnim āpnoti yaṃ devā āpnuvann etam upadhatte yathaivainam ado devā upādadhata | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 11.1]
pariśridbhir evāsya rātrīr āpnoti yajuṣmatībhir ahāny ardhamāsān māsān ṛtūṃl lokampṛṇābhir muhūrtān | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 12.1]
tad yāḥ pariśritaḥ rātrilokās tā rātrīṇām eva sāptiḥ kriyate rātrīṇām pratimā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 13.1]
tāḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi ca śatāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 13.2]
ṣaṣṭiś ca ha vai trīṇi ca śatāni saṃvatsarasya rātrayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 13.3]
tāsām ekaviṃśatiṃ gārhapatye pariśrayati dvābhyāṃ nāśītiṃ dhiṣṇyeṣu dve ekaṣaṣṭe śate āhavanīye | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 13.4]
atha yajuṣmatyaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 14.1]
darbhastambo logeṣṭakāḥ puṣkaraparṇaṃ rukmapuruṣau srucau svayamātṛṇṇā dūrveṣṭakā dviyajū retaḥsicau viśvajyotir ṛtavye aṣāḍhā kūrma ulūkhalamusale ukhā pañca paśuśīrṣāṇi pañcadaśāpasyāḥ pañca chandasyāḥ pañcāśat prāṇabhṛtas tā dvābhyāṃ na śataṃ prathamā citiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 14.2]
atha dvitīyā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 15.1]
pañcāśvinyo dve ṛtavye pañca vaiśvadevyaḥ pañca prāṇabhṛtaḥ pañcāpasyā ekayā na viṃśatir vayasyāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 15.2]
tā ekacatvāriṃśad dvitīyā citiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 15.3]
atha tṛtīyā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 16.1]
svayamātṛṇṇā pañca diśyā viśvajyotiś catasra ṛtavyā daśa prāṇabhṛtaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśac chandasyāś caturdaśa vālakhilyāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 16.2]
tā ekasaptatis tṛtīyā citiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 16.3]
atha caturthī | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 17.1]
aṣṭādaśa prathamā atha dvādaśātha saptadaśa | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 17.2]
tāḥ saptacatvāriṃśac caturthī citiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 17.3]
atha pañcamī | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 18.1]
pañcāsapatnāś catvāriṃśad virāja ekayā na triṃśat stomabhāgāḥ pañca nākasadaḥ pañca pañcacūḍā ekatriṃśac chandasyā aṣṭau gārhapatyā citir aṣṭau punaścitir ṛtavye viśvajyotir vikarṇī ca svayamātṛṇṇā cāśmā pṛśnir yaś cite 'gnir nidhīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 18.2]
tā aṣṭātriṃśaṃ śataṃ pañcamī citiḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 18.3]
tāḥ sarvāḥ pañcabhir na catvāri śatāni | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.1]
tato yāḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi ca śatāny aharlokās tā ahnām eva sāptiḥ kriyate 'hnām pratimā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.2]
tāḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi ca śatāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.3]
ṣaṣṭiś ca ha vai trīṇi ca śatāni saṃvatsarasyāhāni | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.4]
atha yāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśat purīṣaṃ tāsāṃ ṣaṭtriṃśī | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.5]
tato yāś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsalokās tā ardhamāsānām eva sāptiḥ kriyate 'rdhamāsānām pratimā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.6]
atha yā dvādaśa māsalokās tā māsānām eva sāptiḥ kriyate māsānām pratimā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.7]
tā u dve dve sahartulokā ṛtūnām aśūnyatāyai | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 19.8]
atha yā lokampṛṇāḥ muhūrtalokās tā muhūrtānām eva sāptiḥ kriyate muhūrtānām pratimā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.1]
tā daśa ca sahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca śatāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.2]
etāvanto hi saṃvatsarasya muhūrtāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.3]
tāsām ekaviṃśatiṃ gārhapatya upadadhāti dvābhyāṃ nāśītiṃ dhiṣṇyeṣv āhavanīya itarāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.4]
etāvanti vai saṃvatsarasya rūpāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.5]
tāny asyātrāptāny upahitāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 20.6]
taddhaike āhavanīya evaitāṃ saṃpadam āpipayiṣanty anye vā ete 'gnayaś citāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.1]
kim anyatropahitā iha saṃpaśyemeti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.2]
na tathā kuryāt | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.3]
daśa vā etān agnīṃś cinute 'ṣṭau dhiṣṇyān āhavanīyaṃ ca gārhapatyaṃ ca | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.4]
tasmād āhur virāḍ agnir iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.5]
daśākṣarā hi virāṭ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.6]
tān nu sarvān ekam ivaivācakṣate 'gnir iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.7]
etasya hy evaitāni sarvāṇi rūpāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.8]
yathā saṃvatsarasyāhorātrāṇy ardhamāsā māsā ṛtava evam asyaitāni sarvāṇi rūpāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 21.9]
te ye ha tathā kurvanti etāni hāsya te rūpāṇi bahirdhā kurvanty atho pāpavasyasaṃ kurvanti kṣatrāya viśam pratipratinīm pratyudyāminīm | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 22.1]
āgnīdhrīye vā aśmānaṃ pṛśnim upadadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 22.2]
atha taṃ saṃpaśyati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 22.3]
kim u taṃ saṃpaśyann itarā na saṃpaśyet | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 22.4]
yenaiva nirṛtim pāpmānam apahate sa ekādaśaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 22.5]
tad āhuḥ katham u tā atra na saṃpaśyatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 23.1]
na hy enā abhijuhoti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 23.2]
āhutyā vā iṣṭakā sarvā kṛtsnā bhavatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 23.3]
tad āhuḥ katham asyaitā anatiriktā upahitā bhavantīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 24.1]
vīryaṃ vā asyaitāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 24.2]
anatiriktaṃ vai puruṣaṃ vīryam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 24.3]
sa ha vā etaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtsnam prajāpatiṃ saṃskaroti ya evaṃ vidvān etat karma kurute yo vaitad evaṃ veda | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 3 24.4]
{ŚBM, 10, 4, 4}
prajāpatiṃ vai prajāḥ sṛjamānam pāpmā mṛtyur abhiparijaghāna | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 1.1]
sa tapo 'tapyata sahasraṃ saṃvatsarān pāpmānaṃ vijihāsan | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 1.2]
tasya tapas tepānasya ebhyo lomagartebhya ūrdhvāni jyotīṃṣy āyan | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 2.1]
tad yāni tāni jyotīṃṣy etāni tāni nakṣatrāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 2.2]
yāvanty etāni nakṣatrāṇi tāvanto lomagartāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 2.3]
yāvanto lomagartās tāvantaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsarasya muhūrtāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 2.4]
sa sahasratame saṃvatsare sarvo 'tyapavata | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 3.1]
sa yaḥ so 'tyapavatāyam eva sa vāyur yo'yaṃ pavate | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 3.2]
atha yaṃ tam pāpmānam atyapavatedaṃ taccharīram | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 3.3]
ka u tasmai manuṣyo yaḥ sahasrasaṃvatsaram avarundhīta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 3.4]
vidyayā ha vā evaṃvit sahasrasaṃvatsaram avarunddhe | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 3.5]
sarvā evaitā iṣṭakāḥ sāhasrīr upāsīta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.1]
rātrisahasreṇa rātrisahasreṇaikaikām pariśritaṃ sampannām upāsītāhaḥsahasreṇāhaḥsahasreṇaikaikām aharbhājam ardhamāsasahasreṇārdhamāsasahasreṇaikaikām ardhamāsabhājaṃ māsasahasreṇa māsasahasreṇaikaikāṃ māsabhājam ṛtusahasreṇartusahasreṇaikaikām ṛtubhājaṃ muhūrtasahasreṇa muhūrtasahasreṇaikaikām muhūrtabhājaṃ saṃvatsarasahasreṇa saṃvatsaram | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.2]
te ya etam evam agniṃ saṃvatsareṇa sampannaṃ viduḥ sahasratamīṃ hāsya te kalāṃ viduḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.3]
atha ya enam evaṃ na viduḥ na hāsya te sahasratamīṃ cana kalāṃ viduḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.4]
atha ya evaivaṃ veda yo vaitat karma kurute sa haivaitaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtsnam prājāpatyam agnim āpnoti yam prajāpatir āpnot | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.5]
tasmād evaṃvit tapa eva tapyeta | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.6]
yad u ha vā evaṃvit tapa tapyata ā maithunāt sarvaṃ hāsya tat svargaṃ lokam abhisaṃbhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 4.7]
tad etad ṛcābhyuktaṃ na mṛṣā śrāntaṃ yad avanti devā iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 5.1]
na haivaivaṃ viduṣaḥ kiṃ cana mṛṣā śrāntam bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 5.2]
tatho hāsyaitat sarvaṃ devā avanti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 4 5.3]
{ŚBM, 10, 4, 5}
athādeśā upaniṣadām | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 1.1]
vāyur agnir iti ha śākāyanina upāsate | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 1.2]
ādityo 'gnir ity u haika āhuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 1.3]
atha ha smāha śraumatyo vā hāliṅgavo vā vāyur evāgniḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 1.4]
tasmād yadaivādhvaryur uttamaṃ karma karoty athaitam evāpyetīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 1.5]
śāṭyāyanir u ha smāha saṃvatsara evāgniḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.1]
tasya vasantaḥ śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.2]
grīṣmo dakṣiṇaḥ pakṣo varṣā uttaraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.3]
śarad ṛtur madhyamātmā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.4]
hemantaśiśirāv ṛtū puccham pratiṣṭhā | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.5]
vāg agniḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.6]
prāṇo vāyuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.7]
cakṣur ādityaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.8]
manaś candramāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.9]
śrotraṃ diśaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.10]
āpo mithunam | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.11]
tapaḥ pratiṣṭhāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.12]
māsāḥ parvāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.13]
ardhamāsā nāḍyaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.14]
ahorātrāṇi rajatasuvarṇāni patrāṇi | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.15]
sa evaṃ devān apyetīti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.16]
saṃvatsaro 'gnir ity u haiva vidyāt | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.17]
etanmayo bhavatīti tv eva vidyāt | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 2.18]
chelaka u ha smāha śāṇḍilyāyana ima eva lokās tisraḥ svayamātṛṇṇavatyaś citayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 3.1]
yajamānaś caturthī | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 3.2]
sarve kāmāḥ pañcamī | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 3.3]
imāṃś ca lokānt saṃskurv ātmānaṃ ca sarvāṃś ca kāmān ity eva vidyād iti | [ŚBM, 10, 4, 5 3.4]
{ŚBM, 10, 5, 1}
tasya vā etasyāgneḥ vāg evopaniṣat | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 1.1]
vācā hi cīyata ṛcā yajuṣā sāmneti nu daivyā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 1.2]
atha yan mānuṣyā vācāhetīdaṃ kurutetīdaṃ kuruteti tad u ha tayā cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 1.3]
sā vā eṣā vāk tredhā vihitarco yajūṃṣi sāmāni | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.1]
tenāgnis tredhā vihitaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.2]
etena hi trayeṇa cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.3]
apy ahaivaṃ tredhā vihitaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.4]
itthaṃ ha tv evāpi tredhā vihito yad asmiṃs tredhā vihitā iṣṭakā upadhīyante puṃnāmnya strīnāmnyo napuṃsakanāmnyaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.5]
tredhā vihitāny u evemāni puruṣasyāṅgāni puṃnāmāni strīnāmāni napuṃsakanāmāni | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 2.6]
so 'yam ātmā tredhā vihita eva | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.1]
so 'nena tredhā vihitenātmanaitaṃ tredhā vihitaṃ daivam amṛtam āpnoti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.2]
tā u sarvā iṣṭakā ity evācakṣate neṣṭaka iti neṣṭakam iti vāco rūpeṇa | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.3]
vāgghy evaitat sarvaṃ yat strī pumān napuṃsakam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.4]
vācā hy evaitat sarvam āptam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.5]
tasmād enā aṅgirasvad dhruvā sīdety eva sarvāḥ sādayati nāṅgirasvad dhruvaḥ sīdeti nāṅgirasvad dhruvaṃ sīdeti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.6]
vācaṃ hy evaitāṃ saṃskurute | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 3.7]
sā yā sā vāg asau sa ādityaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.1]
sa eṣa mṛtyuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.2]
tad yat kiṃcārvācīnam ādityāt sarvaṃ tan mṛtyunāptam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.3]
sa yo hainam ato 'rvācīnaṃ cinute mṛtyunā hainaṃ sa āptaṃ cinute | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.4]
mṛtyave ha sa ātmānam apidadhāti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.5]
atha ya enam ata ūrdhvaṃ cinute sa punarmṛtyum apajayati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.6]
vidyayā ha vā asyaiṣo'ta ūrdhvaṃ cito bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 4.7]
sā vā eṣā vāk tredhā vihitarco yajūṃṣi sāmāni | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.1]
maṇḍalam evarcaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.2]
arciḥ sāmāni | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.3]
puruṣo yajūṃṣi | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.4]
athaitad amṛtaṃ yad etad arcir dīpyata idaṃ tat puṣkaraparṇam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.5]
tad yat puṣkaraparṇam upadhāyāgniṃ cinoty etasminn evaitad amṛta ṛṅmayaṃ yajurmayaṃ sāmamayam ātmānaṃ saṃskurute | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.6]
so 'mṛto bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 1 5.7]
{ŚBM, 10, 5, 2}
yad etan maṇḍalaṃ tapati tan mahad ukthaṃ tā ṛcaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 1.1]
sa ṛcāṃ lokaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 1.2]
atha yad etad arcir dīpyate tan mahāvrataṃ tāni sāmāni | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 1.3]
sa sāmnāṃ lokaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 1.4]
atha ya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣaḥ so 'gnis tāni yajūṃṣi | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 1.5]

saiṣā trayy eva vidyā tapati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 2.1]

amṛte hy antaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 3.4]
tasmād u na dṛśyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 3.5]
amṛte hy antaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 3.6]

etad eṣa śloko bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 4.12]
tayor vā etayoḥ ubhayor etasya cārciṣa etasya ca puruṣasyaitan maṇḍalam pratiṣṭhā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 5.1]

pratiṣṭhāchinno hi bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 5.5]
ity adhidevatam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 5.6]
athādhiyajñam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.1]
yad etan maṇḍalaṃ tapaty ayaṃ sa rukmaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.2]
atha yad etad arcir dīpyata idaṃ tat puṣkaraparṇam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.3]
āpo hy etāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.4]
āpaḥ puṣkaraparṇam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.5]

tad etad evaitat trayaṃ saṃskṛtyehopadhatte | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.7]

amutra hy eṣa tadā bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.11]
ity u evādhiyajñam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 6.12]
athādhyātmam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 7.1]
yad etan maṇḍalaṃ tapati yaś caiṣa rukma idaṃ tacchuklam akṣan | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 7.2]

atha ya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣo yaś caiṣa hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo 'yam eva sa yo 'yaṃ dakṣiṇe 'kṣan puruṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 7.4]

ardham u haitad ātmano yan mithunam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 8.4]

daivaṃ hy etan mithunam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 11.4]

lokyaṃ ha | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 12.2]

sa eṣa eva mṛtyuḥ ya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣo yaś cāyaṃ dakṣiṇe 'kṣan puruṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 13.1]

etena hīdaṃ sarvaṃ yatam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.8]
viṣam iti sarpāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.9]

ūrg iti devāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.11]

māyety asurāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.13]
svadheti pitaraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.14]
devajana iti devajanavidaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.15]
rūpam iti gandharvāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.16]
gandha ity apsarasaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.17]
taṃ yathā yathopāsate tad eva bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.18]
taddhainān bhūtvāvati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.19]
tasmād etam evaṃvit sarvair evaitair upāsīta | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.20]
sarvaṃ haitad bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.21]
sarvaṃ hainam etad bhūtvāvati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 20.22]
sa eṣa trīṣṭako 'gnir ṛg ekā yajur ekā sāmaikā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 21.1]
tad yāṃ kāṃ cātrarcopadadhāti rukma eva tasyā āyatanam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 21.2]
atha yāṃ yajuṣā puruṣa eva tasyā āyatanam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 21.3]
atha yāṃ sāmnā puṣkaraparṇam eva tasyā āyatanam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 21.4]
evaṃ trīṣṭakaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 21.5]
te vā ete ubhe eṣa ca rukma etac ca puṣkaraparṇam etam puruṣam apītaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 22.1]
ubhe hy ṛkṣāme yajur apītaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 22.2]
evam v ekeṣṭakaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 22.3]
sa eṣa eva mṛtyuḥ ya eṣa etasmin maṇḍale puruṣo yaś cāyaṃ dakṣiṇe 'kṣan puruṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 23.1]
sa eṣa evaṃvida ātmā bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 23.2]

mṛtyur hy asyātmā bhavati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 2 23.5]

{ŚBM, 10, 5, 4}
ayaṃ vāva loka eṣo 'gniś citaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.1]
tasyāpa eva pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.2]
manuṣyā yajuṣmatya iṣṭakāḥ sūdadohāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.3]
oṣadhayaś ca vanaspatayaś ca purīṣam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.4]
āhutayaḥ samidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.5]
agnir lokampṛṇā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.6]
tad vā etat sarvam agnim evābhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.7]
tat sarvo 'gnir lokampṛṇām abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.8]
sa yo haitad evaṃ veda lokampṛṇām enam bhūtam etat sarvam abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 1.9]
antarikṣaṃ ha tv evaiṣo 'gniś citaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.1]
tasya dyāvāpṛthivyor eva saṃdhiḥ pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.2]
pareṇa hāntarikṣaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī saṃdhattaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.3]
tāḥ pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.4]
vayāṃsi yajuṣmatya iṣṭakāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.5]
varṣaṃ sūdadohāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.6]
marīcayaḥ purīṣam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.7]
āhutayaḥ samidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.8]
vāyur lokampṛṇā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.9]
tad vā etat sarvaṃ vāyum evābhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.10]
tat sarvo 'gnir lokampṛṇām abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.11]
sa yo haitad evaṃ veda lokampṛṇām enam bhūtam etat sarvam abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 2.12]
dyaur ha tv evaiṣo 'gniś citaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.1]
tasyāpa eva pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.2]
yathā ha vā idaṃ kośaḥ samubjita evam ime lokā apsv antaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.3]
tad yā imāṃl lokān pareṇāpas tāḥ pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.4]
devā yajuṣmatya iṣṭakāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.5]
yad evaitasmiṃl loke 'nnaṃ tat sūdadohāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.6]
nakṣatrāṇi purīṣam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.7]
āhutayaḥ samidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.8]
ādityo lokampṛṇā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.9]
tad vā etat sarvam ādityam evābhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.10]
tat sarvo 'gnir lokampṛṇām abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.11]
sa yo haitad evaṃ veda lokampṛṇām enam bhūtam etat sarvam abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 3.12]
ādityo ha tv evaiṣo 'gniś citaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.1]
tasya diśa eva pariśritaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.2]
tāḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi ca śatāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.3]
ṣaṣṭiś ca ha vai trīṇi ca śatāny ādityaṃ diśaḥ samantam pariyanti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.4]
raśmayo yajuṣmatya iṣṭakāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.5]
tāḥ ṣaṣṭiś caiva trīṇi ca śatāni bhavanti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.6]
ṣaṣṭiś ca ha vai trīṇi ca śatāny ādityasya raśmayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.7]
tad yat pariśritsu yajuṣmatīḥ pratyarpayati raśmīṃs tad dikṣu pratyarpayati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.8]
atha yad antarā diśaś ca raśmīṃś ca tat sūdadohāḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.9]
atha yad dikṣu ca raśmiṣu cānnaṃ tat purīṣam | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.10]
tā āhutayaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.11]
tāḥ samidhaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.12]
atha yad diśa iti ca raśmaya iti cākhyāyate tal lokampṛṇā | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.13]
tad vā etat sarvaṃ diśa iti caiva raśmaya iti cākhyāyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.14]
tat sarvo 'gnir lokampṛṇām abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.15]
sa yo haitad evaṃ veda lokampṛṇām enam bhūtam etat sarvam abhisaṃpadyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 4 4.16]

{ŚBM, 10, 5, 5}
kuśrir ha vājaśravaso 'gniṃ cikye | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 1.1]
taṃ hovāca suśravāḥ kauṣyo gautama yad agnim acaiṣīḥ prāñcam enam acaiṣīḥ pratyañcam enam acaiṣīr nyañcam enam acaiṣīr uttānam enam acaiṣīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 1.2]
yady ahainam prāñcam acaiṣīḥ yathā parāca āsīnāya pṛṣṭhato 'nnādyam upāharet tādṛk tat | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 2.1]
na te haviḥ pratigrahīṣyati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 2.2]
yady u vā enam pratyañcam acaiṣīḥ kasmād asya tarhi paścātpuccham akārṣīḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 3.1]
yady u vā enaṃ nyañcam acaiṣīḥ yathā nīcaḥ śayānasya pṛṣṭhe 'nnādyaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayet tādṛk tat | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 4.1]
naiva te haviḥ pratigrahīṣyati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 4.2]
yady u vā enam uttānam acaiṣīḥ na vā uttānaṃ vayaḥ svargaṃ lokam abhivahati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 5.1]
na tvā svargaṃ lokam abhivakṣyati | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 5.2]
asvargya u te bhaviṣyatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 5.3]
sa hovāca prāñcam enam acaiṣam pratyañcam enam acaiṣaṃ nyañcam enam acaiṣam uttānam enam acaiṣaṃ sarvā anu diśa enam acaiṣam iti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 6.1]
sa yat prāñcam puruṣam upadadhāti prācyau srucau tat prāṅ cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 7.1]
atha yat pratyañcaṃ kūrmam upadadhāti pratyañci paśuśīrṣāṇi tat pratyaṅ cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 7.2]
atha yan nyañcaṃ kūrmam upadadhāti nyañci paśuśīrṣāṇi nīcīr iṣṭakās tan nyaṅ cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 7.3]
atha yad uttānaṃ puruṣam upadadhāty uttāne srucā uttānam ulūkhalam uttānām ukhāṃ tad uttānaś cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 7.4]
atha yat sarvā anu diśaḥ parisarpam iṣṭakā upadadhāti tat sarvataś cīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 7.5]
atha ha koṣā dhāvayantaḥ nirūḍhaśirasam agnim upādhāvayāṃcakruḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 8.1]
teṣāṃ haika uvāca śrīr vai śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 8.2]
śriyam asya nirauhīt | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 8.3]
sarvajyāniṃ jyāsyata iti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 8.4]
sa ha tathaivāsa | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 8.5]
atha haika uvāca prāṇā vai śiraḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 9.1]
prāṇān asya nirauhīt | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 9.2]
kṣipre 'muṃ lokam eṣyatīti | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 9.3]
sa u ha tathaivāsa | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 9.4]
ūrdhvo vā eṣa etac cīyate yad darbhastambo logeṣṭakāḥ puṣkaraparṇaṃ rukmapuruṣau srucau svayamātṛṇṇā dūrveṣṭakā dviyajū retaḥsicau viśvajyotir ṛtavye aṣāḍhā kūrmaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 10.1]
atha hāsyaitad eva pratyakṣatamāṃ śiro yaś cite 'gnir nidhīyate | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 10.2]
tasmān na nirūhet | [ŚBM, 10, 5, 5 10.3]
{ŚBM, 10, 6, 1}
atha haite 'ruṇe aupaveśau samājagmuḥ satyayajñaḥ pauluṣir mahāśālo jābālo buḍila āśvatarāśvir indradyumno bhāllaveyo janaḥ śārkarākṣyaḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 1.1]
te ha vaiśvānare samāsata | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 1.2]
teṣāṃ ha vaiśvānare na samiyāya | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 1.3]
te hocur aśvapatir vā ayaṃ kaikeyaḥ samprati vaiśvānaraṃ veda | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 2.1]
taṃ gacchāmeti | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 2.2]
te hāśvapatiṃ kaikeyam ājagmuḥ | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 2.3]
tebhyo ha pṛthag āvasathān pṛthag apacitīḥ pṛthak sāhasrānt somān provāca | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 2.4]
te ha prātar asaṃvidānā eva samitpāṇayaḥ praticakramira upa tvāyāmeti | [ŚBM, 10, 6, 1 2.5]

{ŚBM, 10, 6, 4}

{ŚBM, 10, 6, 5}

darbhamayī raśanā bhavati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 1 2.1]

prajāpatiryajñamasṛjata | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 1 4.1]
tasya mahimāpākrāmat sa mahartvijaḥ prāviśat taṃ mahartvigbhir anvaicchat tam mahartvigbhir anvavindad yan mahartvijo brahmaudanam prāśnanti mahimānameva tad yajñasya yajamāno 'varunddhe brahmaudane suvarṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dadāti reto vā odano reto hiraṇyaṃ retasaivāsmiṃstad reto dadhāti śatamānam bhavati śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatendriya āyur evendriyaṃ vīryam ātman dhatte catuṣṭayīr apo vasatīvarīr madhyamāyāhne gṛhṇāti tā digbhyaḥ samāhṛtā bhavanti dikṣu vā annam annam āpo 'nnenaivāsmā annam avarunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 1 4.2]
{ŚBM, 13, 1, 2}
vyṛddham u vā etad yajñasya | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 1.1]

tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 2.1]
dvādaśāratnī raśanā kāryā3 trayodaśāratnī3r ity ṛṣabho vā eṣa ṛtūnāṃ yat saṃvatsaras tasya trayodaśo māso viṣṭapamṛṣabha eṣa yajñānāṃ yadaśvamedho yathā vā ṛṣabhasya viṣṭapam evametasya viṣṭapaṃ trayodaśam aratniṃ raśanāyāmupādadhyāt tad yatharṣabhasya viṣṭapaṃ saṃskriyate tādṛktat | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 2.2]
abhidhā asīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 3.1]
tasmād aśvamedhayājī sarvā diśo'bhijayati bhuvanam asīti bhuvanaṃ tajjayati yantāsi dharteti yantāram evainaṃ dhartāraṃ karoti sa tvamagniṃ vaiśvānaram ityagnim evainaṃ vaiśvānaraṃ gamayati saprathasaṃ gaccheti prajayaivainam paśubhiḥ prathayati svāhākṛta iti vaṣaṭkāra evāsyaiṣa svagā tvā devebhya iti devebhya evainaṃ svagākaroti prajāpataya iti prājāpatyo 'śvaḥ svayaivainaṃ devatayā samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 3.2]
īśvaro vā eṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 4.1]
ārtim ārtor yo brahmaṇe devebhyo 'pratiprocyāśvaṃ badhnāti brahmannaśvam bhantsyāmi devebhyaḥ prajāpataye tena rādhyāsamiti brahmāṇamāmantrayate brahmaṇa evainam pratiprocya badhnāti nārtimārchati taṃ badhāna devebhyaḥ prajāpataye tena rādhnuhīti brahmā prasauti svayaivainaṃ devatayā samardhayatyatha prokṣatyasāveva bandhuḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 4.2]
sa prokṣati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 5.1]

indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭam prokṣāmīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 6.1]

vāyave tvā juṣṭam prokṣāmīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 7.1]
vāyurvai devānāmāśiṣṭho javamevāsmindadhāti tasmādaśvaḥ paśūnām āśiṣṭhaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 7.2]
viśvebhyastvā devebhyo juṣṭam prokṣāmīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 8.1]
viśve vai devā devānāṃ yaśasvitamā yaśa evāsmindadhāti tasmād aśvaḥ paśūnāṃ yaśasvitamaḥ sarvebhyastvā devebhyo juṣṭam prokṣāmīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 8.2]

yat prājāpatyo 'śvo 'tha kathāpyanyābhyo devatābhyaḥ prokṣatīti sarvā vai devatā aśvamedhe'nvāyattā yadāha sarvebhyastvā devebhyaḥ prokṣāmīti sarvā evāsmindevatā anvāyātayati tasmādaśvamedhe sarvā devatā anvāyattāḥ pāpmā vā etam bhrātṛvya īpsati yo 'śvamedhena yajeta vajro 'śvaḥ paro martaḥ paraḥ śveti śvānaṃ caturakṣaṃ hatvādhaspadam aśvasyopaplāvayati vajreṇaivainam avakrāmati nainaṃ pāpmā bhrātṛvya āpnoti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 2 9.2]
{ŚBM, 13, 1, 3}
yathā vai haviṣo 'hutasya skandet evam etat paśo skandati yaṃ niktam anālabdham utsṛjanti yatstokīyā juhoti sarvahutam evainaṃ juhotyaskandāyāskannaṃ hi tadyaddhutasya skandati sahasraṃ juhoti sahasrasaṃmito vai svargo lokaḥ svargasya lokasyābhijityai | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 1]
tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 2.1]
yanmitā juhuyātparimitamavarundhītetyamitā juhotyaparimitasyaivāvaruddhyā uvāca ha prajāpati stokīyāsu vā ahamaśvamedhaṃ saṃsthāpayāmi tena saṃsthitenaivāta ūrdhvaṃ carāmīti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 2.2]
agnaye svāheti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 3.1]
agnaya evainaṃ juhoti somāya svāheti somāyaivainaṃ juhoty apāṃ modāya svāhety adbhya evainaṃ juhoti savitre svāheti savitra evainaṃ juhoti vāyave svāheti vāyava evainaṃ juhoti viṣṇave svāheti viṣṇava evainaṃ juhotīndrāya svāhetīndrāyaivainaṃ juhoti bṛhaspataye svāheti bṛhaspataya evainaṃ juhoti mitrāya svāheti mitrāyaivainaṃ juhoti varuṇāya svāheti varuṇāyaivainaṃ juhoty etāvanto vai sarve devās tebhya evainaṃ juhoti parācīr juhoti parāṅ iva vai svargo lokaḥ svargasya lokasyābhijityai | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 3.2]
īśvaro vā eṣaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 4.1]
parāṅ pradaghor yaḥ parācīrāhutīrjuhoti punarāvartate 'sminneva loke pratitiṣṭhaty etāṃ ha vāva sa yajñasya saṃsthitim uvācāskandāyāskannaṃ hi tadyaddhutasya skandati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 4.2]
yathā vai haviṣo 'hutasya skandet | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 5.1]
evam etat paśo skandati yam prokṣitam anālabdham utsṛjanti yad rūpāṇi juhoti sarvahutamevainaṃ juhotyaskandāyāskannaṃ hi tadyaddhutasya skandati hiṅkārāya svāhā hiṃkṛtāya svāhetyetāni vā aśvasya rūpāṇi tānyevāvarunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 5.2]
tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 6.1]
anāhutir vai rūpāṇi naitā hotavyā ity atho khalvāhuratra vā aśvamedhaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yadrūpāṇi juhoti hotavyā eveti bahirdhā vā etamāyatanātkaroti bhrātṛvyamasmai janayati yasyānāyatane 'nyatrāgner āhutīrjuhoti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 6.2]
sāvitryā eveṣṭeḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 7.1]
purastādanudrutya sakṛd eva rūpāṇyāhavanīye juhoty āyatana evāhutīrjuhoti nāsmai bhrātṛvyaṃ janayati yajñamukhe yajñamukhe juhoti yajñasya saṃtatyā avyavacchedāya | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 7.2]
tadāhuḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 8.1]
yad yajñamukhe yajñamukhe juhuyāt paśubhirvyṛdhyeta pāpīyāntsyāt sakṛdeva hotavyā na paśubhir vyṛdhyate na pāpīyān bhavaty aṣṭācatvāriṃśataṃ juhoty aṣṭācatvāriṃśadakṣarā jagatī jāgatāḥ paśavo jagatyaivāsmai paśūn avarunddha ekamatiriktaṃ juhoti tasmādekaḥ prajāsvardhukaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 3 8.2]
{ŚBM, 13, 1, 4}

{ŚBM, 13, 1, 5}

{ŚBM, 13, 1, 7}
prajāpatirakāmayata aśvamedhena yajeyeti so'śrāmyat sa tapo'tapyata tasya śrāntasya taptasya saptadhātmano devatā apākrāmant sā dīkṣābhavat sa etāni vaiśvadevānyapaśyat tānyajuhot tairvai sa dīkṣāmavārunddha yad vaiśvadevāni juhoti dīkṣāmeva tair yajamāno 'varunddhe 'nvahaṃ juhoty anvahameva dīkṣāmavarunddhe sapta juhoti sapta vai tā devatā apākrāmaṃs tābhir evāsmai dīkṣām avarunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 7 1]
apa vā etebhyaḥ prāṇāḥ krāmanti ye dīkṣām atirecayanti saptāham pracaranti sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇā dīkṣā prāṇairevāsmai prāṇāndīkṣāmavarunddhe tredhā vibhajya devatāṃ juhoti tryāvṛto vai devās tryāvṛta ime lokā ṛddhyām eva vīrya eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 7 2]
ekaviṃśatiḥ sampadyante dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavastraya ime lokā asāvāditya ekaviṃśas tad daivaṃ kṣatraṃ sā śrīs tad ādhipatyaṃ tadbradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ tatsvārājyamaśnute | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 7 3]
triṃśatamaudgrabhaṇāni juhoti triṃśadakṣarā virāḍ virāḍ u kṛtsnamannaṃ kṛtsnasyaivānnādyasyāvaruddhyai catvāry audgrabhaṇāni juhoti trīṇi vaiśvadevāni sapta sampadyante sapta vai śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇā dīkṣā prāṇair evāsmai prāṇāndīkṣāmavarunddhe pūrṇāhutimuttamāṃ juhoti pratyuttabdhyai sayuktvāya | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 7 4]
{ŚBM, 13, 1, 8}
prajāpatiraśvamedhamasṛjata sa sṛṣṭaḥ prarcam avlīnāt pra sāma taṃ vaiśvadevānyudayacchan yad vaiśvadevāni juhotyaśvamedhasyaivodyatyai | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 1]
kāya svāhā kasmai svāhā katamasmai svāheti prājāpatyam mukhyaṃ karoti prajāpatimukhābhirevainaṃ devatābhir udyacchati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 2]
svāhādhim ādhītāya svāhā manaḥ prajāpataye svāhā cittaṃ vijñātāyeti yadeva pūrvāsām brāhmaṇaṃ tad atra | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 3]
adityai svāhā adityai mahyai svāhādityai sumṛḍīkāyai svāhetīyaṃ vā aditir anayaivainam udyacchati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 4]
sarasvatyai svāhā sarasvatyai pāvakāyai svāhā sarasvatyai bṛhatyai svāheti vāgvai sarasvatī vācaivainamudyacchati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 5]
pūṣṇe svāhā pūṣṇe prapathyāya svāhā pūṣṇe naraṃdhiṣāya svāheti paśavo vai pūṣā paśubhirevainam udyacchati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 6]
tvaṣṭre svāhā tvaṣṭre turīpāya svāhā tvaṣṭre pururūpāya svāheti tvaṣṭā vai paśūnām mithunānāṃ rūpakṛd rūpairevainam udyacchati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 7]
viṣṇave svāhā viṣṇave nibhūyapāya svāhā viṣṇave śipiviṣṭāya svāheti yajño vai viṣṇur yajñenaivainam udyacchati viśvo devasya neturiti pūrṇāhutimuttamāṃ juhotīyaṃ vai pūrṇāhutir asyāmevāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 8 8]
{ŚBM, 13, 1, 9}
ā brahman brāhmaṇo brahmavarcasī jāyatāmiti brāhmaṇa eva brahmavarcasaṃ dadhāti tasmātpurā brāhmaṇo brahmavarcasī jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 1]
ā rāṣṭre rājanyaḥ śūra iṣavyo'tivyādhī mahāratho jāyatāmiti rājanya eva śauryam mahimānaṃ dadhāti tasmāt purā rājanyaḥ śūra iṣavyo'tivyādhī mahāratho jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 2]
dogdhrī dhenuriti dhenvāmeva payo dadhāti tasmātpurā dhenurdogdhrī jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 3]
voḍhānaḍvāniti anaḍuhyeva balaṃ dadhāti tasmātpurānaḍvānvoḍhā jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 4]
āśuḥ saptiriti aśva eva javaṃ dadhāti tasmātpurāśvaḥ sartā jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 5]
puraṃdhir yoṣeti yoṣityeva rūpaṃ dadhāti tasmād rūpiṇī yuvatiḥ priyā bhāvukā | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 6]
jiṣṇū ratheṣṭhā iti rājanya eva jaitram mahimānaṃ dadhāti tasmāt purā rājanyo jiṣṇurjajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 7]
sabheyo yuveti eṣa vai sabheyo yuvā yaḥ prathamavayasī tasmāt prathamavayasī strīṇām priyo bhāvukaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 8]
āsya yajamānasya vīro jāyatāmiti yajamānasyaiva prajāyāṃ vīryaṃ dadhāti tasmātpurejānasya vīro jajñe | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 9]
nikāme nikāme naḥ parjanyo varṣatviti | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 10.1]
nikāme nikāme vai tatra parjanyo varṣati yatraitena yajñena yajante phalavatyo na oṣadhayaḥ pacyantāmiti phalavatyo vai tatrauṣadhayaḥ pacyante yatraitena yajñena yajante yogakṣemo naḥ kalpatāmiti yogakṣemo vai tatra kalpate yatraitena yajñena yajante tasmādyatraitena yajñena yajante kﾱptaḥ prajānāṃ yogakṣemo bhavati | [ŚBM, 13, 1, 9 10.2]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 1}
prajāpatirdevebhyo yajñān vyādiśat sa ātmannaśvamedhamadhatta te devāḥ prajāpatimabruvanneṣa vai yajño yad aśvamedho 'pi no'trāstu bhaga iti tebhya etānannahomānkalpayad yad annahomānjuhoti devāneva tatprīṇāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 1]
ājyena juhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ tejasaivāsmiṃstattejo dadhāty ājyena juhoty etadvai devānām priyaṃ dhāma yadājyam priyeṇaivainān dhāmnā samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 2]
saktubhirjuhoti devānāṃ vā etadrūpaṃ yatsaktavo devāneva tatprīṇāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 3]
dhānābhirjuhoti ahorātrāṇāṃ vā etadrūpaṃ yaddhānā ahorātrāṇyeva tatprīṇāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 4]
lājairjuhoti nakṣatrāṇāṃ vā etadrūpaṃ yallājā nakṣatrāṇyeva tatprīṇāti prāṇāya svāhāpānāya svāheti nāmagrāhaṃ juhoti nāmagrāhamevaināṃstatprīṇāty ekasmai svāhā dvābhyāṃ svāhā śatāya svāhaikaśatāya svāhety anupūrvaṃ juhoty anupūrvamevaināṃstatprīṇāty ekottarā juhoty ekavṛdvai svargo loka ekadhaivainaṃ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayati parācīr juhoti parāṅiva vai svargo lokaḥ svargasya lokasyābhijityai | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 5]
īśvaro vā eṣaḥ parāṅ pradaghor yaḥ parācīrāhutīrjuhoti naikaśatamatyeti yad ekaśatam atīyād āyuṣā yajamānaṃ vyardhayed ekaśataṃ juhoti śatāyurvai puruṣa ātmaikaśata āyuṣyevātmanpratitiṣṭhati vyuṣṭyai svāhā svargāya svāhetyuttame āhutī juhoti rātrirvai vyuṣṭirahaḥ svargo 'horātre eva tatprīṇāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 6]
tadāhuḥ yadubhe divā vā naktaṃ vā juhuyādahorātre mohayed vyuṣṭyai svāhety anudita āditye juhoti svargāya svāhety udite 'horātrayoravyatimohāya | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 1 7]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 2}
rājā vā eṣa yajñānāṃ yadaśvamedhaḥ yajamāno vā aśvamedho yajamāno yajño yadaśve paśūnniyunakti yajña eva tadyajñamārabhate | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 1]
aśvaṃ tūparaṃ gomṛgamiti tānmadhyame yūpa ālabhate senāmukhamevāsyaitena saṃśyati tasmādrājñaḥ senāmukham bhīṣmam bhāvukam | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 2]
kṛṣṇagrīvamāgneyaṃ rarāṭe purastāt pūrvāgnimeva taṃ kurute tasmādrājñaḥ pūrvāgnirbhāvukaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 3]
sārasvatīm meṣīmadhastāddhanvoḥ strīreva tadanugāḥ kurute tasmātstriyaḥ puṃso'nuvartmāno bhāvukāḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 4]
āśvināvadhorāmau bāhvoḥ bāhvoreva balaṃ dhatte tasmādrājā bāhubalī bhāvukaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 5]
saumāpauṣṇaṃ śyāmaṃ nābhyām pratiṣṭhāmeva tāṃ kuruta iyaṃ vai pūṣāsyāmeva pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 6]
sauryayāmau śvetaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ kavace eva te kurute tasmādrājā saṃnaddho vīryaṃ karoti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 7]
tvāṣṭrau lomaśasakthau sakthyoḥ ūrvoreva balaṃ dhatte tasmādrājorubalī bhāvukaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 8]
vāyavyaṃ śvetam pucche utsedhameva taṃ kurute tasmādutsedham prajā bhaye'bhisaṃśrayantīndrāya svapasyāya vehatam yajñasya sendratāyai vaiṣṇavo vāmano yajño vai viṣṇur yajña evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 9]
te vā ete pañcadaśa paryaṅgyāḥ paśavo bhavanti pañcadaśo vai vajro vīryaṃ vajro vajreṇaivaitadvīryeṇa yajamānaḥ purastātpāpmānamapahate | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 10]
pañcadaśapañcadaśo evetareṣu pañcadaśo vai vajro vīryaṃ vajro vajreṇaivaitadvīryeṇa yajamāno'bhitaḥ pāpmānamapahate | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 11]
tadāhuḥ apāhaivaitaiḥ pāpmānaṃ hatā ity akṛtsnaṃ ca tvai prajāpatiṃ saṃskaroti na cedaṃ sarvamavarunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 12]
saptadaśaiva paśūnmadhyame yūpa ālabheta saptadaśo vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpatiraśvamedho'śvamedhasyaivāptyai ṣoḍaśaṣoḍaśetareṣu ṣoḍaśakalaṃ vā idaṃ sarvaṃ tadidaṃ sarvamavarunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 13]
tānkathamāprīṇīyādityāhuḥ samiddho añjankṛdaram matīnāmiti bārhadukthībhir āprīṇīyād bṛhaduktho ha vai vāmadevyo'śvo vā sāmudriraśvasyāprīrdadarśa tā etās tābhirevainametadāprīṇīma iti vadanto na tathā kuryājjāmadagnībhirevāprīṇīyāt prajāpatirvai jamadagniḥ so'śvamedhaḥ svayaivainaṃ devatayā samardhayati tasmājjāmadagnībhir evāprīṇīyāt | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 14]
taddhaike eteṣām paryaṅgyāṇāṃ nānā yājyāpuronuvākyāḥ kurvanti vindāma eteṣāmavittyetareṣāṃ na kurma iti na tathā kuryāt kṣatraṃ vā aśvo viḍitare paśavaḥ pratipratinīṃ ha te pratyudyāminīṃ kṣatrāya viśaṃ kurvanty atho āyuṣā yajamānaṃ vyardhayanti ye tathā kurvanti tasmātprājāpatya evāśvo devadevatyā itare kṣatrāyaiva tadviśaṃ kṛtānukarāmanuvartmānaṃ karoty atho āyuṣaiva yajamānaṃ samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 15]
hiraṇmayo'śvasya śāso bhavati lohamayāḥ paryaṅgyāṇāmāyasā itareṣāṃ jyotirvai hiraṇyaṃ rāṣṭramaśvamedho jyotireva tadrāṣṭre dadhāty atho hiraṇyajyotiṣaiva yajamānaḥ svargaṃ lokamety atho anūkāśameva taṃ kurute svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 16]
atho kṣatraṃ vā aśvaḥ kṣatrasyaitadrūpaṃ yaddhiraṇyaṃ kṣatrameva tatkṣatreṇa samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 17]
atha yallohamayāḥ paryaṅgyāṇām yathā vai rājño rājāno rājakṛtaḥ sūtagrāmaṇya evaṃ vā ete'śvasya yat paryaṅgyā evamu vā etaddhiraṇyasya yallohaṃ svenaivaināṃstadrūpeṇa samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 18]
atha yadāyasā itareṣām viḍvā itare paśavo viśa etadrūpaṃ yadayo viśameva tadviśā samardhayati vaitasa iṭasūna uttarato'śvasyāvadyanty ānuṣṭubho vā aśva ānuṣṭubhaiṣā dik svāyāmevainaṃ taddiśi dadhāty atha yadvaitasa iṭasūne 'psuyonirvā aśvo 'psujā vetasaḥ svayaivainaṃ yonyā samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 2 19]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 3}
devā vā aśvamedhe pavamānaṃ svargaṃ lokaṃ na prājānaṃs tamaśvaḥ prājānād yadaśvamedhe'śvena pavamānāya sarpanti svargasya lokasya prajñātyai pucchamanvārabhante svargasyaiva lokasya samaṣṭyai na vai manuṣyaḥ svargaṃ lokam añjasā vedāśvo vai svargaṃ lokamañjasā veda | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 3 1]
yad udgātodgāyet | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 3 2.1]
yathākṣetrajño 'nyena pathā nayettādṛktad atha yadudgātāramavarudhyāśvamudgīthāya vṛṇīte yathā kṣetrajño'ñjasā nayedevamevaitad yajamānamaśvaḥ svargaṃ lokamañjasā nayati hiṃkaroti sāmaiva taddhiṃkaroty udgītha eva sa vaḍavā uparundhanti saṃśiñjate yathopagātāra upagāyanti tādṛktaddhiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇā suvarṇaṃ śatamānaṃ tasyoktaṃ brāhmaṇam | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 3 2.2]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 4}
prajāpatiḥ akāmayata ubhau lokau abhijayeyam deva lokam ca manuṣya lokam ca iti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_1]
saḥ etān paśūn apaśyat grāmyān ca āraṇyān ca | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_2]
tān ālabhata | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_3]
taiḥ imau lokau avārunddha | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_4]
grāmyaiḥ eva paśubhiḥ imam lokam avārunddha āraṇyaiḥ amum | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_5]
ayam vai lokaḥ manuṣya lokaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_6]
atha asau deva lokaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_7]
yat grāmyān paśūn ālabhate imam eva taiḥ lokam yajamānaḥ avarunddhe yat āraṇyān amum taiḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497762_8]
sa yat grāmyaiḥ saṃsthāpayet sam adhvānaḥ krāmeyuḥ samantikam grāmayoḥ grāma antau syātām | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497763_1]
na ṛkṣīkāḥ puruṣavyāghrāḥ parimoṣiṇaḥ āvyādhinyaḥ taskarāḥ araṇyeṣu ājāyeran | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497763_2]
yat āraṇyaiḥ vi adhvānaḥ krāmeyuḥ vidūram grāmayoḥ grāma antau syātām | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497763_3]
ṛkṣīkāḥ puruṣavyāghrāḥ parimoṣiṇaḥ āvyādhinyaḥ taskarāḥ araṇyeṣu ājāyeran | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497763_4]
tat āhuḥ apaśuḥ vai eṣa yat āraṇyaḥ na etasya hotavyam yat juhuyāt kṣipram yajamānam araṇyam mṛtam hareyuḥ araṇya bhāgāḥ hi āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ yat na juhuyāt yajñaveśasam syāt iti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497764_1]
paryagnikṛtān eva utsṛjanti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497764_2]
tat na eva hutam na ahutam | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497764_3]
na yajamānam araṇyam mṛtam haranti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497764_4]
na yajñaveśasam bhavati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497764_5]
grāmyaiḥ saṃsthāpayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497765_1]
vi pitāputrau avasyataḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497765_2]
sam adhvānaḥ krāmanti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497765_3]
samantikam grāmayoḥ grāma antau bhavataḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497765_4]
na ṛkṣīkāḥ puruṣavyāghrāḥ parimoṣiṇaḥ āvyādhinyaḥ taskarāḥ araṇyeṣu ājāyante | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 4 497765_5]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 5}
prajāpatiraśvamedhamasṛjata so'smātsṛṣṭaḥ parāṅait sa paṅktirbhūtvā saṃvatsaram prāviśat te'rdhamāsā abhavaṃs tam pañcadaśibhiranuprāyuṅkta tamāpnot tamāptvā pañcadaśibhiravārunddhārdhamāsānāṃ vā eṣā pratimā yat pañcadaśino yatpañcadaśina ālabhate'rdhamāsāneva tairyajamāno 'varunddhe | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 5 1]
tadāhuḥ anavaruddho vā etasya saṃvatsaro bhavati yo'nyatra cāturmāsyebhyaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tanuta ity eṣa vai sākṣāt saṃvatsaro yaccāturmāsyāni yaccāturmāsyānpaśūnālabhate sākṣādeva tatsaṃvatsaramavarunddhe vi vā eṣa prajayā paśubhir ṛdhyate 'pa svargaṃ lokaṃ rādhnoti yo'nyatraikādaśinebhyaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tanuta ity eṣa vai saṃprati svargo loko yad ekādaśinī prajā vai paśava ekādaśinī yad aikādaśinān paśūn ālabhate na svargaṃ lokam aparādhnoti na prajayā paśubhir vyṛdhyate | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 5 2]
prajāpatirvirājamasṛjata sāsmātsṛṣṭā parācyait sāśvam medhyam prāviśat tāṃ daśibhiranuprāyuṅkta tām āpnot tāmāptvā daśibhiravārunddha yaddaśina ālabhate virājameva tairyajamāno'varunddhe śatamālabhate śatāyurvai puruṣaḥ śatendriya āyurevendriyaṃ vīryamātmandhatte | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 5 3]
ekādaśa daśata ālabhate ekādaśākṣarā vai triṣṭub indriyamu vai vīryaṃ triṣṭub indriyasyaiva vīryasyāvaruddhyā ekādaśa daśata ālabhate daśa vai paśoḥ prāṇā ātmaikādaśaḥ prāṇaireva paśūntsamardhayati vaiśvadevā bhavanti vaiśvadevo vā aśvo'śvasyaiva sarvatvāya bahurūpā bhavanti tasmādbahurūpāḥ paśavo nānārūpā bhavanti tasmānnānārūpāḥ paśavaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 5 4]
{ŚBM, 13, 2, 6}
yuñjanti bradhnamaruṣaṃ carantamiti asau vā ādityo bradhno'ruṣo 'mumevāsmā ādityaṃ yunakti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 1]
tadāhuḥ parāṅvā etasmādyajña eti yasya paśurupākṛto'nyatra vederetīty etaṃ stotaranena pathā punaraśvamāvartayāsi na iti vāyurvai stotā tamevāsmā etatparastāddadhāti tathā nātyeti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 2]
apa vā etasmāt teja indriyam paśavaḥ śrīḥ krāmanti yo'śvamedhena yajate | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 3]
vasavastvāñjantu gāyatreṇa chandaseti mahiṣyabhyanakti tejo vā ājyaṃ tejo gāyatrī tejasī evāsmintsamīcī dadhāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 4]
rudrāstvāñjantu traiṣṭubhena chandaseti vāvātā tejo vā ājyam indriyaṃ triṣṭup tejaścaivāsminnindriyaṃ ca samīcī dadhāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 5]
ādityāstvāñjantu jāgatena chandaseti parivṛktā tejo vā ājyam paśavo jagatī tejaścaivāsminpaśūṃśca samīcī dadhāti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 6]
patnyo'bhyañjanti śriyai vā etadrūpaṃ yatpatnyaḥ śriyamevāsmiṃstaddadhati nāsmātteja indriyam paśavaḥ śrīrapakrāmanti | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 7]
yathā vai haviṣo'hutasya skandet evametat paśo skandati yasya niktasya lomāni śīyante yatkācānāvayanti lomānyevāsya saṃbharanti hiraṇmayā bhavanti tasyoktaṃ brāhmaṇam ekaśatam ekaśataṃ kācānāvayanti śatāyurvai puruṣa ātmaikaśata āyuṣyevātmanpratitiṣṭhati bhūrbhuvaḥ svariti prājāpatyābhirāvayanti prājāpatyo'śvaḥ svayaivainaṃ devatayā samardhayanti lājīñchācīnyavye gavya ity atiriktam annam aśvāyopāvaharanti prajām ivānnādīṃ kuruta etad annam atta devā etad annam addhi prajāpata iti prajām evānnādyena samardhayati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 8]
apa vā etasmāt tejo brahmavarcasaṃ krāmati yo'śvamedhena yajate hotā ca brahmā ca brahmodyaṃ vadata āgneyo vai hotā bārhaspatyo brahmā brahma bṛhaspatis tejaścaivāsminbrahmavarcasaṃ ca samīcī dhatto yūpamabhito vadato yajamāno vai yūpo yajamānamevaitattejasā ca brahmavarcasena cobhayataḥ paridhattaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 9]
kaḥ svidekākī caratīti asau vā āditya ekākī caraty eṣa brahmavarcasam brahmavarcasamevāsmiṃstaddhattaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 10]
ka u svijjāyate punariti candramā vai jāyate punarāyurevāsmiṃstaddhattaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 11]
kiṃ sviddhimasya bheṣajamiti agnirvai himasya bheṣajaṃ teja evāsmiṃstaddhattaḥ | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 12]
kimvāvapanam mahaditi ayaṃ vai loka āvapanam mahadasminneva loke pratitiṣṭhati | [ŚBM, 13, 2, 6 13]
